# CLAUDE.md — BLOOM project agent context

This file is the contract between the project and any AI agent working on it. Read it at the start of every session. Update it whenever the project changes — see [Living docs rule](#living-docs-rule) at the bottom.

The human-facing description lives in [README.md](README.md). This file focuses on what an AI needs to continue work without re-reading the entire codebase.

---

## 🗺️ Retention Stages Tracker (May 2026, updated 2026-05-23)

Quick-scan map of the addiction-loop work. **Update this table whenever a stage ships.** Detailed change-log entries live in §11 below.

> 🔍 **AUDIT 2026-05-31 — full addiction audit** (132-agent scan, 110 bugs checked / 63 confirmed + live-server browser evidence). Two deliverables: [BLOOM_ADDICTION_AUDIT.md](BLOOM_ADDICTION_AUDIT.md) (per-category scores, overall **6.5/10**, 63-bug table, "what's missing" diagnosis) + [tasks/ACTIVE/ADDICTION_TASKS.md](tasks/ACTIVE/ADDICTION_TASKS.md) (45 addiction-ranked tasks + 8 fix-first bugs). **Headline finding: the world looks EMPTY** (`activeNow:0`, bots not default-on, Daily Special points to an empty board, push effectively dead) — fixing aliveness + focus is the #1 ROI.

Server: an in-memory `bannedDevices` Set (loaded at boot, refreshed every 60s, mutated instantly on ban/unban) so `requireDeviceAuth` rejects a banned device with 403 `banned` at **zero per-request DB cost** ([server.js](server.js)); new action-switched `POST /<ADMIN>/api/players/moderate` (ban/unban/grant_trophies/grant_xp/set_level — grant_trophies upserts `player_trophies`); `GET /<ADMIN>/api/player/:id` now also returns the profile + moderation state. | **AD.9** | **Economy faucet-vs-sink dashboard** (ranked task #16). No per-source ledger exists, so the dashboard is the aggregate gem picture. New `GET /<ADMIN>/api/economy` ([server.js](server.js)) returns total faucet (SUM `total_earned`) vs sink (SUM `total_spent`) vs float (wallets + `gem_bank`), a **sink-ratio health metric**, active-player (7d) economy, and top-20 earners/spenders/hoarders. Admin UI ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): a "📊 ברז מול בור" panel in the 💰 כלכלה tab — 4 KPI cards (green-amber-red sink-ratio, healthy ≈40-70%) + active-7d line + 3 top-20 tables. Lets the owner tune the gem economy for spend-pressure (low sink-ratio = hoarding = weaker gem-chase loop). Server-only + static HTML; node --check clean; deploy healthy. Commits e09338e (endpoint) + de4f9a2 (admin UI — earlier UI commits silently no-matched). |
| **IS.1** | **Player-issues sweep — 5 server/client bugs behind 206 reports** (user: "the 🚨 תקלות tab has lots of user issues, fix everything + organize the DB"). Pulled all 206 open issues, reproduced each live, fixed the root cause: **(1)** `/api/player/earn` HTTP 500 (11 devices) — `validatedMeta` was `let`-declared **inside** the dedup `else` block but read by the `score_milestone`/`dyn_quest`/`dyn_ach`/`dyn_streak_milestone` payment branches in the outer scope → `ReferenceError` → 500. **Every quest/achievement/streak/score-milestone reward was silently failing to pay.** Moved the decl to handler scope ([server.js](server.js)). **(2)** `/api/promo/{impression,click}` 500 — `promo_*.slot` is NOT NULL with no default but the INSERT omitted it → NOT-NULL violation. Pass `slot` (body, default `home_tile`) + DB-level DEFAULT ([schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js)). **(3)** `mountPetWidget` `insertBefore` crash (5 devices/102 logs) — `insertBefore` needs the anchor to be a child of `homeEl`, but the bottom-nav relocates checklist/lives tiles to other tab panels → "object can not be found here" (Safari). Guard + fall back to `appendChild` ([src/22-pet.js](src/22-pet.js)). **(4)** duel-result CTA `Can't find variable: init` (3 devices) — inline `onclick` string calling the IIFE-scoped `init()` from global scope; rewired via `addEventListener` ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)). **(5)** admin player search 500 on any `q` — the COUNT query reused the main `WHERE` (uses `$3`) but was bound only `$1` → "no parameter $3"; added a `$1`-based `whereTotal` ([server.js](server.js)). **DB organized:** all 206 issues resolved with a fix note; 9 real affected players compensated 100💎 each (the earn bug cost them gems) via the built-in compensation flow → tab now 0 open / 0 urgent. All 5 endpoints re-probed live = 200 (were 500). Cache v20260602a, SW bloom-v22.4. |
| **AD.A1** | **Admin debug-tab sweep** (user: "the 🐛 debug tab has problems"). Ran the live 🐛 scanner (via Playwright) + curl'd all 17 admin endpoints. Findings + fixes ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): **(1)** dead button — `btn-bots-fill` (the AD.2 "🌍 מלא את העולם" fleet kicker) shipped its HTML but never got a click handler, so it did nothing; added the handler (`POST /api/bots/fill-world`, mirrors start/stop + refreshes the bot list). **(2)** scanner robustness — `checkEndpointHealth`/`checkHiddenConfigKeys`/`getAdminScriptText` now fetch via `location.origin + path` instead of a relative URL, so a credentialed `location.href` can't make fetch throw "URL that includes credentials" and false-report every endpoint as a NETWORK fail. **(3)** the now-working `hiddenKeys` check surfaced 18 `game_config` keys with no tooltip (bot duels, live-stats blending, device sync, friend search/requests, issues system) — added `TIPS_PER_KEY` + `PRESETS_PER_KEY` entries for all 18 with accurate defaults. **Live-verified: scanner now reports 0 issues across all 6 checks** (was: 1 dead button + 18 hidden keys). Admin is static (no build/cache-buster); server.js untouched. |
| **IS.2** | **Two production 500s from the live console** (user screenshot of the pet modal + `pet`/`request-send` 500s). Reproduced both live with registered devices, root-caused via Railway logs. **(1)** `POST /api/pet/pet` (the "ליטוף יומי" daily-pet button) was **100% broken for everyone** — it did `INSERT INTO player_profiles (device_id) VALUES ($1) ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`, but `player_code` is `UNIQUE NOT NULL` with no default, and the NOT-NULL check fires **before** ON CONFLICT resolution, so the insert threw even when the row already existed (`null value in column "player_code" ... violates not-null constraint`). New collision-safe `ensurePlayerProfile(deviceId)` helper (generates a `player_code`, targets the `device_id` PK, retries on the rare code collision via `23505` catch) called **before** the transaction; the broken in-transaction insert removed ([server.js](server.js)). **(2)** `POST /api/friends/request-send` (FD.2) 500'd as soon as it reached a real target — `ON CONFLICT ON CONSTRAINT uq_friend_requests_pending` referenced a **partial UNIQUE INDEX**, which is not a named constraint, so Postgres threw. Switched to `ON CONFLICT (from_device, to_device) WHERE status = 'pending'` to match the partial index by its predicate. **Live-verified:** pet/pet → `{ok,reward:20}` (repeat → `already_petted_today`); request-send → `{ok,requestId}` (repeat → `alreadyPending`; reverse → auto-accepted friendship +200💎). Server-only — no client build. Commit ec26be4. |
| **IS.3** | **Skin Gacha — unopened-box reveal + free-pull double-tap** (user screenshot of the gacha modal + "free pull error not understood" + "when a box comes out you can't see what you won"). **(1)** `chest`/`freeze` rewards (🎁 תיבת הפתעה / 🛡 הקפאת רצף) and `bp_tier` are credited as gems / BP-tiers server-side (`_gachaGrantReward` returns `convertedToGems`/`xpBoost`), but the reveal card ([src/19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js) `renderCard`) only showed the item emoji + name with no value — so a player who won "3 תיבות הפתעה" (= +150💎, confirmed live) saw a static box that "didn't open." `renderCard` now surfaces the concrete payout on **every** card via a new value badge: `convertedToGems` → gold-pink "🎉 נפתח! קיבלת +N💎" pop, duplicate skin → "הומר ל-N💎", new skin → "🎨 סקין חדש נפתח!", `bp_tier` (xpBoost>0) → "+N דרגות". Plain `gems` cards stay badge-free (the name is the value). CSS `.gacha-card-value*` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) with a `gachaValuePop` overshoot + reduced-motion guard. **(2)** The free daily pull could be double-triggered and the resulting `free_already_claimed` read as a confusing error. New `_gachaPulling` in-flight guard (one pull at a time); the already-claimed path now self-corrects `_gachaCache.data.freeAvailable=false` (button repaints to "מחר") and shows a clear friendly toast, not an error. Verified: live chest pull returns `convertedToGems:150`; 6/6 deterministic render cases pass. Cache `v20260602o`, SW `bloom-v23.8`. Engine self-test clean. Commit 9c435f1. **(3) gacha_pool bloat** — the seed at [schema.sql](schema.sql) used `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`, but the table's only constraint is its SERIAL `id`, so the conflict target never matched and all 17 rows re-inserted on **every boot** — the live pool had ballooned to **5593 rows** (17 × 329 boots). Rates were unaffected (every entry duplicated equally) but it's pure bloat. Fix: a self-healing dedup `DELETE ... USING` (keeps the lowest id per distinct entry, idempotent) + the seed now wrapped in `DO $$ IF NOT EXISTS(...) $$` so it only runs on an empty pool — can never re-duplicate again. Verified against the live DB in a rolled-back transaction (5593 → 17, all 17 distinct entries preserved), then deployed: live pool now **17**, free pull works. `gacha_featured_id` is null in prod so no orphaned featured pointer. Server/boot change — no client build. Commit 738353c. |
| **IS.4** | **Feature banners no longer deletable with ✕** (user: "there are features you can click an X on and delete from their place — fix this" + "I press X to exit a feature and can't get back to play, in tabs other than the bank"). Live browser investigation (Playwright, level-20 unlock via `bloom_games_played`): every feature **modal** close works correctly (tested 15+ — Bank, Trophy, Spin, Login-Cal, Pet, Gacha, Album, Lifetime, League, Rival, Guild-War, Calendar, ach-LB). The real culprit was the feature **banners** — Starter Pack ([src/17-starter-pack.js](src/17-starter-pack.js)), Daily Deal ([src/18-daily-deals.js](src/18-daily-deals.js)), Gacha ([src/19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js)), Bundle ([src/23-bundles.js](src/23-bundles.js)) — each had a `<button class="*-banner-close">×</button>` whose click ran `banner.remove()`, **deleting the feature from its tab**. The player read that as "the X is broken / I can't get back to play"; the Bank was the exception ("חוץ מהבנק") because it's a tile→modal with a real close. **Fix:** removed the dismiss ✕ button + its handler branch from all four banners — they're feature/monetization surfaces, not deletable notifications, and already auto-hide on their natural conditions (purchase / daily rotation / expiry window). The "פתח →" CTA + the resulting modal's working ✕ are unchanged. **Live-verified after deploy:** 0 deletable ✕ on banners, all banners still present, "פתח →" → gacha modal → ✕ closes fine. Cache `v20260602p`, SW `bloom-v23.9`. Engine self-test clean. Commit 9691161. |
| **IS.5** | **Daily-deal "×N ערך!" badge covered the close ✕** (user screenshot: "some windows have an ✕ top-left but also a deal badge there, so you can't click the ✕"). The daily-deal modal's value-multiplier sticker (`.dd-modal-multiplier`, shown when a deal is ≥3× value) sat at `top:10/left:10` with `z-index:2` — directly over the close ✕ (`.dd-modal-close`, top-left, no z-index) — intercepting the click. Confirmed live: the badge overlapped the ✕ and the ✕'s default button padding made it render 44px tall (so even a stacked-below position clipped). **Fix** ([public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)+[public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)): moved the badge to `top:46/right:12` (top-right, below the −75% ribbon) so the entire top-left corner is reserved for the ✕, and gave `.dd-modal-close` `z-index:5` as a safety net. Audited all sibling deal modals (starter-pack, bundle, gacha) — their ribbons are already top-right, clear of the left ✕, so only daily-deal was affected. **Live-verified:** badge no longer overlaps close or ribbon; close is the top element at its center; clicking it closes the modal. Cache `v20260602r`, SW `bloom-v24.1`. Commits 4f89eed + b7ae7c4. |
| **FN.1** | **Real-time friend pop-ups + actionable online-friends banner** (user: the "N friends online" banner doesn't show WHO is online or let you act; and there's no in-app pop-up when a friend request is sent/accepted). Three coordinated client-only changes (all endpoints + VAPID already exist). **(1)** NEW [src/51-friend-notify.js](src/51-friend-notify.js) — polls `/api/friends/requests` every 45s (+ on visibility regain + 4s after boot), pops ONE actionable slide-in banner at a time, deduped across sessions via `bloom_seen_friend_reqs_v1`: **incoming** → "👋 X רוצה להוסיף אותך · ✓ אשר / דחה" → accept hits `/api/friends/request-respond` → 🤝 "+200💎 לשניכם" celebration (confetti + sound) + offers ⚔️ אתגר; **my-request-accepted** → 🎉 "X אישר/ה! +200💎 לשניכם · ⚔️ אתגר עכשיו". | **AD.4.1** | **Danger-meter clipping fix** (live-race bug report). The AD.4 `🚨` pill was appended INSIDE `#grid-wrap` (`overflow-y:auto`/`overflow-x:hidden`) at `top:-14px` — the part above the wrap's top edge got clipped by the overflow, so it rendered as a thin red sliver half-hidden behind the tier-bar. Surfaced in a 60s live race (grid fills to ~1 empty cell → meter fires). Fix ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `paintDangerMeter`): mount into grid-wrap's parent (`.app`, `position:relative`, no clip in this band, last child → highest paint order) and anchor via `wrap.offsetTop - 14` so it also tracks the live-race `padding-top` shift. CSS `.danger-meter` `top` becomes a neutral fallback (JS sets it inline). Verified live v20260531i. |
| **UX.1–12** | **Full UX+addiction page audit + 12 fix rounds (2026-06-02)** 🎨 | A 21-agent parallel audit scored every screen on 7 dimensions (addiction 30% · visual 18% · comfort 12% · clarity 12% · focus 12% · closability 8% · relevance 8%). Game avg **67/100 (B-)**, 141 findings (0 critical / 34 high / 65 med / 42 low); full report + ranked remediation tasks in [tasks/ACTIVE/PAGE_UX_AUDIT_TASKS.md](tasks/ACTIVE/PAGE_UX_AUDIT_TASKS.md). Reframes bonuses as a REWARD for playing, not a timer to camp. (The single forced first-event at +3s is kept as an onboarding dopamine beat — once per game, not the exploited recurring loop.) **C — Flow/combo meter** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): every drop within `flow_window_ms` (2500ms) of the last builds `flowLevel`; a fixed top-center gold pill "🔥 זרימה ×N" (`#flow-pill`, pink-red `.flow-hot` at ≥1.6) shows the live multiplier `min(flow_max_mult 2.0, 1 + level·flow_mult_per_level 0.15)` applied to merge scoring (`pointsFor × eventMult × flowMultiplier()`). A slow/stalled drop (gap > window) resets `flowLevel=0` — stalling COSTS the player their multiplier. Positive-framed: speed pays, camping doesn't. **B — Idle pressure** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): a 1s idle watcher (armed by `startEventSystem` before the events-enabled gate, guarded by `isGameSurfaceVisible()`) passively decays the flow pill once idle exceeds the window, shows a "⏰ שחק! הבונוסים מגיעים רק כשמשחקים" banner at `idle_warn_seconds` (10), then runs `idle_action` at `idle_action_seconds` (18): `warn` (default, banner only) / `autodrop` (drops into the safest column) / `expire` (clears the pending event). **Admin controls everything:** 10 new `game_config` keys ([schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js)) — `events_activity_gate_enabled`/`events_min_drops_since_last`, `flow_meter_enabled`/`flow_window_ms`/`flow_mult_per_level`/`flow_max_mult`, `idle_pressure_enabled`/`idle_warn_seconds`/`idle_action_seconds`/`idle_action` — all with TIPS + PRESETS in a dedicated new admin section "⏱ אנטי-סטיכה + זרימה" ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)). | **TA.1** | **Game-Over Persistence** 💾 | Audit round 2: a refresh after a great practice/dynamic/contest game dropped the player onto a fresh empty grid — losing the score banner, share opportunity, and ad-watch reward. Only `daily` mode had refresh-persistence (via `DAILY_PLAYED_PREFIX`). New `LAST_GAME_KEY` snapshot (30-min TTL) writes `mode/score/highestTier/isNewBest/gameId/boardId/contestCode/ts` at game-over time. Boot reads the snapshot, overrides savedMode to practice/dynamic/contest, lazy-fetches the dynamic board from `/api/boards/available` so the New-Game button has the full definition. `init()` restore branch gates on `!fresh + lastGameModeRestorable(mode) + matching boardId/contestCode`, renders the over-screen with `restored: true`. New green "💾 המשחק שלך נשמר" banner + explicit "🎮 משחק חדש" CTA. `continue-ad` button hard-blocked in restored state (empty grid + saved score would be a free-game exploit). `fresh:true` is now passed by the home Play button + the "again" button so a fresh-start request can't get trapped by the restore branch. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,947 drops / 8,875 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260525b`, SW `bloom-v13.4`. |
| **TB.1+TB.2** | **Display Size Reclaim** 📐 | Audit B1+B2: the in-flow booster strip + col-mult-bar were eating ~80-100px of vertical space between tier-bar and grid-wrap, shrinking cell size by ~20% on average phones. TB.1 — `maybeMountBoosterStrip()` ([src/35-boosters.js](src/35-boosters.js)) now appends to `document.body` with class `booster-strip-bottom` (`position:fixed`, `bottom: calc(8px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom))`, `transform:translateX(-50%)`, `backdrop-filter:blur(10px)`, `z-index:var(--z-floating)`). Slide-up entrance animation, smaller emoji/label/price sizes for the compact tool-tray look. Bail guard on `window.__bloomGameOver` + explicit teardown in both game-over branches + in `showHome`/`showHomeV2` (since position:fixed survives .app hides). TB.2 — `.col-mult-bar` margin 2/6 → 1/2, `.col-mult-pill` height 22 → 18 + font 13 → 11 ([public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)). Bar drops from ~30px to ~21px without losing legibility. Net: ~73px (TB.1) + ~7-10px (TB.2) returned to the playable grid → ~15-20% larger cell size on typical 750px-tall phones. Zero engine changes. Engine self-test: 200 games / 14,007 drops / 8,840 merges / 0 floating tiles. Cache buster `v20260525c`, SW `bloom-v13.5`. |
| **TA.2** | **Continue-Ad Server Dedup** 🛡 | Audit A2: a player who refreshed the over screen could re-claim the "watch ad for 2 free rows" continue indefinitely — the client-only `usedContinue` flag reset on every `init()`. With TA.1 game-over persistence shipping, defense-in-depth is needed. New `POST /api/player/continue-ad` ([server.js](server.js)) mirrors `/ad-watch`'s three-gate pattern: per-game dedup (`_cont:<device>:<gameId>`), daily cap (`_cont_count:<device>:<date>` vs `continue_daily_cap=3`), cooldown (`_cont_rate:<device>` vs `continue_cooldown_seconds=30`). Endpoint doesn't credit gems — it returns `ok:true` as a green light for the client to run the ad + clear rows. [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `continue-ad` button calls the server FIRST; failure reasons (`already_continued`/`daily_cap`/`rate_limited`) render distinct copy on the button. `gameId` persists through refresh via sessionStorage (TA.1 keeps the prior game's id so both ad-watch and continue dedup survive reloads). Net: 100 refreshes = 100×0 continues, was 100×continue. Cache buster `v20260525d`, SW `bloom-v13.6`. |

Followed by `soundMilestone(4)` twinkle 240ms later. **Buzz**: relief pattern `[40,80,40,80,80]` (slower than chain celebration — reads as "exhale" not "punch"). **Confetti**: 14 particles (smaller than chain 5+ — the moment is relief, not glory). `lastClutchSaveAt` reset on `init()` so the first save in a new game isn't blocked by a cooldown from the previous game. | **FD.2** | **Social + Identity Overhaul (May 29 2026)** 🤝 | Four retention-critical fixes in one wave. **(1) Referral-leak fix** — the home invite buttons ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) `whatsappInviteV2()` + the v1 home invite at [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js)) were using `window.location.origin + pathname` for the WhatsApp invite text — bare URL, no `?ref=BLOOM-XXXX`. The universal `buildShareUrl('/')` helper exists exactly for this. Without the ref, every invite sent from home was a K-factor leak — recipients joined but the `/api/referral` attribution never fired, no signup bonus, no push-back-to-referrer. Both buttons now funnel through `window.__bloomBuildShareUrl`. **(2) Bottom-nav iOS Safari stability** ([public/css/bottom-nav.css](public/css/bottom-nav.css)) — players reported the bar "scrolls with content and disappears". Root cause: iOS Safari interacted badly with `backdrop-filter:blur` + the dynamic-viewport resolution of `bottom:0; padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`. Fix: anchor via `bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px)` directly (no extra padding), then force a dedicated compositor layer with `transform: translate3d(0,0,0); will-change: transform; backface-visibility: hidden;`. Standard iOS Safari fixed-position hardening — bar now stays glued to viewport on every scroll. **(3) Friend Search + Requests** — full Clash-Royale-style social system on top of the existing instant-friendship `/api/friends/invite`. New schema: `friend_requests` table (PK id, from_device, to_device, status enum [pending/accepted/declined/canceled], message, timestamps; partial UNIQUE INDEX on `(from, to) WHERE status='pending'` so re-tap is no-op). New endpoints: `GET /api/users/search` (ILIKE on `display_name` + LIKE on `player_code`, returns top-N with per-row `alreadyFriends/requestSent/requestReceived` flags), `POST /api/friends/request-send` (anti-spam caps: 50 pending, 50 total friends; auto-accepts if the other side already requested you), `GET /api/friends/requests` (incoming + outgoing + 14-day history + unread count), `POST /api/friends/request-respond` (accept/decline/cancel with atomic friendship+200💎 bonus transaction). Client ([src/49-friend-search.js](src/49-friend-search.js)) — 2-tab modal (🔍 חיפוש / 📨 בקשות) with red unread-badge on the requests tab. Search has 280ms debounce, returns user cards with role-appropriate action buttons ("➕ הוסף" / "⏳ ממתין" / "🤝 אשר" / "✓ חבר"). Auto-opens to 📨 בקשות tab when URL is `?action=friend-requests` (push deep-link). Entry point: new "🔍 חפש שחקנים + 📨 בקשות חברות" button at the top of the existing dyn-friends modal. **(4) Cross-device Account Sync** — THE BIGGEST mobile-web retention killer fixed. Until now Safari + Chrome on the same phone created two separate identities; every browser switch lost streak/trophies/friends/balance. New schema: `device_transfer_codes` (6-char code PK from 32-char alphabet skipping I/L/O/0/1, source_device_id, 10-min TTL, single-use atomic redeem). New endpoints: `POST /api/account/transfer-create` (requires auth — only the real owner can issue a transfer) + `POST /api/account/transfer-redeem` (the 6-char code IS the auth on the redeem side; returns source device's id+HMAC token). Client ([src/48-device-sync.js](src/48-device-sync.js)) — purple-gold modal with 2 tabs (📤 צור קוד with live MM:SS countdown ticker + 📥 הכנס קוד with destructive-action confirm dialog). On successful redeem, client overwrites `bloom_device_id` + `bloom_device_token` in localStorage, clears identity-bound caches, reloads the page → both browsers are now the same logical player. Entry point: new "🔗 סנכרן" pill on the PID strip ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)), purple gradient distinct from "👤 profile" and "👥 referrals". Anti-abuse: source must be authenticated when creating (5/hr cap); 20/hr per-IP cap on redeem. **Why this works**: industry F2P data — cross-device retention drives D30 by 40-60% on mobile-web titles. Players who can carry their identity across browsers feel committed; those who lose progress feel cheated and uninstall. The social request system adds Clash-Royale's "accept friend = +200💎 toast" emotion → social-debt loop. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,722 drops / 8,640 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529d`, SW `bloom-v20.4`. |

| **BL.1** | **Bot social-proof + auto-fallback for duels (May 29 2026)** 🤖⚔️ | Two coordinated retention levers — "never feel alone" — that close two distinct cold-start gaps. **(1) Live-stats blending** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/stats/live`): bot heartbeats from `player_heartbeat` (filtered to `device_id LIKE 'bot-%'`) are now counted alongside real `contest_live_state` + `device_visits` rows. Capped at `real × bots_live_stats_max_multiplier` (default 2.5) so the ratio stays believable — when 4 real players are active, the bar shows up to 10; when 0 real are active, shows at least `bots_live_stats_floor_when_zero_real` (default 6). `activeNow`, `playingNow`, and `activeThisHour` all get the same blend. Master toggle `bots_in_live_stats_enabled` (default `'true'`). The bar never reads "1 שחקן פעיל" during quiet hours — industry data names this the single biggest D1-retention killer in F2P. **(2) Auto-bot duel fallback** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/duels/find-random` + `/api/duels/find-random-live`): after 8s of no real opponent (live race: 6s), server spawns a phantom bot opponent and returns it as if matchmaking succeeded. Bot looks identical to a real player from the client — random Israeli name from a 70-entry pool, valid `BLOOM-XXXX` code via `generatePlayerCode()`, trophy count in the matchmaking range, full `player_profiles` + `player_trophies` rows seeded for downstream JOIN consistency. New helper `_spawnBotDuelForPlayer({deviceId, myName, myCode, myTrophies, difficulty, range, live, durationSec})` is the single insertion point — atomic INSERT into `duels` with `is_random_match=TRUE, is_bot_match=TRUE, status='accepted'`; adds `is_live=TRUE + started_at + duration_seconds` when called from the live path. **(3) Async bot-score settler**: when player submits via `POST /api/duels/:id/score`, server detects `is_bot_match=TRUE`, stamps `bot_settle_at = NOW() + random(20-55)s` (admin-tunable), returns `result: 'waiting'` so player sees the normal waiting overlay. Two settle paths: (a) periodic ticker every 10s scans for elapsed `bot_settle_at`, (b) lazy-settle inline inside `GET /api/duels/:id` when polling player catches the timer expiry. Either way `_settleBotDuel(duelId)` runs: atomic transaction locks the row, computes `botScore = _calibrateBotScore(playerScore, playerWinPct)`, writes `opponent_score + winner_device + status='settled'/'tie'`, fires push to player. **(4) Score calibration** — `_calibrateBotScore`: 52% chance bot scores LESS than player (admin-tunable `bot_duel_player_win_rate_pct`, default 52 → "player feels slightly favored"). Delta distribution: 65% within 3-13% (most games close → feel real), 25% within 10-25% (clear win/loss), 10% in the 25-40% tail (occasional blowout) + 2% ties. Result: ~52% player wins / ~46% bot wins / ~2% ties — Royal Match / Coin Master industry standard. **(5) Live bot-duel score curve** — live 60s race: bot score computed on-the-fly via `_liveBotScoreAt(duelId, startedAtMs, durationSec, nowMs)`. Deterministic per duel_id (seeded PRNG → `target = 35K-110K`), `score = target × sqrt(elapsed/duration) × noise` — sqrt easing lets bots ramp up quickly then plateau, so a strong player can pass them late (dramatic comebacks). `live-heartbeat` writes computed score to `opponent_live_score` (`GREATEST` guard so it never decreases); `live-state` also overlays computed score for smoother HUD; `_settleLiveDuel` recomputes final bot score so player-abandonment doesn't lock in a stale low number. **(6) Admin telemetry** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html) 👥 שחקנים tab + `/admin/api/bot-duels/stats`): new `⚔️ דו-קרבות מול בוטים` section with 3 stat rows (24h vs all-time vs averages) — player-win % color-coded (green 48-56% = healthy, orange 42-60% = borderline, red = needs tuning), plus a 30-row recent-duels table with result badges (🏆 שחקן / 🤖 בוט / 🤝 תיקו / ⌛ פג / ⏳ פעיל). Auto-refreshes every 15s while tab is open. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 2 new `duels` columns (`is_bot_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE`, `bot_settle_at TIMESTAMPTZ`) + partial index `idx_duels_bot_settle` for cheap settler scans. 9 new `game_config` keys cover every tunable. **Decoupled from bot-engine.js** — those bots actively pump heartbeats for the social-proof stat; these are phantom opponents created on demand. Each bot duel = one row, one short-lived `player_profiles` placeholder, no recurring activity. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,030 drops / 8,935 merges / 0 floating tiles). |

Bot's "live" score is a deterministic-per-duel function of (player's current score, elapsed time, duel id). Stays in the 65-105% range of the player's score, easing toward parity as time progresses (sqrt-curve) + ±8% noise oscillating every ~3s. | **BL.1.3** | **Bot-duel monotonicity + test harness (May 29 2026)** 🤖⚔️🔬 | Second live test showed the bot's score in the **spectator widget** still oscillated up AND down between 1.5s polls — even after BL.1.2 fixed the duel-HUD ticker. Root cause: `_synthesizeBotLiveState` (server-side) and `_liveBotScoreAt` both had `sin()` noise factors that swung negative between polls → displayed score decreased. Also `_calibrateBotScore` used `Math.random()` so the live preview never matched the eventual settled value — a calibration jump on settle that could LOWER the score visibly (regression). Three coordinated changes + a test harness. **Fix 1 — deterministic calibration** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_seededBotRng(seed)` Mulberry32 PRNG; `_calibrateBotScore(duelId, playerScore, playerWinPct)` now takes `duelId` and seeds the PRNG from it. Same inputs → same output, every time. Live preview and final settle produce identical numbers. **Fix 2 — strictly monotonic live score** ([server.js](server.js)): `_liveBotScoreAt` dropped the `sin*0.02` noise factor. Now `target × sqrt(elapsed/duration)` — strictly non-decreasing in `nowMs`. **Fix 3 — DB-enforced monotonic ceiling** ([server.js](server.js)): `_synthesizeBotLiveState` was rewritten with a new pure `_botAsyncCandidateScore` helper. After computing the candidate, the function runs `UPDATE duels SET opponent_live_score = GREATEST(COALESCE(opponent_live_score, 0), $1) RETURNING opponent_live_score` — the existing `opponent_live_score` column (originally for live races) is repurposed as a monotonic ceiling. Even if the candidate formula has a discontinuity (e.g. when player submits and target switches from estimate to calibrated final), the displayed score NEVER decreases — the GREATEST guard preserves the highest value ever computed. Atomic + concurrency-safe. **Test harness** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) — duplicates the four formulas (in sync with server.js) and runs 6 assertions across **thousands of synthetic ticks**: (1) determinism — 50 duels × 4 player scores × 3 calls each, every triple must match; (2) win-rate distribution — 10,000 simulated calibrations, player wins must fall in 48-56%; (3) live monotonicity — 200 duels × 1801 ticks (50ms each), no down-jumps allowed; (4) async monotonicity within anchor — 200 duels × 2502 ticks; (5) full poll lifecycle with DB ceiling — 500 duels × 68 polls each, simulates the GREATEST guard, **0 down-jumps**; (6) settled-matches-preview — preview === actual for 100 duels. **Test run 5×** — all 5 runs produced **identical numbers** (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1%), all 6 tests pass each run, zero down-jumps total. The deterministic seeding is what enables this consistency. **Why this matters**: the waiting-overlay spectator widget is the highest-emotion moment in any duel — a bot whose displayed score visibly drops while the player watches is the loudest possible "this is fake" signal. With DB-enforced monotonicity + deterministic calibration, the bot's score becomes indistinguishable from a real player's. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,931 drops / 8,827 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529g`, SW `bloom-v20.7`. |

When a tier changes, fires one of three keyframes: `dspecAppear` (scale-up + fade from 0; tile dropped from empty), `dspecMerge` (scale 1.28 + gold drop-shadow brightness boost; existing tile upgraded), `dspecClear` (shrink + fade-out; tile vanished). The board now WORKS like a real game in real time. **Fix 6 — _synthesizeBotGrid evolves with score** ([server.js](server.js)): the previous version seeded only on duelId, so the grid was 100% deterministic per (duel, score) — but since score grows by ~600 per server tick, the grid stayed identical for ~2-3 polls before changing. Rewritten to seed on `(duelId XOR bucket)` where `bucket = floor(score / 600)` (roughly one merge event per bucket). Result: the bot's grid evolves smoothly over the game, ~50 distinct layouts per duel by score 30K. Also: `fillBase` now scales with score (1 cell/col at low scores, 3 cells/col at 50K+) so the board "fills up" over time like a real game. **Verification** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) — 2 new tests added: (6a) grid deterministic per (duelId, score), (6b) grid evolves ≥10 changes across 30K range. **Result: 50.0 average grid changes per duel, 30/30 duels evolve well above threshold.** All 8 tests pass × 3 runs each, IDENTICAL results (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1% player/bot/tie). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,009 drops / 8,968 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529h`, SW `bloom-v20.8`. |
| **BL.1.5** | **Bot plays the SAME GAME — real trajectory simulation (May 29 2026)** 🤖🎮⚡ | User caught the lie: the bot's spectator grid was "different shapes every second" — random configurations, not actual gameplay. Also: the bot didn't use the player's chosen difficulty (player at גיהנום with bot in קל), bot's grid score didn't match the eventual final, and the spectator widget didn't show remaining time. Same engine the real game uses → bot's moves look identical to a real player's. **Fix 2 — `_simulateBotDuelTrajectory(seed, weights, durationSec)`**: runs the engine forward for the full game duration, taking 1 snapshot per drop (~33 snapshots in 60s, ~50 in 90s). **Crucially uses the duel's `board_seed` + `difficulty_weights`** — so the bot plays the SAME piece distribution + speed as the player. Hell difficulty → bot also gets weighted 3-7 pieces. Easy → tier 1-2 dominant. Returns `{snapshots: [{t, s, h, g}], finalScore, finalGrid, finalTier}`. Verified: 1-3ms execution, deterministic per seed (same input → identical output), Hell hits tier 8, Easy tier 5, Default tier 6 — confirms difficulty is honored. **Fix 3 — `bot_trajectory JSONB` column + `_getOrComputeBotTrajectory(duel)` cache** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) + [server.js](server.js)): trajectory computed on first spectator poll, stored on the duel row, ~4KB per duel. Subsequent polls hit the cache, zero CPU. **Fix 4 — `_synthesizeBotLiveState` snapshot lookup by PROGRESS** ([server.js](server.js)): the live displayed bot score follows the existing monotonic calibrated curve (BL.1.3 ceiling guard). The GRID is now selected from the trajectory by `progress = displayed_score / target_final`. New helper `_snapshotForProgress(traj, ratio)` returns `snapshots[floor(ratio × (n-1))]`. Result: as the bot's displayed score grows from 0 → calibrated final, the player sees the bot's REAL board evolve through ~30-50 actual gameplay snapshots. Tiles drop, merge, upgrade naturally. Target denominator picks correctly per duel mode: live race → `_liveBotTargetScore`, async post-submit → calibrated final (matches settle), async pre-submit → 40K estimate. Response now also includes `timeLeftMs`, `status`, `difficulty`, `isLive`. **Fix 5 — spectator widget red theme + countdown** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `injectDuelSpectatorWidget` + `pollDuelLiveState` + inline CSS): new countdown row at the TOP of the widget in red-gold gradient — "⏰ נשארו ליריב 23 שניות" — adapts label per duel type (live: "נשארו ליריב", async: "מגיש בעוד"). Header text changes to "⚡ צופה בקרב חי" for live duels (distinct from regular "צופה ב-X חי"). In last 10 seconds: red pulsing border via `dspecCountdownPulse` 0.6s keyframe. Opponent score gets a `dspecScoreBump` cubic-bezier animation when it grows. Cell change animations from BL.1.4 still apply. **Why this is "the right architecture"**: every previous attempt (BL.1.0-BL.1.4) tried to simulate the bot's appearance via randomized synthesis. The bot was always a Potemkin village — looked plausible at first glance but broke under scrutiny ("the tiles don't move like a real game"). BL.1.5 makes the bot actually PLAY THE GAME — same merge engine, same seed, same difficulty. The grid the player sees IS the bot's real board at that moment. The lie disappears because there is no lie. **The score-calibration / visual-decoupling**: trajectory provides the GRID (real), `_calibrateBotScore` provides the SCORE (controlled). Both are deterministic per (duelId, playerScore) so they're consistent across reads. The natural simulation final and the calibrated final aren't the same number, but they're decoupled — natural is metadata, calibrated is what player sees. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,887 drops / 8,774 merges / 0 floating tiles). All 8 bot-score tests pass × 3 runs identical. Cache buster `v20260529i`, SW `bloom-v20.9`. |
| **BL.1.6** | **Bot-duel score-credibility fixes + active-stats coverage (May 29 2026)** 🤖💯📊 | User reported the most-credibility-breaking bug yet: "bot leads with 17K mid-game then ends with 9K final + player wins" — the live displayed score JUMPED DOWN to the settled score. Plus: bot's score starts way ahead of player from t=1s of a 60s race (sqrt-easing's bias toward early scoring). Plus: bot opponents in random matches don't update the home page's "players today" stats. **Four coordinated fixes + a critical regression test.** **Fix 1 — `_botAsyncCandidateScore` pre-submit anchor 40000 → 8000** ([server.js](server.js)): the high anchor caused the live ceiling to grow into the 25-35K range during the player's game; when player submitted with (e.g.) 5000, the calibrated final was ~4500 — a visible drop of ~30K at settle. With anchor=8000, pre-submit ceiling tops out at ~6-7K (matching a "warming up" bot), so when calibrated comes in (typically much higher), the live score climbs UP toward it — no regression possible from this path. **Fix 2 — `_liveBotScoreAt` easing sqrt → quadratic** ([server.js](server.js)): sqrt easing means at t=2s/60s the bot showed `target × sqrt(2/60) = target × 0.182` — already at 6.4K if target=35K, before the player even completed their first merge. Quadratic (`ratio²`) gives `target × 0.001` = 35 points at the same moment — matches a real player's first-tile pace. Curve still reaches full target at t=duration, just back-loaded toward dramatic finish. New test confirms avg bot score at t=2s is **80 points** (was 6000+). **Fix 3 — `_settleBotDuel`: `bot_score = MAX(calibrated, opponent_live_score)`** ([server.js](server.js)): the load-bearing fix. Whatever the live curve displayed, the settled value can NEVER be less. New test 8 simulates 500 duels through the full poll lifecycle and asserts `settled >= liveAtSettle` — **0 regressions across all 500**. User explicitly said: "I don't mind losing, just no lies in the scores" — this fix prioritizes credibility over the 52% win-rate guarantee. In the rare case where pre-submit ceiling exceeds calibrated final (player scored very low), bot ends up winning instead of losing — acceptable. **Fix 4 — `/api/stats/live` bot-duel counts** ([server.js](server.js)): three new queries — `bot_duels_active_now` (status=accepted, 5min window), `bot_duels_active_30m`, `bot_duels_active_hour` — added to `activeNow` / `playingNow` / `activeThisHour` blending. Every random-match bot opponent now contributes to the home-page social-proof bar. Test results stay verified by the existing multiplier cap. **Test harness updates** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) — 2 new tests: **(8) settled ≥ live** — 500-duel poll-lifecycle simulator with strict assertion that settled bot score never falls below the maximum live ceiling ever displayed (0 violations); **(9) bot starts slow** — at t=2s of a 60s race, average bot score must be <500 + max <800 across 200 duels. Both pass on all 5 runs. **Test results 5× consecutive runs, all identical**: deterministic 51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1% win rate, 0 monotonic violations, 0 settle regressions, avg bot t=2s = 80 / max = 122. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,851 drops / 8,786 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529j`, SW `bloom-v21.0`. |
| **BL.1.7** | **Live-race difficulty isolation (May 30 2026)** ⚡🎯 | User reported the practice difficulty was bleeding into 60s live races: "I'm in גהינום (insane) practice → I start a live race → bot duel runs in גהינום too even though I picked default in the duel modal". Two-line root cause: `startLiveRaceGame` ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)) calls `init('practice', { fresh, seed })` to seed the engine with the duel's board_seed — but `init()` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js):164) unconditionally calls `readPracticeDifficulty()` when `mode === 'practice'`, which overrides whatever difficulty the duel was created with. Friend duels + async random match avoid this because they go through `startDuelGame` which sets `sessionDifficulty` directly without calling `init()`. **Fix**: in `startLiveRaceGame`, after the `init()` call, re-apply the duel's stored difficulty (mirrors `startDuelGame`'s pattern). When the duel row has `difficulty_weights`, use them; when null (default duel), explicitly clear `sessionDifficulty = null` so the practice-localStorage override doesn't survive. Plus `updateModeBar()` re-paint so the in-game UI reflects the duel's actual difficulty. Now the rule is unified across all three matchmaking paths: friend duel → modal picker → applied; async random → modal picker → applied; live 60s race → modal picker → applied. Practice difficulty stays in practice. The duel modal pre-selects "default" (the fair option for competitive play), and the player can switch to any of the 5 difficulties before pressing the random / live button. | **DU.2** | **Duel System Overhaul — 3 distinct modes + real wager + score-unification (May 30 2026)** ⚔️💎🤖 | User report: in an async random duel vs a bot, the spectator widget's climbing score didn't match the final result ("bot leads 17K mid-game then settles 9K, scores feel like lies"), AND a 60s timer appeared on the random duel making it indistinguishable from the live race. Full overhaul (spec+plan in [docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-30-duel-system-overhaul-design.md](docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-30-duel-system-overhaul-design.md) + [docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-30-duel-system-overhaul.md](docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-30-duel-system-overhaul.md)). **(1) Score-unification (the headline fix)** — the calibrate-vs-preview split is gone. `POST /api/duels/:id/score` ([server.js](server.js)) now computes `_calibrateBotScore(duelId, playerScore)` ONCE at submit time and persists it in the new `duels.bot_final_score` column, also clamping `opponent_live_score = LEAST(..., final)` so a pre-submit peek can't overshoot. `_synthesizeBotLiveState` async post-submit path drives the displayed score monotonically (quadratic ease, `min(final, final·progress²)`) UP to EXACTLY that locked number, and the grid `_snapshotForProgress` tracks the same ratio. `_settleBotDuel` reads the locked `bot_final_score` and the result-flipping `MAX(calibrated, live_ceiling)` guard is **removed** — the curve is structurally ≤ final, so settle and display always agree. Harness ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) gains Test 10 (500 duels × 61 polls: 0 down-jumps, 0 over-final, converges to exact final) + Test 11 (wager conservation). **(2) Three clearly-distinct modes** — duel modal ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)) labels ⚔️ דו-קרב חבר (purple) + 🎲 דו-קרב אקראי (blue) both as "♾️ משחק מלא · בלי שעון", ⚡ מרוץ חי (red-pink) as "⏱ 60 שניות". Async duel HUD shows the "♾️ בלי שעון" tag; all client `duration` reads gated to `is_live` so the DB-default `duration_seconds=60` never surfaces on async (the 60s leak). **(3) Real gem wager in all 3 modes incl. vs bot** — initiator picks via preset chips (0/50/100/250/500) + balance line; stake deducted atomically at first queue entry, escrowed on the new `duel_matchmaking_queue.wager` column, matched EXACTLY (bot fallback covers quiet queues so exact never traps). `_settleBotDuel` + `_settleLiveDuel` pay the winner `2×wager−rake` (reuses `wager_rake`), refund on tie, nothing on bot-win. Cancel + 5-min stale-cleanup refund any escrowed stake (CTE) so an abandoned search never loses gems. Insufficient-gems → inline hint, never a blocking alert. **(4) Difficulty** — async random bot already honored the duel's difficulty (`_spawnBotDuelForPlayer` → `resolveDifficulty` → trajectory); confirmed `startDuelGame` (sets `sessionDifficulty` directly, no `init()` bleed) + `startLiveRaceGame` (BL.1.7) both clean. **(5) Rematch** carries the same wager + difficulty into the modal. **(6) Admin** — bot-duel card shows 💎 staked vs 💎 paid-out; 5 new config keys with tooltips. Schema: `duel_matchmaking_queue.wager` + `duels.bot_final_score` (idempotent in [schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)) + 5 `game_config` keys. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,012 drops / 0 floating tiles). All 11 bot-score tests pass × 3 runs identical (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1%, 0 down-jumps, 0 over-final, 0 conservation mismatches). Cache buster `v20260530b`, SW `bloom-v21.2`. |
| **DU.2.1** | **Spectator board continuity — no restart-from-zero (May 30 2026)** 🤖🔗 | Follow-up to DU.2. User: "when I finish before the bot and watch its board, the bot's score appears NOT from where I saw it during the game, but from the beginning." Root cause confirmed numerically (live test): the in-game duel HUD shows a CLIENT-computed bot score (`computeBotLiveScore`, ~70-92% of the player's live score, [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)), but the post-finish spectator widget read the SERVER curve `final×progress²` which restarted from ≈0 — two independent sources, so the bot's score jumped backward at the HUD→spectator handoff. DU.2 fixed the END (convergence to the settled final) but not the START. **Fix**: `submitDuelScore` now sends `botSeen` = the last bot score the HUD displayed (`_botLiveScoreCeiling`) before teardown. Server (`POST /api/duels/:id/score` bot branch, [server.js](server.js)) clamps it under the player's score (`min(botSeen, 0.97×playerScore)` — can't flip a player-win), locks `bot_final_score = MAX(calibrated, seen)`, and seeds `opponent_live_score = seen`. `_synthesizeBotLiveState`'s existing `GREATEST(opponent_live_score, candidate)` then makes the spectator START at exactly `seen` and climb to the final — continuous, monotonic, converges, win-rate preserved (seen < player score). Live-verified on production across 4 duels (both player-win + bot-win outcomes): HUD value 17000 → spectator FIRST poll = 17000 (was ~100), 0 down-jumps, converges to final. Harness Test 12 (600 duels: 0 started-below-seen, 0 down-jumps, 0 over-final, 0 win-flips). Cache buster `v20260530c`, SW `bloom-v21.3`. |
| **DU.2.2** | **Bot score never shows an absurd sub-20 value (May 30 2026)** 🤖🔢 | User: "the bot's score suddenly jumps below the minimum of 20 — e.g. 16 — looks very weird." Root cause: `_liveBotScoreAt` (the 60s live race, [server.js](server.js)) was the ONLY bot-score formula without a minimum floor — `_calibrateBotScore`, `_botAsyncCandidateScore`, and the locked async path all floor at `Math.max(100, …)`, but the live formula returned a bare `Math.floor(target × ratio²)`, which early in a race yields 1-19. Real BLOOM scores jump in merge-sized steps (a first tier-1 merge is ~20), so a displayed "16" reads as broken. **Fix**: new `_floorBotVisibleScore(raw)` snaps any value below `BOT_MIN_VISIBLE_SCORE = 20` to 0 ("hasn't merged yet") — kills the weird 1-19 range while keeping BL.1.6's slow start (no head-start gap; t=2s is already ~80). Applied to `_liveBotScoreAt` (server) + `computeBotLiveScore` (client async HUD, [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)). Live-verified on production: the early-race bot curve is now `0 → 26 → 73 → 147 → …` (was `0 → 7 → 16 → 26`). Harness Test 13 (300 duels × 601 ticks: 0 sub-20 nonzero values); Test 9 slow-start + Test 3 monotonic still pass. Cache buster `v20260530d`, SW `bloom-v21.4`. |
| **GH.1** | **GitHub-audit fix sweep (May 30 2026)** 🔬 | User asked to verify the claims in [BLOOM_GITHUB_AUDIT.md](BLOOM_GITHUB_AUDIT.md) and fix only what genuinely needs it. Audit was mostly accurate on architecture but **overstated §2.1** ("22 unprotected `JSON.parse`") — only ONE was truly unprotected; the other 3 cited (07-identity:424, 08-contest-helpers:189/206) are already inside try/catch, and the long stale line-number list (04-ui-utils:467/538, 05a:1428, 05b:94, 05c:245/279/334/518) no longer matches the code. Fixed the 4 verified real bugs: **(1.1 critical)** `ownedSkins = JSON.parse(...)` at [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js):277 ran at boot with NO try/catch — a corrupt `bloom_owned_skins` value → boot throw → white screen → player gone forever. Wrapped in try/catch with `['classic']` fallback + Array/empty guard. **(1.2)** `startLiveRaceGame()` ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)) set `_liveRaceHbTimer`/`_liveRacePollTimer` with no clear-first guard — a double-start (double-tap/rematch) leaked the prior intervals (battery + colliding scores). Added clear-orphan-timers guard at function top. **(1.3)** Self-promo weighted pick at [server.js](server.js):8540 used `ORDER BY RANDOM() * p.weight DESC` — NOT correct weighted sampling (high-weight nearly always wins, low-weight promos starve). Replaced with Efraimidis-Spirakis reservoir sampling `ORDER BY -LN(RANDOM()) / GREATEST(p.weight, 0.001) ASC` → weight now maps to a true proportional probability. **(3.3)** `startLiveRaceMatchmaking` optimistically deducted the wager from `playerBalance` with no `>= wager` check → could flash a negative balance (server escrow was already authoritative, so cosmetic-only); added a guard that shows "💎 אין מספיק יהלומים" and bails. **Not done (judgment / overstated)**: §2.1 (no real unprotected parses remain beyond 1.1), §2.2 dedup-cleanup-cron (`_earn:`/`_gift_rate:` purges already exist; extending to `_ad:`/`_cont:` is minor hardening), §2.3 express error middleware + §2.4 uncaughtException-exit (real but low-value trade-offs; current log-and-stay favors uptime per Railway), §3.1/3.2/3.4 (audits, not simple fixes). | **DU.3→DU.4** | **Bot duels play a REAL game (May 30-31 2026)** 🤖🎮💯 | User: "the bot doesn't really play — it rises in steps, and the points suddenly change at the end." Root: the bot's score was a SYNTHETIC curve decoupled from its board, settle used a third formula. A multi-agent design workflow chose a "trajectory-truth" rewrite (DU.3); a 4-lens **adversarial review workflow** found **12 confirmed bugs** — load-bearing one: `_botEngProcessChains` used the OLD **linear** scoring formula (no tier bonuses), so the bot's "real game" only hit ~5K (3-7× weaker than a human), and real games *cluster* → calibration could never reach 52% without faking (owner vetoed faking). **DU.4 pivot — "One Real Game, One Truth"**: (1) **Scoring parity** ([server.js](server.js) `_botEngProcessChains`): `tier*10*(1+(tier-1)*0.3)*group*chain` (chain capped ×3) + first-time `_BOT_TIER_UP_BONUS` {5:500…8:15000} → bot scores in **human range** (default-90s median ~19K, insane ~40K, live-60s ~9K). (2) **One real game, no calibration**: `_pickBotTrajectory` generates a small bank at spawn, picks a ~40th-percentile (beatable, real) game; `bot_trajectory`+`bot_final_score` locked at spawn (async+live). Deleted `_generateCalibratedTrajectory` + all recalibration/reach-filter/join/cap — kills the handoff-drop, reach-flip, tie, bimodal, live-band, and freeze bugs at the source. (3) `_synthesizeBotLiveState`: ONE trajectory by elapsed time — pre-submit = wall clock (real score+board, no cap), post-submit = replay the SAME game's remaining tail from `submitElapsed` over a window finishing ~6s **before** settle (final held on screen, never a result-screen surprise). (4) **Emergent honest win-rate** (~50%, real-vs-real); **zero faking, ever**. (5) Boot config-warm so the rollback flag (`bot_duel_trajectory_truth`) is honored at once. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): deleted `computeBotLiveScore`; bot painted exactly like a real opponent. **Live-verified on production**: human-range finals, monotonic, board moves (12-16 distinct grids/duel), settle == last frame, mixed outcomes. Config: `bot_traj_candidate_count`=6, `bot_traj_pick_percentile`=0.40 (lower = more player wins). Harness Test 15+16 (snapshot-by-time exact + post-submit continuity 0/0/0). ### 📋 Backlog — PURE ADDICTION (no real money needed — ready to ship)
| Rank | Stage | What it does | Effort | Impact |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **A1** | **Notification Inbox 📬** | Red-badge counter at top-right of home. List of all "new since last visit" events (push history + friend activity + achievement unlocks + tournament results). The single most-tapped UI element in Clash Royale / Brawl Stars / Royal Match. Solves home-discoverability problem. | Med (1-2d) | ★★★★★ |
| **A2** | **Friend Challenges 🎯** | "אני מאתגר אותך לעבור 67K בלוח X" — direct push to a specific friend with deep-link to the board. Reciprocal: when they finish, you get push with their score. K-factor viral lever. | Med (1-2d) | ★★★★★ |
| **A3** | **Trophy Chests 🎁** | Unlock physical "chests" at trophy milestones — chest opens after a real-time delay (4h / 8h / 24h). Player must come back to open. Coin Master + Clash Royale pattern — drives 2-3× DAU. | Med (1-2d) | ★★★★★ |
| **A4** | **Weekly Recap / "BLOOM Wrapped" 📊** | Every Sunday: full-screen summary of the past week (games played / best score / trophies gained / friends played with / hours). Spotify Wrapped pattern. One-time share-ready image. | Small (1d) | ★★★★ |
| **A5** | **Live PvP Race ⚡** | Real-time 1v1 — both players see the same board seed, race to highest score in 60 seconds. Pure adrenaline. Requires WebSocket. | Large (3-4d) | ★★★★★ |
| **A6** | **Skill-based duel matchmaking 🎚** | Currently duels are friend-to-friend by code. Add auto-matchmaking for random opponents in the same trophy range. Brings duels to solo players. | Small (1d) | ★★★★ |
| **A7** | **Daily 7-day Login Calendar 📅** | Visual 7-day grid where each day grants escalating bonus (50→100→200→500→1000💎). Miss a day → start over. Stronger than current single-line daily login. Genshin pattern. | Small (1d) | ★★★ |
| **A8** | **Squad Tournaments 🏟** | Extends Live Tournaments to be guild-based — 4 guilds compete in a bracket weekend. Massive social pull. | Med (2d) | ★★★★ |
| **A9** | **Ghost Mode 👻** | While playing, see a faint overlay of a friend's tile placements on the same board (replay data). "Beat their ghost" mechanic. | Med (2d) | ★★★ |
| **A10** | **Compound interest gem bank 💰** | "Deposit" 💎 in the bank, earn 1%/day passive interest. Players hoard, but exit costs 5%. Behavioral economics hook. | Small (1d) | ★★★ |
