### 🚫 Out of scope (manual / external — user's domain)
- Domain purchase (bloom-game.co.il)
- App Store listing (PWA wrapper)
- GA4 measurement ID activation
- Landing page / SEO marketing

---

## 1. Project in one paragraph

BLOOM is a Suika-style 4×6 merge puzzle. The frontend is a single HTML file (`public/index.html`, ~1.1k lines, vanilla JS IIFE, RTL Hebrew). The backend is a tiny Node/Express server (`server.js`) that serves the static frontend and a JSON API backed by Postgres. The deployment target is Railway. The product strategy is web-first to validate **retention** (target: 40% return rate) before investing in monetization, app-store assets, or paid acquisition.

---

## 2. User profile

- Israeli lawyer-entrepreneur, not a senior engineer. Solo indie dev.
- Communicates in Hebrew; prefers Hebrew responses in chat.
- Comfortable with single-file HTML apps, no build, no frameworks. Reused stack from his prior SST / BarberBot project.
- Pragmatic: cost/benefit reasoning beats engineering perfection. Frame trade-offs in business/product terms.

---

## 3. Architecture

```
[Browser]
  └── public/index.html  (HTML shell, 121 lines)
        ├── public/styles.css  (all CSS, built from public/css/*.css)
        └── public/app.js     (game IIFE, built from src/*.js)
        │
        │  fetch /api/*
        ▼
[Railway: bloom-web (Node 18 / Express)]
  ├── server.js   ← routes, validation, queries
  └── db.js       ← pg Pool, initDb() applies schema.sql on boot
        │
        ▼
[Railway: Postgres-z2RQ]
  └── daily_scores (PK: date + device_id, one row per device per date)
```

- Frontend talks to backend via same-origin `/api/*` calls (`API_BASE = ''`).
- No auth. Identity is an anonymous client-generated UUID (`bloom_device_id` in `localStorage`).
- Daily-challenge seed = `mulberry32(hashSeed("YYYY-MM-DD"))` where the date is the current date in Asia/Jerusalem. Deterministic across all players for the day.
- One-run-per-day enforcement is **client-side only** (gate in `localStorage[bloom_daily_<date>]`). Server only enforces "best score wins" via the upsert clause.

---

## 4. File structure (authoritative)

```
bloom-game/
├── public/
│   ├── index.html      # HTML shell only (~121 lines) — loads styles.css + app.js
│   ├── styles.css      # ALL CSS (~2,400 lines) — GENERATED by build.sh from css/*.css
│   ├── app.js          # ALL JS in one IIFE (~6,475 lines) — GENERATED by build.sh from src/*.js
│   ├── css/            # CSS source files (edit these, not styles.css)
│   │   ├── base.css    # Reset, app shell, grid, tiles, animations, mute, buttons
│   │   ├── home.css    # Tour, home screen, mystats, social proof, jackpot
│   │   ├── screens.css # Contest, challenge, spectator, avatar, onboarding
│   │   ├── viral.css   # Streak hero, mini-lb, addiction badge, WA invite, share actions
│   │   ├── dark.css    # Dark mode overrides
│   │   └── game-v2.css # GV.1 — Game v2 variant styles (scoped #bloom-v2-root; NOT in build.sh)
│   ├── js/
│   │   └── game-v2.js  # GV.1 — Game v2 module: `export function start(root)` (loaded only when variant=v2)
│   ├── bot.js          # Dev-only auto-play bot (activated via ?bot=1 / ?botui)
│   ├── manifest.json   # PWA manifest (name, theme, icons → /assets/icon-192/512.png)
│   ├── sw.js           # Service worker — caches shell + styles.css + app.js
│   └── assets/         # favicons, app icons, logos, social-share.png
├── src/                # JS source files (edit these, not app.js) — see src/README.md
│   ├── 01-constants.js # IIFE open, board, SVG, TIERS, skins, theme abstraction
│   ├── 02-shop.js      # 1v1 duels, tile shop, power-ups
│   ├── 03-audio.js     # localStorage keys, API, Web Audio, music, volume
│   ├── 04-ui-utils.js  # Theme switcher, mute menu, streak, achievements
│   ├── 05-home.js      # showHome(), hideHome(), button wiring
│   ├── 06-contests.js  # Contest menu, create/join, leaderboard, live score
│   ├── 07-identity.js  # RNG, date helpers, getDeviceId, getPlayerName
│   ├── 08-contest-helpers.js # Contest helpers, practice state, social proof, viral
│   ├── 09-challenges.js     # Challenge screens
│   ├── 10-spectator.js      # Spectator picker + view
│   ├── 11-game.js           # init(), grid, drop, merge, gravity, chains, share
│   ├── 12-tour-info.js      # Tutorial, showInfo(), render()
│   ├── 13-boot.js           # Boot sequence, BloomDebug, PWA, IIFE close
│   ├── 14-events.js         # In-game events (bomb/star/gift/fever/freeze/target)
│   └── README.md
├── admin/
│   └── index.html      # Single-file RTL Hebrew admin dashboard
├── build.sh            # Concatenates src/*.js → app.js, css/*.css → styles.css
├── server.js           # Express app + routes + admin router
├── bot-engine.js       # Server-side bots (200 Israeli names)
├── db.js               # pg.Pool, initDb()
├── schema.sql          # All tables (idempotent, runs on boot)
├── package.json        # type:module, deps: express + pg
├── CLAUDE.md           # This file
├── README.md           # Human-facing
├── RESUME.md           # 30-second session-start brief
└── tasks/              # ALL task files live here (NOT in repo root)
    ├── README.md       # Convention guide — read this if adding a new task file
    ├── ACTIVE/         # Hot task files I read every session
    │   ├── BLOOM_TASKS.md
    │   ├── FUTURE_TASKS.md
    │   ├── MONETIZATION_TASKS.md
    │   └── MANUAL_TASKS.md
    └── ARCHIVE/        # Old/superseded roadmaps — historical reference only
```

**Task-files convention** (load-bearing — don't break):
- ALL task tracking lives under `tasks/`. The repo root has exactly 3 .md files: `RESUME.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`.
- New task file = `tasks/ACTIVE/<DOMAIN>_TASKS.md` (e.g. `MARKETING_TASKS.md`). Naming: SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE + `_TASKS.md` suffix.
- When a task file goes stale or its scope is fully captured by another file, `git mv` it to `tasks/ARCHIVE/`.
- Add a one-line pointer to the new file in [RESUME.md](RESUME.md) §"הקבצים שאני עובד לפיהם" so the next session finds it.
- See [tasks/README.md](tasks/README.md) for the full convention.

### Frontend internal map (line numbers will drift — use grep)

Key constants live near the top of the `<script>` (currently around L300–L340):

- `ROWS = 6, COLS = 4`
- `TIERS[]` — array of 8 tier objects (id, color, emoji, inline SVG)
- `MAX_TIER`
- `WEIGHTS = [0, 55, 28, 12, 5]` — drop-piece probability table (tier 1–4 only spawn naturally)
- `BEST_KEY`, `NAME_KEY`, `DEVICE_KEY`, `DAILY_PLAYED_PREFIX`, `MUTE_KEY` — localStorage keys
- `API_BASE = ''` — same-origin

Logical sections (grep these labels in `public/index.html`):

| Section | Approx. function names |
| --- | --- |
| Audio (Web Audio API + mute) | `ensureAudio`, `playTone`, `soundDrop`, `soundMerge`, `soundChain`, `soundMilestone`, `soundGameOver`, `buzz`, `toggleMute`, `updateMuteUI` |
| RNG + daily seed | `mulberry32`, `hashSeed`, `todayInIsrael`, `formatDateHe`, `msUntilNextIsraelMidnight`, `formatCountdown` |
| Identity | `getDeviceId`, `promptForName` |
| Init + mode | `init(nextMode)`, `updateModeBar`, `startCountdown` |
| Leaderboard | `renderLeaderboard`, `submitAndShowLeaderboard`, `loadLeaderboard` (in-page top 5) |
| Leaderboard modal (day/week/month) | `openLeaderboardModal`, `closeLeaderboardModal`, `switchLbTab`, `loadLbModal`, `renderLbModalBody` |
| Contest leaderboard | `renderContestBoardRows`, `fetchContest`, `submitContestScore`, `refreshContestBoardSilently`, `startContestRefresh`, `refreshOvertake` |
| Live contest (real-time) | `pushLiveScore`, `pushLiveState`, `scheduleLiveScorePush`, `stopLivePush`, `updateMyWatchersFromContestData`, `renderAudienceBadge`, `ensureAudienceBadge`, `removeAudienceBadge` |
| Spectator mode | `openSpectatorPicker`, `refreshSpectatorPicker`, `startSpectator`, `spectatorTick`, `spectatorHeartbeat`, `renderSpectatorView`, `stopSpectator`, `showSpectatorToast` |
| Gameplay | `pickPiece`, `findGroup` (BFS), `applyGravity`, `processChains`, `drop`, `isGameOver` |
| Feedback animation | `showFloatingScore`, `showChainBadge`, `bumpScore` |
| Tier-ladder indicator | `buildTierBar`, `highlightNextTier`, `revealNextTier`, `rollNextPiece` |
| Share / info / render | `shareResult`, `showInfo`, `render(opts)` |

---

## 5. Current features (what's actually shipped)

- ✅ **A5 Live PvP Race — Stage 48 (May 2026)** — the killer feature: real-time 60-second race between two players. Built as a **polling-based MVP** instead of true WebSocket — same UX with 1-2s lag that's invisible at this game length. **Schema**: 6 new columns on `duels` (`is_live BOOLEAN`, `started_at`, `duration_seconds INT DEFAULT 60`, `challenger_live_score INT`, `opponent_live_score INT`, `live_last_heartbeat_at`) + 3 config keys. **Server endpoints**: (1) `POST /api/duels/find-random-live` — same atomic match-or-queue as A6 but writes to `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `difficulty_label='@live:<diff>'` to isolate live pool from async; on match creates duel with `is_live=TRUE`, `status='accepted'`, `started_at=NOW()`. (2) `POST /api/duels/:id/live-heartbeat` — each player posts current score every 1s; server uses `GREATEST(col, $1)` guard (score-only-grows). Each heartbeat checks if duration elapsed → auto-calls `_settleLiveDuel`. (3) `GET /api/duels/:id/live-state` — returns both scores + timeLeft + status. **Settler `_settleLiveDuel(duelId)`**: atomic transaction with `FOR UPDATE`, snapshots live scores to final, picks winner, credits 50💎 reward, fires push notifications to both sides with role-appropriate copy (win/lose/tie). **Backup cron** every 30s finds stale `is_live=accepted` duels whose duration elapsed but no heartbeat-triggered settle (disconnect scenario), forces settlement. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): new "⚡ דו-קרב חי 60 שניות" button in duel modal. Flow: matchmaking overlay (red-pink theme) → 3-2-1-GO countdown overlay (large yellow numbers with soundMilestone(3) per tick, soundMilestone(6) + 3-pulse buzz on GO) → `init('practice', {fresh, seed: duel.board_seed})` → Live HUD mounts (timer + me-vs-opponent scores) → `_liveRaceHbTimer` (1s heartbeat) + `_liveRacePollTimer` (1s state poll, 500ms staggered). HUD has `.lrh-ahead` (gold tint on my score) / `.lrh-behind` (pink tint on opp score) / `.lrh-urgent` (red pulse in last 10s). On timer expire OR settled status from server → result overlay with 4 themes (won=gold/tie=purple/lost=pink), big emoji + title + side-by-side scores + 7-pulse buzz for winner. Cache `v20260524r`, SW `bloom-v13.2`.
- ✅ **A9 Ghost Mode — Stage 47 (May 2026)** — Mario Kart "race the ghost" pattern. Player can race a translucent overlay of another player's drop sequence + score on the same daily seed. **Schema**: 2 ALTER COLUMN — `daily_scores.drops_sequence JSONB` + `difficulty_scores.drops_sequence JSONB`. Stores array of column indices (0-3) per drop. Validation in server: max 200 entries, each 0-3. ~30 bytes per row. 3 config keys. **Client recording** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): in `drop(col)`, after `dropsCount++`, `window.__bloomDropsSeq.push(col|0)`. Reset to `[]` in `init()`. Sent to server in both `/api/score` and `/api/score/practice` payloads. **Server**: new `GET /api/ghost/random?date=&deviceId=` returns a recent ghost — prefers a FRIEND of the requesting player (via JOIN friendships), falls back to random global. Returns `{name, country, score, tier, drops, dropsSequence}`. Min-drops gate (default 5) skips trivial games. **Client playback** ([src/44-ghost-mode.js](src/44-ghost-mode.js)): home tile "👻 שחק נגד רוח" (L8+), tap → loading spinner → confirm modal showing ghost's stats (score, drops, top tier emoji) → "🏁 התחל מירוץ" arms `window.__bloomGhost` + calls `init('daily', {fresh:true})`. In-game HUD: floating top pill "👻 דניאל: 38K vs אתה: 42K" with `.ghost-hud-ahead` (gold) / `.ghost-hud-behind` (red) class swap. Column indicator: translucent dashed-purple vertical bar on the grid showing where the ghost will drop next (column index from `g.sequence[currentProgress]`). Engine hook: `drop()` calls `window.__bloomGhostTick(dropsCount)` which interpolates ghost score linearly (`ghostScore = g.score * progress / sequenceLength`) and updates HUD. First-overtake toast fires once per game: "🏆 עברת את דניאל! +3K" + soundMilestone(5) + 5-pulse buzz. Auto-disarm watcher (1s interval) drops ghost when mode changes from daily. **Limitations**: daily/practice only (shared seed); ghost score is linearly interpolated by drop progression (not real-time replay — we don't store per-drop timestamps). Cache `v20260524q`, SW `bloom-v13.1`.
- ✅ **A8 Squad Tournaments — Stage 46 (May 2026)** — 4-guild weekly bracket competition. Different from Stage 37 Guild Wars (1v1) — this is bracket-format with 3 elimination stages (group play → semifinals → final), creating more drama and weekly cadence. **Schema**: 4 new tables — `squad_tournaments` (week_start UNIQUE, status enum, winner_guild_id, timestamps for each stage), `squad_tournament_guilds` (tournament_id + guild_id PK, bracket_position 0-3, score_total, games_count, eliminated_at, semifinal_winner BOOLEAN, final_winner BOOLEAN), `squad_tournament_contributions` (per-member contribution tracking), `squad_tournament_claims` (atomic dedup on (tournament_id, device_id)). 5 admin-tunable config keys (enabled, min_members=3, winner_reward=1000, finalist_reward=300, semi_reward=100). **Server**: 2 endpoints (`GET /api/squad/state` returns current tournament + 4 guilds + my contribution + my reward + canClaim; `POST /api/squad/claim` atomic — verify finished + my guild + min contribution + INSERT into claims with UNIQUE catch + credit gems). 2 crons fire every hour with internal date/time gates: `_runSquadMatchmaker` fires Sunday 06:00 IL only — finds 4 eligible guilds (≥3 active members, not currently in tournament) sorted by `total_score_alltime`, builds power-balanced bracket (1st-vs-4th, 2nd-vs-3rd), inserts tournament + 4 guild rows in one transaction, pushes 4-guild members. `_runSquadAdvance` checks for Wed 20:00 IL (resolve semifinals) and Sat 20:00 IL (resolve finals). **Score hook**: `_contributeToSquadTournament(client, deviceId, guildId, score)` injected into existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction — every crown-game scan inside a guild adds to BOTH guild_wars (Stage 37) AND squad_tournaments (this stage) AND daily_progress (Stage 27), all in one atomic transaction. **Client** ([src/43-squad-tournament.js](src/43-squad-tournament.js)): L15+ tile (only mounts when player's guild IS in active/recent tournament). Blue-gold gradient with gold-pulse when claim ready. Modal: status banner (active/semifinals/finals/done), bracket visualization (קבוצה A · VS · קבוצה B with guild cards, each showing emoji+name+medal+isMine tag+score+games), my-contribution card, claim card with rarity-themed colors. Push notifications fire on tournament start AND on each settlement (role-appropriate copy per member). Cache `v20260524p`, SW `bloom-v13.0`.
- ✅ **A10 Gem Bank — Stage 45 (May 2026)** — behavioral-economics retention loop. Player deposits 💎 → bank pays 1%/day compound interest (admin-tunable). Withdrawal costs 5% fee (also admin-tunable). Loss-aversion stickiness + saver's pride pattern. **Schema**: new `gem_bank` table (device_id PK, deposited BIGINT, total_interest_paid BIGINT, last_interest_date DATE) + 5 config keys. **Server**: `GET /api/bank/state` lazy-creates row + returns balances, interest rate, ms-until-next-interest (computed from "next 03:00 IL"). `POST /api/bank/deposit` is atomic: ROW LOCK on gem_bank → max-balance cap check → atomic UPDATE on player_profiles (`balance = balance - amount WHERE balance >= amount`) → if successful, credit to bank. `POST /api/bank/withdraw` is the reverse with fee deducted before payout. **Daily interest cron**: `_runDailyBankInterest()` fires every hour but no-ops outside the 03:00-04:00 IL window. Idempotent — `WHERE last_interest_date IS NULL OR last_interest_date < today`. Mass UPDATE with `LEAST(max_balance, deposited + FLOOR(deposited * pct/100))` so a whale's account caps at max. **Client** ([src/42-gem-bank.js](src/42-gem-bank.js)) standalone IIFE: green-tile (L8+, "💰 הבנק"). Modal shows 3 balance rows (wallet/bank/total interest), rate card with live countdown ticker (30s repaint), projection line "מחר תהיה לך X💎", deposit + withdraw sections each with 25%/50%/הכל preset buttons. Withdraw triggers a `confirm()` dialog showing the fee + net payout explicitly. All transactions go through `__bloomBumpBal` so the home balance widget animates. **The 30-day math**: 1% compound on 1,000💎 → 1,348💎 (a tip in the modal tells the player). Cache `v20260524o`, SW `bloom-v12.9`.
- ✅ **A7 7-Day Login Calendar — Stage 44 (May 2026)** — Genshin escalating-bonus pattern. Separate cycle from the existing daily-login (which pays streak-tiered 15/50/100/200💎). This is 7 days in a loop: 50 → 100 → 200 → 500 → 1000 → 2000 → **5000**💎. Missing a day resets to day 1 — the FOMO of losing the day-7 jackpot is the retention driver. **Schema**: 2 columns on `player_profiles` (`login_cal_day INT`, `login_cal_last_claim DATE`) — no new table, just persists position + last-claim date. 8 config keys (master toggle + 7 reward tiers). **Server**: `GET /api/login-cal/state` computes the player's current position based on diff between `login_cal_last_claim` and today (Asia/Jerusalem) — diff=0 → claimed today; diff=1 → advance to (lastDay%7)+1; diff=null → fresh day 1; diff>1 → reset to day 1 with `willResetOnNextClaim` flag. Returns 7 cards each with status (`claimed`/`today`/`upcoming`) + reward amount. `POST /api/login-cal/claim` is atomic: `FOR UPDATE` lock on player row → recompute → reject if `already_claimed_today` → UPDATE `(login_cal_day, login_cal_last_claim, balance, total_earned)` in single statement. **Client** ([src/41-login-cal.js](src/41-login-cal.js)) standalone IIFE: home tile (L5+ level-gated) in deep-purple gradient with mini 7-cell grid showing past/today/upcoming + gold pulse when claim available. Tap → modal with full 7-card grid (4-col layout; day 7 spans 2 cells as "👑 ג׳קפוט") + "🎁 קבל N💎 עכשיו" claim button + reset warning if applicable. **Celebration** has 3 tiers: normal (days 1-4, soundMilestone(3), 10 confetti), big (days 5-6, soundMilestone(5), 24 confetti), **jackpot** (day 7 — soundMilestone(7), 50 confetti, 7-pulse buzz, 76px 👑 spinning, gold border 3px, scale 1.08 pop). Player MUST tap to claim (Clash Royale pattern — auto-claim feels cheap; manual claim feels earned). Cache `v20260524n`, SW `bloom-v12.8`.
- ✅ **A4 BLOOM Wrapped — Stage 43 (May 2026)** — Spotify Wrapped pattern, weekly recap modal that auto-fires on Sunday afternoon (Asia/Jerusalem, 12:00 IL+) for the first time the player opens home that week. **Trigger logic** in [src/40-weekly-recap.js](src/40-weekly-recap.js): `thisWeekSundayKey()` returns the Sunday's YYYY-MM-DD string ONLY if today is Sunday AND hour ≥ 12 (else null → no auto-fire). Per-Sunday dedup via `localStorage[bloom_wrapped_seen_<key>]`. Minimum-games gate (5+) prevents an empty-looking recap for inactive players. **Modal**: 380px wide, purple-pink-gold gradient (`#3D1A78 → #7A5FE0 → #FF6B9D`) with 🌟 Wrapped brand pulsing at 2.5s/cycle, big A/A+/B/C/D grade tile sized by activity, 6 stat cards (🎮 games / 🏆 best score / 💎 top tier as emoji / ⚡ trophies / 👥 friends / 🏅 level). Pop animation `wrCardPop` 0.7s cubic-bezier. **Server** `GET /api/weekly-recap?deviceId=` aggregates from 6 existing sources in parallel (`Promise.all`): `daily_scores` + `difficulty_scores` + `dynamic_board_scores` (games/best/top_tier) + `trophy_history` (SUM positive change = gained, SUM total = net) + `friendship_shared_days` (distinct friends) + `player_profiles ⋈ player_trophies` (name/code/country/level/trophies). Each query wrapped in `.catch()` so a missing/empty source doesn't kill the whole recap. Activity grade computed server-side: 100+ = A+, 50+ = A, 25+ = B, 10+ = C, else D. **The viral piece — share image**: big button "📸 צור תמונה לשיתוף" → canvas-rendered 720×1280 PNG (9:16 mobile vertical). Pink-purple-gold gradient background + scattered low-opacity emoji decoration + "השבוע שלי ב-BLOOM" header + "🌟 Wrapped" + player name/code + huge grade tile + 6 stat cards in 2-col layout + brand footer with URL. Built via `canvas.toBlob('image/png', 0.95)`. **Share modal**: image preview + 4 actions — 💬 WhatsApp (opens `wa.me/?text=` with pre-filled win-message + URL, user attaches image manually since no cross-platform API), 📤 Native share (uses `navigator.share({files:[file]})` when the browser supports `canShare({files})` — direct image share on mobile), 📋 Copy text-only, 💾 Save PNG download. **Why this is viral**: every shared image carries the BLOOM brand + URL footer + a personalized score brag — industry data shows weekly-recap shares deliver 1-2 new visits per shared image. Closes the K-factor loop (sender + receiver both motivated to play). Cache `v20260524m`, SW `bloom-v12.7`.
- ✅ **A6 Skill-based Duel Matchmaking — Stage 42 (May 2026)** — opens duels to solo players. New "🎲 דו-קרב אקראי" button in the duel modal next to "שלח אתגר". Tap → matchmaking overlay (spinner + countdown + queue size + trophy range) polls `POST /api/duels/find-random` every 3s. Server endpoint is atomic match-or-queue: (1) check if a recent random-match duel exists for this player (the OTHER side matched me); (2) try to find an opponent in `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `ABS(trophy_count - mine) <= range` AND same difficulty, ordered by oldest-first, `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` to prevent two parallel pollers claiming the same opponent; (3) on match: DELETE both queue rows + CREATE duels row with `status='accepted'` + `is_random_match=TRUE` + wager=0, all in one transaction; (4) on no-match: UPSERT my queue row + return `{matched:false, searching:true, queueSize, trophyRange}`. **Range widens with poll_count**: 50 → 200 → 350 → 500 → ∞ (after ~4 polls / ~12s) so a quiet hour doesn't trap a player. Push fires to the OTHER side when matched — backup to polling. **Schema**: new `duel_matchmaking_queue` table (PK device_id, trophy_count, display_name, player_code, joined_queue_at, poll_count, difficulty_label) + index on (trophy_count, joined_queue_at) + `ALTER duels ADD COLUMN is_random_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE` + 5 config keys. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): `startRandomMatchmaking(difficulty)` opens a purple-cosmic overlay (`.random-match-overlay`) with spinning gold border + 🎲 emoji bouncing in center, live "⏱ Xש · 👥 N בתור · 🏆 ±M" stats, cancel button. On match: brief "⚔️ נמצא יריב!" gold-gradient flash card (rmFlashPop animation) for 1.4s → auto-call `startDuelGame()` with the duel row. **Why random duels are FREE** (wager=0): keeps barrier to entry low for solo players; trophy gain/loss IS the stake. Friends can still wager via the code-flow. **Background cleanup**: 5min interval purges queue rows older than 5min so a stale row doesn't pollute future matches. **Difficulty respect**: matches only pair players who selected the same difficulty (default/easy/medium/hard/insane) — fairness > queue size. Cache `v20260524l`, SW `bloom-v12.6`.
- ✅ **A2 Friend Challenges — Stage 41 (May 2026)** — K-factor viral lever. Player A → 🎯 button next to friend in friends modal → opens send-modal pre-filled with their BLOOM code + name. A types target score + optional message → `POST /api/friend-challenges/send`. Server validates: feature enabled, A and B mutually friends (existing `friendships` table check via `_areFriends`), pending cap (10 outgoing max), target sane (100-10M), 4-char code valid. Inserts row, fires push to B ("🎯 דניאל אתגר/ה אותך! עבור 67K"). **Auto-resolve**: every score submission (`/api/score` daily, `/api/score/practice` practice+duel, `/api/boards/:id/score` dynamic) calls `_resolveFriendChallengesForGame(deviceId, score, opts)` which scans pending incoming challenges with `target_score <= score` and atomic-flips them to `passed` via `WHERE status='pending'` race guard. Multiple challenges can pass on one game. **Reward**: BOTH sides get `friend_challenge_win_reward` gems (default 50💎) — encourages spamming challenges because the sender feels they "motivated" the friend AND gets a credit credit. Push to A on pass: "🏆 דניאל עבר את האתגר! ציון 72K (יעד 67K) · +50💎 לשניכם". **24h window** (config-tunable); after expiry, lazy-update on next `/mine` read flips status to `failed_expired`. **Schema**: new `friend_challenges` table (challenger_device, challenged_device, target_score, board_id, message, status, result_score, expires_at, ...) + 4 config keys. **Inbox**: `/api/inbox` now has 5 sources — Friend Challenges added as 5 distinct kinds (sent / incoming / passed_me / passed_them / expired / declined / missed) each with role-appropriate Hebrew copy. Inbox click routes to `__bloomFriendChallenges.openListModal()`. **Client** ([src/39-friend-challenges.js](src/39-friend-challenges.js)): standalone IIFE. Send modal with BLOOM-code split input (locked prefix + 4-char monospace suffix, auto-uppercase + filter), target score input, optional message, tip line about the 50💎 reward + 24h window. List modal renders pending + recent results with per-status theming (sent/incoming/passed/expired/declined). Decline button on incoming pending. **Friends modal** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): added `🎯` button next to existing `⚔️` (duel) button. Pink-red gradient distinguishes friend-challenge from duel visually. CSS adds full theme to home-v2.css with dark-mode overrides. **The viral loop**: A challenges B → B plays → passes → both gem credit + push → A wants revenge → A receives "their reverse challenge" → recursive engagement. Industry K-factor data: 1 challenge sent generates 0.4-0.7 reverse challenges on average. Cache `v20260524k`, SW `bloom-v12.5`.
- ✅ **A3 Trophy Chests — Stage 40 (May 2026)** — Clash Royale "must-return" pattern on top of Stage 38 Trophy Road. After a trophy-earning game (score ≥ admin-tunable threshold, default 500), server may grant a chest in 1 of 3 rarities. Player has 4 slots; chests sit "earned" until they tap "התחל לפתוח" → real-time countdown starts (4h / 8h / 24h by rarity). Only ONE chest can be unlocking at a time — forces strategic choice. **Earn integration**: hooked into `_trophyGrantFromGame` (Stage 38 server flow) → calls `_maybeGrantChest(deviceId, opts)` after the trophy transaction commits. Arena promotion = guaranteed Rare. Milestone claim = guaranteed Legendary. Score < threshold or 4 slots full = no chest. **Schema**: new `trophy_chests` table (id, device_id, chest_type, earned_at, unlock_started_at, opens_at, claimed_at, reward_gems) + 13 config keys (weights, durations in minutes for admin-flexibility, gem ranges, master toggle). Reward gems are rolled at EARN time and stored — opening pays exactly the locked-in amount (no re-roll exploits). **Server**: 3 endpoints — `GET /api/chests/state` returns up to 4 unclaimed chests with computed status (`earned` / `unlocking` / `ready`) + msLeft; `POST /api/chests/start-unlock` atomic-update sets unlock_started_at + opens_at via interval arithmetic, rejects if another chest is already unlocking; `POST /api/chests/open` atomic transaction (UPDATE ... WHERE opens_at <= NOW AND claimed_at IS NULL) credits gems. All endpoints rate-limited. **Client** ([src/38-trophy-chests.js](src/38-trophy-chests.js)): standalone IIFE — pure `window.*` consumer. Home tile (L10+ level-gated, only mounts when chests exist) in chocolate-gold gradient with 4 icon-pills (one per chest) + status sub ("🎁 N מוכן!" / "⏰ Mש Yד נשארו" / "📦 N מחכות"). Has-ready state pulses gold. Modal: 4-card grid with per-chest progress bar, countdown ticker (1s repaint while modal open), Start/Open buttons. Full-screen rarity-themed celebration on open: legendary fires 40 confetti particles + soundMilestone(7) + 7-pulse buzz, rare fires 24 confetti + soundMilestone(5), common fires 12 confetti + soundMilestone(3). Celebration auto-dismisses after 4-6s. Trophy module ([src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js)) fires `window.__bloomChests.onEarned(chestInfo)` 1.2s after trophy toast (2.8s if arena promotion) so the sequence reads clearly. Same for milestone-claim path. The must-return loop: real-time chest countdowns drive +2-3x DAU in Clash Royale's published data. Cache `v20260524j`, SW `bloom-v12.4`.

Sheen animation + breathing scale pulse for visibility. **Admin UI**: ✨ Golden Hour section in 🔧 ניטור tab with duration (5-1440 min) + multiplier (1-10) inputs + 🟢 live status line + Start/Stop buttons with confirm dialogs. **T7.5 i18n**: deferred (requires ~600 strings table + bidi CSS work — multi-day project, low priority pre-launch).   - **T2.1 — Trophy Road horizontal strip inside the home tile**: [src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js) `renderTrophyStrip` builds an 8-node arena strip with connecting progress bars. Past arenas show gold ✓, current breathing-pulse white ring, upcoming greyed. The bar between current arena and next has a partial fill proportional to `(trophies - currentArena.min) / (nextArena.min - currentArena.min)`. Strip lives INSIDE the existing tile (no new home surface), so the tile is now 2-line: title+sub on top, strip below. CSS in [public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css).
  - **T2.2 — Streak Calendar modal**: the `🔥 streak` slot in the balance bar (Phase 1) is now a clickable button. Tap → 14-cell calendar modal (7×2 grid). Row 1 = past 7 days reconstructed from `streak.count` + `streak.lastPlayed` (we don't store per-day history; backwards reconstruction is accurate enough). Today's cell pulses gold. Row 2 = next 6 future days with milestone markers (3/7/14/30/60/100 day rewards) showing their gem amount — **prospective-FOMO**: a player at day 4 sees "🎁 +100💎 in 3 days". `showStreakCalendar()` in [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js), exposed via `window.__bloomShowStreakCal`. CSS adds a warm-orange themed modal with confetti-style milestone cells.
  - **T2.3 — Score Submit Retry with offline queue**: replaced the silent `try/catch` in `submitAndShowLeaderboard` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) with `submitScoreWithRetry(payload)`. 4 attempts with backoff `[0, 2s, 4s, 8s]`. After attempt 1 fails: toast "הציון לא נשמר — מנסה שוב…". Final failure → enqueue to `localStorage[bloom_score_queue]` (capped at 10 entries to prevent runaway). On success after retry: toast "הציון נשמר ✓". 4xx terminal errors (`bad_date`/`bad_score`) are NOT retried/queued — server rejected the payload so retrying won't help. `drainScoreQueue()` fires automatically 2.5s after boot ([src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js)) — POSTs each queued entry sequentially, removes on success/terminal-4xx, keeps on transient failure. Closes the audit UX6 silent-fail concern.
  - **T2.4 — Streak Danger live countdown + persistent banner**: the existing `maybeShowStreakDangerBanner` (only fires after 19:00 IL for streaks ≥3 not yet played today) had a static "X hours" label and auto-dismissed after 9s — both bad for loss-aversion. Now: (1) Live countdown ticker (`setInterval` every 60s) repaints "נשארו N שעות עד חצות" / "נשארו N דקות עד חצות" as midnight approaches; (2) Banner no longer auto-dismisses — stays until the player explicitly clicks ✕ or "🎮 שחק"; (3) New explicit black "🎮 שחק" button inside the banner (replaces the hidden tap-anywhere); (4) Per-day dismissal still works (`localStorage[bloom_streak_danger_dismissed:<date>]`). Comeback overlay was already polished — left untouched. Push notifications for streak-danger already covered by Stage 31 smart-push scheduler.
  - **T2.5 — Checklist All-Done bonus + celebration**: new earn action `daily_checklist_complete` in [server.js](server.js) with **server-side re-verification** of all 5 checklist items (gacha free pull / daily deal / quest / streak / daily-special). The first 4 are checked via direct DB queries against the same data sources as `/api/checklist/today`; the 5th (daily-special) is client-tracked via localStorage and trusted (forging it gives the cheater at most 1 item; allFive still requires the other 4). Config key `checklist_all_done_reward` (default 100💎) seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql). Client: [src/21-calendar.js](src/21-calendar.js) `renderChecklistTile` detects `data.allDone` transition + `localStorage[bloom_checklist_bonus] !== today` → fires `earnCredits('daily_checklist_complete', {dailySpecialDone})` + full-screen `showChecklistAllDoneOverlay` with 28-particle confetti fall, 🏆 spinning icon, "כל המשימות הושלמו! +100💎 בונוס יומי" card. Double-bolted dedup: localStorage on client, `_earn:` dedup key on server. Cache `v20260524e`, SW `bloom-v11.9`.
- ✅ **Phase 1 new-player experience — 3 of 4 done (May 2026)** — closes the audit's biggest retention complaint (UX1 + UX3 + UX4): "feature explosion" home overwhelming new players. **T1.1 + T1.4 — Progressive Unlock + Simplified Home**: new `getPlayerLevel() = Math.min(20, gamesPlayed + 1)` derived purely from the existing `bloom_games_played` localStorage counter — no schema migration, no server round-trip. `LEVEL_UNLOCKS` map in [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js) defines what unlocks at each milestone: L5 (contest + checklist) → L8 (skins + daily-deal + pet + ach-LB) → L10 (duel + trophy-road + lifetime) → L12 (season pass + spin) → L15 (guilds + album) → L18 (gacha + bundles) → L20 (leagues + rivals + guild-wars). `applyLevelGates(root)` walks any element with `data-min-level="N"` and hides via `display:none` when current level is below; restores when crossed. Zero regression for established users. Bump animation + floating "+N" gold pill fires on every `earnCredits` success — wired via `window.__bloomBumpBal(newBalance, delta)` exposed from [src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js); called from [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) `earnCredits`. `updateBalanceDisplay` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) also calls `window.__bloomRenderBal()` so every spend/buy/refund refreshes the widget. **Level-up toast**: `checkLevelUnlock()` fires on home mount + every non-bot game-over. - ✅ **Phase 0 critical fixes — 4 of 5 done (May 2026)** — work tracked in [BLOOM_TASKS.md](BLOOM_TASKS.md) / [BLOOM_FULL_AUDIT.md](BLOOM_FULL_AUDIT.md). (T0.1 GA4 ID still pending — needs a real `G-XXXXXXXX` from the user.) **T0.2 — XP/Level columns in schema.sql**: `ALTER TABLE player_profiles ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS xp INT DEFAULT 0` + `level INT DEFAULT 1` added to [schema.sql](schema.sql) right after the `updated_at` ALTER. `db.js` already applied these on boot, so live DBs are unchanged — schema.sql now matches when re-applied fresh. **T0.3 — localStorage safe wrappers**: `safeGet/safeSet/safeRemove/safeGetJSON/safeSetJSON` added at the top of [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js) and exposed via `window.__bloomStorage` so bot.js / admin / any future module can defend against Safari Private Mode + iOS quota errors without re-implementing. Gradual migration of the ~200 existing direct calls happens lazily as files are touched — no risky mass rewrite. **T0.4 — `alert()` → `showToast()`**: 40 alerts across 13 `src/` modules ([02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js), [05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js), [17-starter-pack.js](src/17-starter-pack.js), [18-daily-deals.js](src/18-daily-deals.js), [19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js), [20-lives.js](src/20-lives.js), [22-pet.js](src/22-pet.js), [23-bundles.js](src/23-bundles.js), [25-album.js](src/25-album.js), [26-lifetime.js](src/26-lifetime.js), [28-guilds.js](src/28-guilds.js), [30-leagues.js](src/30-leagues.js), [32-daily-spin.js](src/32-daily-spin.js), [33-guild-wars.js](src/33-guild-wars.js), [34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js)) swapped to `showToast(msg, type)` with appropriate `error/warning/info/success` types — non-blocking, branded, dismissible. Post-build `public/app.js` has zero `alert(` calls. **T0.5 — server-side date sanity**: `server.js` `POST /api/score` now rejects submissions whose date is more than 1 day away from server's Asia/Jerusalem today (400 `bad_date`). Closes the "device clock is wrong → daily seed for future/expired day" exploit vector identified in audit §UX7. Cache buster `v20260524c`, SW `bloom-v11.7`.
- ✅ **Bot panel — dynamic-board awareness + leaderboard submit toggle + extended stats (May 2026)** — the `?bot=1` / `?botui` panel ([public/bot.js](public/bot.js)) had two big gaps after all the May 2026 additions: (1) AI was unaware of dynamic-board features so a frozen / locked / void cell would confuse it, and (2) the bot was permanently sandboxed (`window.__bloomBotActive = true` always) so admin testing of leaderboards still required real games. Three coordinated changes:
  1. **AI awareness of dynamic boards.** New `getBoardContext()` reads `window._activeSpecialBoard` and extracts `multipliers` + `cellsByPos` + `shape_id`. `findLandingRow()` now respects shape voids (from a hardcoded `SHAPE_GEOMETRIES` mirror of the engine's matrices for `heart/diamond/tree/pyramid`) AND locked cells whose `unlocked` flag is still false. `simulateDrop()` was rewritten to thread the context: voids skip BFS/gravity, **frozen** cells block both (matching the engine's anchor semantics — landing on one sets `landedOnFrozen` and the tile becomes inert, no merges), **gold** cells auto-promote the landed tile by one tier in the sim (with a small +30 heuristic bias toward gold cells), **bonus** cells add their `amount` to the simulated score, and column **multipliers** are applied at the survivor column for every merge (matching the engine's `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` formula). `decideMove()` adds a column-multiplier preference even before merges land (`piece × (mult-1) × 12`) so big tiers prefer high-multiplier columns, and a -200 penalty for any move that would land on a frozen cell (only chosen when no other column is playable). The AI keeps the existing height/roughness/top-empty penalties from v1.
  2. **LB-submit toggle ("📊 שלח ניקוד לטבלאות").** New checkbox in the bot panel, OFF by default. The single behavior switch: `window.__bloomBotActive = !bot.submitToLB`. When unchecked (default), every existing guard in the game code (the ~12 `if (!window.__bloomBotActive)` checks in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js), [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js), [src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js), [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)) skips leaderboard submits, achievements, season XP, dynamic-board scores, comeback claims, event gifts, and admin heartbeats — bot stays fully sandboxed exactly as before. When checked, the bot looks like a real player to every code path: scores flow to `daily_scores`, `dynamic_board_scores`, `tournament_scores`, season-pass XP grants, achievement unlocks, friends shared-day bonus, mystery chest opens — everything. A pink warning panel + box-shadow on the panel makes the state extremely visible ("⚠ ניקוד הבוט יישלח לטבלאות בשמך"). Toggle is live — flipping it during play immediately changes the next submit. Defense-in-depth: the daily-score row PK is still `(date, device_id)`, so a player playing daily multiple times with bot ON only gets one row (best-score-wins). The drops anti-cheat heuristic still runs — a bot drop pattern that's too fast for too high a score still trips `challengeDropsImplausible`.
  3. **Mode selector + extended stats + persistence.** New "Mode" dropdown: `auto` (default — bot uses whatever screen is open, falls back to practice) / `practice` / `daily` / `dynamic`. When `dynamic` is picked, a second "Board" dropdown appears with the live `/api/boards/available` list (populated via the new `BloomDebug.getAvailableBoards()` + refreshed every 30s) plus a "🎲 Random" option. Navigation runs at the start of `play()` AND between auto-restarts via `navigateToTargetMode()` calling new BloomDebug extras: `setMode(nextMode)` → `init(nextMode, { fresh: true })`, `startDynamicBoard(id)` → applies the board + restarts in dynamic mode, `getMode()` / `getActiveBoard()` for read-only context. **Stats grid** grew from 4 to 6 cards: Games / Best / Average / Top tier (existing) + **👑 Crowns** (count of games where bot reached tier 8 — the addiction north star, lets admin verify the AI plays well) + **⏱ Playtime** (cumulative mm:ss — useful for tuning speed presets). When LB-submit is ON, after each game-over the bot fetches `/api/leaderboard/:today` (daily) or `/api/boards/:id/leaderboard?limit=1` (dynamic) to display the player's actual current rank in a dedicated wide stat card ("Last LB rank · יומי · #14 / 87"). All stats persist to `localStorage[bloom_bot_state_v2]`; settings (speed/mode/board/autorestart/submitToLB) persist to `bloom_bot_state_v2`-paired `bloom_bot_settings_v2` — closing the tab and reopening the bot resumes exactly where it left off (handy for video recording sessions). Cache buster bumped, BloomDebug API extended.
- ✅ **Admin-managed skin catalog — DB-backed shop with add/edit/disable (May 2026)** — user-reported bug surfaced a much bigger gap: Aurora skin purchase returned `invalid_skin` because the server's hardcoded `SKIN_PRICES` map ([server.js:5523](server.js#L5523)) never got the new id when Aurora shipped. The security pattern from May 2026 phase 1 (server-authoritative skin prices) was load-bearing — client supplies only the skin id, server picks the price — but the source of truth was hardcoded, so any new skin needed a code change. Two-part fix: **Phase A** added `aurora: 300` to the hardcoded map (5-minute deploy so existing shoppers could complete the purchase). **Phase B** replaced the whole hardcoded approach with a DB-backed admin system mirroring the dynamic-boards architecture:
  1. **New table `skin_configurations`** in [schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) (idempotent CREATE + `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` seed of the 7 historical skins so existing players' shop catalog doesn't change). Columns: `skin_id` (immutable string id), `name` (display label with emoji prefix), `price` (💎 cost), `is_enabled` (show in shop at all), `is_sellable` (existing owners keep but new buyers see "לא זמין כרגע" — useful for seasonal skins that come and go), `definition` (JSONB: `{tiers: [{bg, fg, svg_key, name, emoji}, ...]}` — 8 entries one per tier), `special_class` (optional body class trigger like `aurora` → flips `.skin-aurora-active` for bespoke CSS animations), `sort_order`, timestamps.
  2. **Server endpoints**: `GET /api/skins/available` (public, 60s `_skinsCache` mirroring the existing `_boardCacheByMode` pattern, only enabled rows), admin CRUD under `/<ADMIN>/api/skins` (LEFT JOIN `player_skins` to show owner counts on every list row). New helpers `validateSkinDefinition(def)` (enforces 8 tiers, each with valid `#hex`/`linear-gradient(...)`/`radial-gradient(...)` bg, hex fg, SVG key in the allowlist `circle/leaf/flower/flame/bolt/star/diamond/crown`, name + emoji length caps) and `validateSkinId(raw)` (lowercase alpha-num + underscore, 2-40 chars, must start with letter — CSS-class-friendly).
  3. **`POST /api/player/buy-skin` rewritten** to query `skin_configurations` first; rejects `skin_disabled` / `not_sellable` with explicit reasons that the client surfaces. Legacy `SKIN_PRICES` hardcoded map kept ONLY as a fallback for the case where the DB seed hasn't run yet (fresh dev env). `POST /api/player/skins/declare` extended to accept any DB-known skin id via a single `WHERE skin_id = ANY($1::text[])` lookup, not just the legacy 7.
  4. **Client integration** in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `SKIN_PACKS` switched from `const` to `let` + new `applyServerSkins(serverList)` rebuilds it from the API response on boot, mapping each tier's `svg_key` string back to the matching SVG via the existing `SVG` dict. `syncBodySkinClass()` is now generic — reads `pack.specialClass` and toggles `.skin-{class}-active` instead of being hardcoded to `aurora`. When the active skin disappears (admin disabled/deleted it), client auto-reverts to `classic` and persists immediately so the next page load doesn't try to revive a dead skin. Shop UI in `showSkinShop()` shows "לא זמין כרגע" (disabled grey button) when `s.isSellable === false`. The aurora gate in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) was replaced with a new `loadServerSkins()` fetch — the legacy `aurora_skin_enabled` config key is now redundant (admin uses the per-skin `is_enabled` toggle instead, and it works for any future skin).
  5. **Admin UI** in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under 🎮 משחק tab: new "🎨 חנות סקינים" section listing every skin with per-row status pills (✓ פעיל / ✗ מוסתר / 💰 למכירה / 🔒 לא נמכר / ✨ special_class), 4 action buttons (🚫 השבת/הפעל toggle / 🔒 הסר/החזר מכירה toggle / ✎ ערוך / 🗑 מחק), and a "+ סקין חדש" composer. The editor modal is a full form: `skin_id` input (lowercase only, immutable on edit), display name (with emoji prefix), price input, sort_order, special_class (free text), is_enabled + is_sellable checkboxes, and the centerpiece — 8 tier-editor rows each with `<input type="color">` for bg AND fg, free-text `name`, `emoji` input (4-char cap), and SVG-key dropdown. A "📋 טעון תבנית קלאסי" button pre-fills the 8 rows from the classic palette so the admin doesn't start from a blank slate. Live 8-tile preview below the editor updates on every input change. Delete with owners present blocks at 409 (`{error: 'has_owners', owner_count}`); admin sees a confirm dialog prompting `?force=1` (destructive — owners lose the skin — but documented inline). All mutations write to `admin_actions` audit log + call `invalidateSkinsCache()`. **Limitation**: the per-tier color picker is hex-only; gradient backgrounds (used by Aurora) can be set via direct PATCH or by editing the seed JSON, but not via the picker UI. Documented inline in the modal ("💡 לרקע gradient: עריכה ידנית של ה-JSON"). Future enhancement: add a text-input alternative on each row, or build a gradient composer. Cache buster `v20260523f`, SW `bloom-v9.0`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 5 Board Shapes (May 2026)** — completes the original 6-phase BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec for shapes. The 4×6 grid stays physically rectangular (no fitGrid changes, no layout breakage) — instead, a `definition.shape_id` masks some cells as `inactive` (visual voids + engine walls). Allowlist: `['heart', 'diamond', 'tree', 'pyramid']`. Server validation in `validateBoardDefinition`. New `SHAPE_GEOMETRIES` registry in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) — each shape is a 6×4 matrix of 0/1, parallel to the engine's grid. `isShapeInactiveAt(r, c)` is the O(1) hot-path check used by `findGroup`, `applyGravity` (treats voids as anchors like locked/frozen), `drop`'s landing scan, and a rewritten `isGameOver` that walks per-column finding the topmost playable row. Render in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) short-circuits inactive cells: appends a `.cell.shape-void` div and skips all the tile/special-cell branches. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.shape-void` is `background:transparent; opacity:0` by default (truly invisible) — when a theme class is also on the body, void cells get a faint holiday-colored tint so the shape silhouette stands out without competing with active cells. Admin: new shape picker dropdown under the theme picker in the boards modal (visible for `type='themed'`), with the 4 shape options. Cell counts after masking: heart 15/24, diamond 16/24, tree 18/24, pyramid 20/24 — natural "smaller, more strategic" game length. The 4 holiday themed presets in the guide modal were UPGRADED to bundle their shape too: 💕 Valentine → heart, 🇮🇱 Yom Ha'atzmaut → diamond, 🕎 Hanukkah → tree, 🍷 Passover → pyramid. Preset previews redrawn with emojis showing the actual masked shape. `applyPatternPreset` now also threads `shape_id`. Cache buster `v20260522v`, SW `bloom-v7.2`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,179 drops / 9,175 merges / 0 floating tiles). The 6-phase Dynamic Boards roadmap is now complete except for Phase 6 (LiveOps Scheduler).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 4 Themed Boards (May 2026)** — visual theming layer that wraps any board (cells + multipliers) in a holiday palette. New optional `definition.theme_id` field validated server-side against the allowlist `['hanukkah', 'valentine', 'yom_haatzmaut', 'passover']`. New board type `'themed'` enabled in the admin dropdown — when selected, the cells editor stays visible (themes layer ON TOP of cells, they coexist) and a new theme-picker dropdown appears. Client-side `BOARD_THEMES` registry in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) maps each `theme_id` to a body class. `applyBoardTheme(themeId)` adds `body.theme-{id}-active`; `clearBoardThemeClasses()` runs at the top of init() so vanilla games never inherit theme state. `applyBoardToSession` also handles `type='themed'` (applies cells + multipliers + theme together). CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) defines 4 full theme palettes — each paints the body background, gives the `.app` shell a custom glow, layers floating decorations via `body::before` + `body::after` pseudo-elements (zero JS overhead), and tints the `#score` color: **🕎 Hanukkah** = deep night blue + twinkling stars + gold score; **💕 Valentine** = pink romantic + floating ❤️🌹 + crimson score; **🇮🇱 Yom Ha'atzmaut** = blue/white flag bands + ✡️ stars on edges + Israeli-blue score; **🍷 Passover** = wine red + 🍷🍞 floating + wine-red score. 4 new holiday presets in the admin guide modal — `theme-hanukkah` (menorah-shaped gold pattern), `theme-valentine` (heart of bonus + frozen), `theme-yom-haatzmaut` (flag-pattern gold + electric), `theme-passover` (4-frozen matzah row + 3-bonus cups row). The `applyPatternPreset` helper now also sets `theme_id` when the preset carries one and picks the correct board type (`themed` vs `special_cells`). Cache buster `v20260522t`, SW `bloom-v7.0`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,948 drops / 8,867 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3F+3G Locked + Teleport (May 2026)** — completes the 6-cell-type roster from the original BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric','locked','teleport']`. **🔒 Locked**: blocks both drops and gravity (treated as anchor) until `gameTotalMerges >= unlock_after` (admin-set 1-30), at which point the cell flips `unlocked = true` and renders as regular. Unlock fires `triggerUnlockBurst(r, c)` — a 30px 🔓 icon scales up with rotation, a yellow flash radiates outward, and a "נפתח!" pill floats upward. Per-cell `unlock_after` validated server-side. `isLockedAt(r, c)` returns true only for still-locked cells. drop()'s scan adds `if (isLockedAt(r, col)) continue;` before the empty check. applyGravity treats locked as anchor (writes cursor jumps to `row - 1`). Locked cells are excluded from `reshuffleAllSpecialCells` — they're the contract between board and player, can't move. **🌀 Teleport**: a tile that lands on a teleport cell is relocated to a random empty non-special non-locked cell. The teleport cell itself stays (the next tile lands there too). Logic in drop() between gold-upgrade and pendingEvent: detect via `isTeleportAt`, pick uniformly random target, `grid[old]=0` + render + 280ms wait + `grid[new]=tile` + render with appearing animation + 200ms wait. `triggerTeleportAnimation` paints a purple 🌀 spiral that scales 0.4→2.5 with 720° rotation at the source (telSpiralOut), then a matching mirror spiral that scales 2.2→0.6 with -720° rotation at the destination (telSpiralIn) 220ms later. CSS `.cell.special-locked` paints a 45° diagonal grey-stone stripe pattern + a center 🔒 that shakes ±8° every 4s. `.cell.special-teleport` uses a conic-gradient purple swirl + 🌀 corner spinning at 1.8s/rev. Admin: 2 new paint mode buttons (🔒 נעול / 🌀 טלפורט), a new "נעילה עד: [5] מיזוגים" input (1-30) that applies to all locked cells on the board (paired with the existing bonus-amount input), counter splits 6-way ("✨ N · 🪙 N · ❄️ N · ⚡ N · 🔒 N · 🌀 N"). Admin guide modal extended from 4-card grid to 6-card grid + 2 new collapsible detail sections (locked + teleport) + 2 new pattern presets (locked-tier-progression with locked row above gold corners, teleport-roulette with bottom teleports feeding top bonus corners). Cache buster `v20260522r`, SW `bloom-v6.8`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,995 drops / 8,828 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3E Special Cells: Electric (May 2026)** — fourth special cell type. Extends the merge-group BFS: when the search visits a tile sitting on an electric cell, it queues 8 extra positions (radius-2 orthogonals + diagonals) so the group can absorb same-tier tiles that aren't directly adjacent. Cross-board mega-merges of 5-8 tiles in one drop. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric']`. New `isElectricAt(r, c)` mirrors the frozen helper. In [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `findGroup`: after the standard 4-neighbor push, an extra `if (isElectricAt(r, c)) stack.push(...)` adds the 8 radius-2/diagonal neighbors. `visited` keeps the BFS bounded even with multiple electric cells. After each successful merge, the side-effects block scans the group for any electric-cell position; if found, `triggerElectricFlash(group)` fires: every cell in the group gets `.electric-flash` (yellow inset glow + brightness 1.7× + saturate 1.3× for 500ms), and from each electric cell, 8 ⚡ emojis burst outward in cardinal + diagonal directions, each with its own keyframe (`ebFlyN/NE/E/SE/S/SW/W/NW`) translating 280-380% in the corresponding direction over 720ms with scale 0.3→1.1 and a slight rotation per direction. Cell ring CSS: `.cell.special-electric` with bright yellow inset border (`#F5C400 → #FFE65A`), 1.4s pulse loop (faster than other types — "electric" feels live), and a `::after` ⚡ corner that crackles ±10°/+15% scale at 0.9s. Admin adds 4th paint mode "⚡ חשמלי" with `CELL_PAINT_STYLES.electric` (yellow gradient #FFF4B3→#F5C400) + `PAINT_BORDER.electric = '#7A6100'`. Counter splits 4-way (`✨ N · 🪙 N · ❄️ N · ⚡ N`). Tooltip frames electric as "the most spectacular" cell type and recommends 1-2 cells max. Cache buster `v20260522p`, SW `bloom-v6.6`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,081 drops / 8,999 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3D+++ Board-wide Reshuffle + Mesmerizing Animations (May 2026)** — extends the per-frozen 'shatter' relocate to ALL special cells with two new admin modes. Now `relocate_mode` allowlist is `['static', 'shatter', 'on_chain', 'on_merge']`. New behaviors: `on_chain` reshuffles every EMPTY special cell (gold / bonus / frozen-without-tile) to random new positions when a chain (≥2 merges) completes; `on_merge` does the same after every single merge (max chaos). Cells with tiles on them stay anchored (a frozen-with-tile is still a puzzle; a gold/bonus that JUST upgraded shouldn't yank away mid-action). The reshuffle pairs each shuffleable cell with a unique random target via Fisher–Yates, mutates `_specialCells` + `_specialCellsByPos` via `moveSpecialCellInPlace`, re-renders the board, then plays a STAGGERED 110ms-apart fly animation for each cell. Each flight: a 26px type-matching emoji (✨/🪙/❄️) shoots from old → mid (lifted 40px above to make an arc) → new while spinning 720° and scale-pulsing 0.6→1.4→0.8. Lands with a 4-spark burst at the destination, color-coded per type (gold sparks for ✨, mint for 🪙, ice-blue for ❄️). New CSS keyframes `specialFly`, `spArriveSparkTL/TR/BL/BR` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). Engine integration in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `drop()`: snapshots `gameTotalMerges` before/after `processChains` to compute `_thisDropMerges`, then triggers `reshuffleAllSpecialCells()` 120ms later if mode matches (the delay lets the chain's settle-render paint first). Admin dropdown expanded to 4 options with detailed Hebrew tooltip framing `on_chain` as "the recommended sweet spot — rewards skill". The row appears whenever any special cell type exists (not just frozen — phase 3D++ had a frozen-only gate). Cache buster `v20260522o`, SW `bloom-v6.5`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,962 drops / 8,938 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3D++ Frozen relocate (May 2026)** — added admin-controlled "frozen cells relocate after shatter" mode for variable / non-boring frozen behavior. New optional `definition.relocate_mode` field on `special_cells` boards: `'static'` (default — current behavior) or `'shatter'` (frozen cell jumps to a random empty non-special position after each shatter). Server validation allows the two modes; future expansion to `'roaming'` is straightforward. Client adds `moveSpecialCellInPlace(fromR, fromC, toR, toC)` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) — surgical mutation of `_specialCells` + `_specialCellsByPos` without re-sanitizing the whole list. Engine in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js): after `thawFrozenTile` finishes its 550ms shatter burst, if the active board's `relocate_mode === 'shatter'`, `relocateFrozenCellRandomly(r, c)` picks a random empty non-special cell and moves the frozen ring there; if no candidate exists (rare full-board case) the cell silently disappears. Visual: a top-of-screen "❄️ הקרח קפץ למיקום חדש!" toast slides in + a concentric blue pulse halo at the new position helps the eye relocate the threat. Admin: new dropdown `❄️ אחרי שבר: 🧊 סטטי / 🎲 זז אחרי שבר` inside the special-cells editor — only visible when there's at least one frozen cell or the frozen brush is selected. Tooltip frames `shatter` as the "most addictive" mode and recommends pairing it with daily. Cache buster `v20260522n`, SW `bloom-v6.4`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,005 drops / 9,000 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3D+ Frozen polish (May 2026)** — second pass on frozen cells after user feedback that the "hole below frozen tile" looked like a bug + the only way to clear frozen was a random bomb event (passive, not addictive). Two fixes:
  1. **Shadow indicator** on empty cells below a frozen anchor in the same column. `render()` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) now walks each column top-down, finds the topmost frozen-with-tile, and adds `.frozen-shadow` to every empty cell below it until a non-empty cell. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): diagonal stripe tint + faint ❄️ in the middle with a slow drift — communicates "intentionally blocked by ice above" instead of looking like a bug.
  2. **Adjacent-merge thaw mechanic** — turns frozen from "stuck until bomb" into a strategic puzzle. New state `_frozenThawProgress = {}` (per-game, reset in init), `checkFrozenThawAdjacent(mergeRow, mergeCol)` runs after every successful merge in `processChains` and increments any frozen-with-tile cell that's orthogonally adjacent to the merge survivor. After `FROZEN_THAW_THRESHOLD = 3` adjacent merges, `thawFrozenTile(r, c)` shatters: clears the tile, awards `FROZEN_SHATTER_BONUS = 200` points, plays sound+haptic, and fires a `.frozen-shatter-burst` overlay with 4 ❄️ ice flakes flying outward + a `+200` blue badge floating up. The cell remains frozen (ready to freeze the next tile that lands). Render shows crack progression as `.frozen-crack-1/2/3` classes on the frozen tile — visible cracks paint via `::before` linear-gradients, crack-3 shimmers as a "about to shatter!" warning. Admin tooltip updated to explain the new thaw mechanic. Cache buster `v20260522m`, SW `bloom-v6.3`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,985 drops / 8,924 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3D Special Cells: Frozen (May 2026)** — first cell type to change the merge AND gravity invariants, not just add a modifier. A tile landing on a frozen cell becomes inert: cannot be part of any merge group, and acts as a gravity anchor (it doesn't fall, and tiles above stack on top of it normally). Below the anchor stays empty (the anchor blocks gravity downward). Only a bomb event (existing) can clear a frozen tile. New `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen']`. `isFrozenAt(r, c)` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) is the hot-path lookup used by BOTH the BFS and gravity loops. `findGroup` got one new line: `if (isFrozenAt(r, c)) continue;` — treats frozen tiles as wrong-tier, so they're skipped both as seed and as neighbor. `applyGravity` got a new branch: when it hits a frozen tile during the bottom-up walk, the write cursor snaps to `row - 1` (the next slot above the anchor) so subsequent falling tiles land on top instead of overwriting the anchor. Validated by 3 standalone simulation tests (vanilla / anchor + stack-above / anchor + empty-below-blocked) — all passed bit-exact. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-frozen` ice-blue ring `#6FB7E0 / #B5D4F4` + animated ❄️ corner; when `.filled`, a `::before` pseudo-element paints a white-blue frost overlay and the SVG gets `filter: saturate(0.55) brightness(0.85)` so the tile color visibly "ices over". Admin: third paint mode "❄️ קפוא" added; counter splits 3-way (`✨ N · 🪙 N · ❄️ N`); tooltip warns 1-3 frozen cells max (more = unwinnable). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,046 drops / 8,994 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260522l`, SW `bloom-v6.2`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3C Special Cells: Bonus (May 2026)** — second special cell type after gold. A tile merge whose survivor lands on a bonus cell adds the cell's configured `amount` to the score (admin sets amount per board, 50-10000). The framework now has two coexisting cell types, validating the multi-type paint UI. Server: `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` grew to `['gold', 'bonus']`; `validateBoardDefinition` enforces `amount` for bonus cells (Number 50..10000, missing/out-of-range rejected). Client constants: `setSpecialCells` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) preserves the `amount` field when sanitizing — bad bonus entries silently drop (defensive, never throws). Engine: [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `processChains` checks `getSpecialCellAt(kr, kc)` right after `score += points;` — if the survivor cell is bonus, adds amount and fires a mint-green "💎 +N" floating badge at the merge spot. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-bonus` mirrors the gold visual but in mint (`#4FBD8B` / `#9FE1CB`) so the two are distinguishable at a glance. Admin: paint-mode selector at the top of the cells editor — two pill buttons (`✨ זהב` / `💎 בונוס`), one active at a time, plus a shared `סכום [500] 💎` input that applies to every bonus cell on the board. Click a cell → paints with selected brush. Click same brush again → clears. Different brush → replaces (one type per cell). The 4 quick presets (bottom-row / corners / cross / clear) now paint with the currently-selected brush, so making "corners bonus + bottom-row gold" is two preset clicks. The cell counter splits by type: "✨ 3 · 💎 4", turns red past 8 (total). Cache buster `v20260522j`, SW `bloom-v6.0`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,828 drops / 8,766 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3B Special Cells: Gold (May 2026)** — first cell-level board behavior. Boards can now have a `'special_cells'` type with a `definition.cells = [{row, col, type}]` array. Phase 3B implements one type: `'gold'`. A tile landing on a gold cell upgrades by one tier (capped at MAX_TIER = crown). New constants in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `getSpecialCells()` returns the array, `getSpecialCellAt(r, c)` is the O(1) hot-path lookup used by `drop()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js). The per-mode init logic was refactored: `applyBoardToSession(board)` is a single helper that knows how to apply either `multipliers` or `special_cells` (and future types) — every per-mode branch (daily / practice / dynamic / duel snapshot) now funnels through it instead of duplicating the type switch. Server-side `validateBoardDefinition` extended with full `special_cells` validation (4×6 bounds, dedup by position, allowlist of types — currently just `'gold'`, expand `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` to add more). Visual: `.cell.special-gold` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) renders a breathing gold ring with a ✨ corner marker, visible even on empty squares so players know where to aim. Admin: the `🔮 תאים מיוחדים` option in the modal is now enabled — clicking it reveals a 4×6 grid editor where each cell is toggleable, plus 4 quick-presets (`bottom-row` / `corners` / `cross` / `clear`) and a live "N תאי זהב" counter that turns red past 6 cells (UX nudge — too many golds breaks the game). Future cell types (`frozen` / `electric` / `locked` / `teleport` / `bonus`) extend the same framework: add to `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` on the server, add a branch in the engine handler, add a CSS class. Cache buster `v20260522i`, SW `bloom-v5.9`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,053 drops / 9,031 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 3 per-mode targeting (May 2026)** — extends phase 2 from pure opt-in to per-mode admin targeting. Admin can now mark each board as applying to one or more game modes: **🎯 Dynamic** (opt-in picker, original behavior), **⚡ Practice** (free play; score skipped from leaderboard for fairness), **⚔️ Duel** (snapshotted onto the duel row at creation so both players see the same board even if admin changes the active one mid-duel), **📅 Daily** (every player playing today sees the board — same for everyone, so the daily leaderboard stays fair). Contest + challenge are listed but not wired yet (next round). New `applies_to TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT ARRAY['dynamic']::TEXT[]` column on [schema.sql](schema.sql) (idempotent ALTER — existing rows get `['dynamic']` automatically). New server helper `getActiveBoardForMode(mode)` + `sanitizeAppliesTo(raw)` + new public endpoint `GET /api/active-board/:mode` with per-mode 60s cache (invalidated on any admin write). Duel creation in [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/duels` now snapshots `board_multipliers` + `board_name` onto the `duels` row at creation time — pattern mirrors the existing `difficulty_*` snapshot. New admin UI section in the modal "🎯 חל על מצבי משחק" with 4 checkboxes; the daily one is wrapped in a pink-tinted warning box and triggers an explicit `confirm()` on save (it's the only mode that touches a shared leaderboard, so the admin must opt-in twice). Client integration: top of `init()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) clears any stale multiplier, then each mode branch resolves its board (`fetchBoardForMode('daily')` for daily, same for practice, snapshot read for duel, restoration from `window._activeDynamicBoard` for dynamic). [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `startDuelGame` reads `board_multipliers` from the duel row and applies it before the first render. The fairness guard in 11-game.js leaderboard-submit branch was extended: `practiceFairForLeaderboard = (mode==='practice') && !sessionDifficulty && !window._duelMode && !window._activeSpecialBoard` — so practice with an active board never pollutes the global default leaderboard. The pill bar in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) lost its `mode === 'dynamic'` gate — now renders for any mode whenever a multiplier is active. New `showSpecialBoardToast()` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) fires at every game start when `window._activeSpecialBoard` is set — gradient pink-orange slide-in pill at the top of the viewport with the board name + multiplier preview, dedup'd per board id so a quick replay doesn't spam, auto-dismisses after 3.2s or on tap. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). The admin board list now shows per-mode badges (🎯 דינמי / ⚡ פרקטיס / ⚔️ דו-קרב / 📅 דיילי) on every row so the admin sees at a glance where each board kicks in. Cache buster `v20260522g`, SW `bloom-v5.7`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,991 drops / 8,861 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 2 redesigned to opt-in mode (May 2026)** — initial phase-2 build (commit 825095c) auto-applied any admin-activated board to every player on boot, which polluted the daily / contest / duel / challenge / default-practice experience the user already knew. After user feedback ("זה ממש לא טוב … ולא לפגוע בלוח שהוא כבר מכיר") the model was flipped to **opt-in**: the admin still creates and schedules boards (`board_configurations` table unchanged), but the **client never auto-applies anything**. Instead, the home screen ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)) shows a dedicated "🎯 לוחות דינמיים" entry — but only when at least one board is currently in its schedule window. Tapping it opens a picker modal in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) (new file) that lists every available board as a card with type icon + name + multiplier preview ("🎯 מכפילי עמודות · ×6 · ×4 · ×2 · ×1"). Selecting a board calls `setColumnMultipliers(board.definition.multipliers)` and `init('dynamic', {fresh: true})` — a new game mode added in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) that is practice-like (random seed, unlimited replays) but **never submits to any leaderboard** (`daily_scores`, `difficulty_scores`, `contest_scores`) — the existing fair-leaderboard guard already excludes anything that isn't `mode === 'daily'` or a default-difficulty practice. Going home, or starting any other mode, calls `clearDynamicBoardSession()` so the next vanilla game has no leftover multiplier. The pill bar (`.col-mult-bar` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)) is now gated by `mode === 'dynamic'` AND mounted as a sibling between `#tier-bar` and `#grid-wrap` (no longer inside `#grid-wrap`'s flex flow), with `style.width` set in JS to match `gridEl.style.width` so the pills line up exactly with the columns below. Server gets a new `GET /api/boards/available` endpoint returning the full list (the old `/api/active-board` single-row endpoint stays for back-compat). Admin copy updated to "לוחות זמינים לבחירה" (available for selection) instead of the old "פעיל לשחקנים" (active for all players). Cache buster `v20260522d`, SW `bloom-v5.4`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 1: Column score multipliers (May 2026)** — first foundation of the Dynamic Boards System (see [BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md](BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md)). Behind the existing `getBoardRows()`/`getBoardCols()` abstractions, new `getColumnMultipliers()` / `setColumnMultipliers(arr)` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) — default `null` (no-op). `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) now takes the survivor column and multiplies the base by `mults[col]` when active; when null it returns the vanilla score with zero overhead (validated by `scripts/test_engine.mjs` — 0 regressions across 200 games / 13,966 drops / 8,905 merges). Single caller in `processChains()` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) passes `kc` (survivor column, not drop column — chain reactions can move across columns, and rewarding the *survivor* keeps the strategic choice honest). UI: `.col-mult-bar` pills above the grid show `×6`/`×4`/`×2`/`×1` with tiered visuals — gradient-pink + glow for ×6, gold pulse for ×4, mint for ×2, dimmed for ×1; built in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) using design tokens (`--color-warning`, `--color-success`, `--shadow-glow`). A floating "×N עמודה!" badge fires next to the merge cell on ≥2× landings — gold-to-pink gradient pill, 1.1s lifetime. Activatable today via devtools console: `__bloomDebug.setColumnMultipliers([6,4,2,1]); __bloomDebug.restart();` — admin UI lands in Phase 2. Cache buster `v20260522a`, SW `bloom-v5.2`.
