Active tier is scaled up with a colored glow ring and its score un-fades to the tile color. After each drop a silent left-to-right sweep cycles through tiers 1-4 (`revealNextTier`) and settles on the chosen piece, teaching the ladder order through repetition.
- ✅ **Live contest leaderboard** — while a contest game is in progress, the active player's score updates onto every other contestant's leaderboard view as a pulsing green pill, 1×/sec via `pushLiveScore`. The pill is shown *in addition to* the accumulated total so the rank ordering reflects the projected end-of-game score.
- ✅ **Live spectator mode** — players can watch any other contestant who's currently mid-game. Two entry points: (a) post-game from the game-over modal, (b) **mid-game** from the contest leaderboard screen (`showContestLeaderboard`) — every row with `liveScore !== null` is `spectatable` (role=button, data-spectate-target/data-spectate-name), wired via a delegated handler on `#clb-board`. A top-level "צפה במשחק חי (N)" button shows when at least one live row is rendered. Mid-game entry calls `saveContestGameState()` then `stopLivePush()`, and on exit (`init('contest')`) resumes from the saved state. Watched grid + score + next-piece refreshes every 1s via `GET /api/contests/:code/live-state/:targetDeviceId`. Watching is cost-aware: the active player only POSTs grid frames (`/live-state`) when the server confirmed they have at least one watcher (`hasWatchers` in `/live-score` response). The spectator's `/watch` heartbeat (every 5s) carries either `lastFinalScore` or — when paused mid-game — their *current* in-progress score, so the watched player sees an honest "this watcher reached X" value.
- ✅ **Audience awareness** — the active player sees a floating "👁 N" badge over the board with the watcher count. Tap to expand a list of each watcher's name + last-completed-game score. Watcher heartbeat is 5s; TTL on the server is 10s, so closing a tab disappears the watcher from the badge within ≤15s without any explicit teardown.
- ✅ **Admin dashboard** at `admin/index.html` — gated behind `ADMIN_PATH` (URL slug) **and** `ADMIN_PASSWORD` (HTTP Basic Auth). Includes DAU/WAU/MAU/D1 KPIs vs 2026 hybrid-casual benchmarks (40/20/7), 30-day DAU sparkline, 7-day funnel (visited → played → completed → returned-next-day), weekly cohort retention table (D1/D7/D30 per cohort), time-of-day heatmap (7×24, Asia/Jerusalem), top-scores with z-score outlier flagging (threshold > 3σ), contest management (PATCH endsAt/status/name, DELETE), paginated player list with drill-down + cascading delete, "what's happening right now" live view (from `contest_live_state` + `contest_watchers` filtered to 30s), audit log (`admin_actions` table), CSV export with UTF-8 BOM for every table. Reuses existing `cleanContestName`, `isValidDate`, and the rate-limit helper from server.js.
- ✅ **Visit tracking** — `/api/ping` upserts `device_visits` rows on each page boot. Lightweight (~1 row/device/day), enables bounce-rate and accurate retention denominators.
- ✅ **Demo seeder** (`scripts/seed_demo.js`) — populates 30 players × 30 days × 5 contests for screenshots/load-testing. Scoped to `device_id LIKE 'demo-%'` and contest codes `D…DEMO`. Refuses to run if >1000 non-demo `daily_scores` rows exist unless `--force`. npm scripts: `seed:demo`, `seed:reset`, `seed:clean`.
- ✅ **UX Polish + Addiction Maximizer — stage 39 (May 2026)** — comprehensive polish round after 38 stages. The home had 156 infinite animations on one page = visual chaos that diluted focus. Three coordinated fixes:
  1. **Priority Calmer** ([src/80-polish.js](src/80-polish.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE, loads after all other 30s before 99-close). `TILE_PRIORITIES` array ranks every home tile by addiction priority: streak-danger=100 / pet-crying=95 / trophy-milestone=90 / guild-war-reward=88 / league-reward=86 / BP-claim=84 / ach-claim=82 / album-claim=80 / prestige-ready=78 / spin-available=70 / daily-deal=65 / starter-pack=60 / bundle=55 / pet-sad=50 / checklist=40 / guild-war-active=38 / rival-active=35 / passive tiles=4-25. `applyPriorityCalmer()` runs after `applyHomeVariant()` (monkey-patched into the existing window function), finds all matching tiles, picks the highest-priority winner, applies `.polish-spotlight` to it (gold-pink animated halo via `::before` pseudo-element) and `.polish-calmed` to everything else (animation-play-state:paused, filter:saturate(0.75) brightness(0.94), opacity:0.88). Re-runs at 800ms / 2200ms / 3500ms / 5000ms to catch tiles that mount late.
  2. **First-visit Micro-tutorials** — `TUTORIAL_TEXT` dict maps tile IDs to 1-sentence Hebrew explanations (e.g. spin → "🎡 גלגל יומי חינם — סובב פעם ביום וזכה בפרס משתנה"). `showMicroTooltip()` mounts a gold gradient balloon next to the tile with auto-positioning (flips below if too close to top, clamps horizontally). Per-tile dedup via `localStorage[bloom_tile_seen_v1]`. **Only ONE tooltip at a time** to avoid overload. Auto-dismisses after 8s or on "הבנתי ✓" click. Re-show via `window.__bloomPolish.resetTutorials()`.
  3. **Unified loading spinner** — `MutationObserver` watches body for new DOM, finds any element with text "⏳ טוען..." and replaces with `.polish-spinner` (36px gold-border spinning circle). Consistent loading state across all 14 modals built across stages.
  4. **Admin Engagement Overview** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)) — new section at TOP of 📊 דשבורד tab with `.engagement-grid` of cards. Each card shows: icon + system name + stat number + status badge (✓ פעיל / ⏰ צריך טיפול / ⏸ אין שחקנים) + auto-jump-to-section on click (switches tab + scrolls). Currently 4 systems: Trophy Road / Spin Wheel / Guild Wars / Rivalries — extensible. Fetches all 4 stats endpoints in parallel via `Promise.all`. Solves "where is X feature in admin?" pain after 38 stages spread the addiction stack across 6 tabs.
  Cache buster `v20260523ad`, SW `bloom-v11.4`.
- ✅ **Trophy Road — stage 38 — Clash Royale pattern (May 2026)** — the #1 retention mechanism in mobile games. Unlike League/Battle Pass, **trophies can GO DOWN** if you play poorly — the fear of losing is the strongest dopamine driver. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_trophies` (device_id PK, trophies, trophies_lifetime, highest_trophies, current_arena_id, claimed_milestones JSONB, total_games, total_wins, last_change, last_change_at), `trophy_history` (BIGSERIAL audit log). 11 master config keys + 10 milestone pairs (`trophies_milestone_N_at` + `_gems`). Defaults: win (≥500 score) = +15🏆, lose (<100) = −8🏆, crown bonus +40🏆, personal-best bonus +25🏆. New-player protection: under 50 trophies = no loss. Safe floor 0. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 8 visual arenas hardcoded in `TROPHY_ARENAS` (🌱 sprout/0 → 🌳 forest/50 → 🏘 village/200 → 🏰 castle/600 → 🌋 volcano/1500 → ❄️ ice/3000 → 🌌 galaxy/6000 → ⚡ legend/12000). `_calcTrophyChange(opts, cfg)` is the pure calc — score+tier+isNewBest+currentTrophies → `{delta, breakdown}`. `_trophyGrantFromGame(deviceId, opts, cfg)` is the atomic transaction — row-lock, calc, UPDATE state, INSERT history, set per-game dedup key `_trophy:<deviceId>:<gameId>`. 3 endpoints: `GET /api/trophies/state` (returns trophies + arena + nextArena + milestones with claimed/ready flags + stats), `POST /api/trophies/grant-from-game` (rate-limited 200/hr, called from client game-over with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId), `POST /api/trophies/claim-milestone` (atomic claim with row-lock + JSONB array append + balance credit). **Client** ([src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **dark-blue→gold gradient** showing current trophies + arena + next-arena hint, gold-pulsing when milestone unclaimed. **Game-over hook** wired into [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) right after Stage 27 guild-contribute — `grantTrophiesForGame()` fires fire-and-forget with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId, skipped for bots/skin-trials. **Toasts**: green `+15🏆` fly-in (up arrow + count) for wins, red `−8🏆` for losses, plays soft tones + scaled buzz. **Arena promotion**: 1.4s after trophy toast, full-screen radial overlay with arena emoji spinning + "קודמת לארנה חדשה! · ארנת [name]" + 5-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Modal: big arena header with breathing emoji + trophy count + last-change pill (green/red), next-arena progress bar, 3-stat row (highest/games/winrate), 10-milestone list (locked = greyed with "🔒 N🏆 needed", ready = gold-pulsing with "🎁 קבל +N💎" button, claimed = mint), full arena ladder visualization. Integrated into Stage 35 home variants: 3rd-priority hot card in Carousel + Hero candidate when milestone unclaimed. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🏆 Trophy Road` section in 💰 כלכלה tab — 4-stat overview (active players, max, avg, total games) + top-30 leaderboard with 🥇🥈🥉 medals + win%. New `GET /admin/api/trophies/stats` endpoint. Cache buster `v20260523ac`, SW `bloom-v11.3`.
- ✅ **Guild Wars — stage 37 — clan-vs-clan competition (May 2026)** — Clash Royale pattern that boosted Supercell's guild retention 3-5x at launch. Auto-matched weekly competition between two guilds. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `guild_wars` (BIGSERIAL + 2 FK to guilds + window + 2 scores + 2 game counts + status + winner_guild_id + finalized_at), `guild_war_contributions` (PK on war+device, per-member score + games count), `guild_war_claims` (PK on war+device, atomic dedup). 6 config keys: enabled / duration_days=7 / min_members_active=3 / winner_reward_per_member=500 / loser_reward_per_member=100 / min_games_to_claim=1. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_runGuildWarMatchmaker()` runs every 6h — finds eligible guilds (3+ members, no active war), sorts by total_score_alltime, pairs adjacent (power-balanced), inserts war rows with NOW + 7 days. `_maybeContributeToWar(guildId, deviceId, score, client)` is called INSIDE the existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction (zero client wiring — automatic for every guild member's game-over scan-for-crowns hook). Atomic UPDATE both `guild_wars.guild_X_score/games` + UPSERT into `guild_war_contributions`. `_finalizeGuildWar(warId)` is idempotent — picks winner by score (tie → no winner), flips status, fires push notifications to all contributing members (best-effort `setImmediate`). `GET /api/guilds/war` returns active war + my contribution + top 10 contributors + unclaimed reward; also lazy-finalizes any expired wars for the player's guild on read. `POST /api/guilds/war/claim` atomic transaction: row-lock contribution → verify eligibility (min games + winner status) → INSERT-or-fail claim → balance credit. Admin: `GET /admin/api/guild-wars` lists 100 most recent (active first), `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/match-now` triggers immediate matchmaker, `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/:id/finalize` force-ends early with audit log. **Client** ([src/33-guild-wars.js](src/33-guild-wars.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gradient** (gold when unclaimed reward exists) — only mounts when in-guild + has active war OR unclaimed reward. Tile shows status text dynamically ("👑 מובילים ב-N נקודות" / "🔥 מאחור ב-N — קדימה!" / "⚔️ המלחמה החלה!" / "🏆 נצחון!" when claim ready). Modal: optional reward card at top (gold-gradient for winners, silver for losers, with claim button → atomic claim → full-screen celebration with 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7) for wins). Active war card: countdown, VS row with both guild emojis + names + scores + game counts, dual-color progress bar (green vs red), my-contribution highlight, top-10 contributors with 🥇🥈🥉 medals + names + scores. Tips footer explaining mechanic. Integrated into Stage 35 home variants: 2nd-priority card in Carousel (gold when unclaimed) + #2 hero candidate in Hero variant (after spin wheel). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 🛡⚔️ Guild Wars section in 💰 כלכלה tab — 6 config keys + "🔄 Match Now" button + scrollable wars list with status badges (⚔️ active / ✓ finalized) + winner + per-guild scores + "💰 Finalize Now" action per active war. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with Clash-Royale-pattern rationale + economic-math. Cache buster `v20260523ab`, SW `bloom-v11.2`.
- ✅ **Daily Spin Wheel — stage 36 — Coin Master pattern (May 2026)** — single most addictive daily-return mechanic in F2P puzzles ($1B/year industry). One spin per device per day. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_spin_state` (device_id PK, last_spin_date, current_streak, longest_streak, total_spins, total_gems_won, last_reward JSONB). 4 master config keys + 12 segment definitions (each = 6 keys: label, emoji, type, amount, weight, color). Default 12 segments: 10💎(w25) / 25💎(w20) / 50💎(w15) / 5BP(w12) / 100💎(w8) / 🛡freeze(w5) / 20BP(w6) / 🎁chest(w4) / 200💎(w3) / 500💎(w1.5) / 1000💎(w0.4) / 🏆JACKPOT 5000💎(w0.1). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/spin/state` returns canSpin + streak + last reward + 12 segments + bonus config. `POST /api/spin/today` is the atomic transaction: row-lock state, server-rolls weighted segment, applies streak bonus to gem rewards (+10%/day cap +200%), grants per reward type (gems → balance UPDATE, bp_xp → player_season_progress UPSERT, freeze → client-counter, chest → gem-equivalent), updates state with new streak (yesterday → +1, else → 1). All inside BEGIN/COMMIT. **Client** ([src/32-daily-spin.js](src/32-daily-spin.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gold gradient** (Coin Master vibe) with `🎡` icon that auto-tilts every 4s, breathing pulse when canSpin. Click → modal with: streak card (when streak ≥ 1) showing 🔥 + bonus%, **SVG wheel** (12 colored segments + emoji + label per segment + pointer at top + spinning gold center), spin button. **Animation choreography**: click → `_spinning = true` → POST → on response, calculate target rotation = `-(idx + 0.5) × 30° - 5 × 360°` (5 full turns + decel to target) → CSS transition with `cubic-bezier(0.17, 0.67, 0.21, 0.99)` over 4.2s → tick sounds at 300ms intervals during spin → reveal overlay with reward card. **4-tier reward card**: `small` (<100) / `big` (100-499) / `huge` (500-999) / `jackpot` (5000+). Jackpot card has continuous gold-glow animation + 32-particle confetti burst + 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Each tier gets scaled confetti count + scaled buzz pattern. Streak bonus rendered as red-orange "🔥 +N%" pill. **Integrated into Stage 35 home variants**: top-priority card in Carousel + #1 candidate signal in Hero (when canSpin). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): `🎡 גלגל יומי / Spin Wheel` section in 💰 כלכלה tab with 4-stat overview (total spins / 7-day active / total gems / longest streak). 12 segment definitions editable via the generic "כל ההגדרות" config table. New `GET /admin/api/spin/stats` endpoint. Cache buster `v20260523aa`, SW `bloom-v11.1`.
- ✅ **Home Variants A/B — stage 35 — 4 home layouts pickable from admin (May 2026)** — solves the home-screen overload problem (the v2 home grew to 14+ tiles after stages 17-34, classic mobile cognitive-load territory). Admin picks ONE layout globally via `game_config.home_variant`. **Architecture**: pure decorator pattern in [src/31-home-variants.js](src/31-home-variants.js) (NEW FILE in own IIFE) — `applyHomeVariant()` is called at the end of `showHomeV2()` after a 3.4s delay (waits for all `maybeShow*Tile` deferred mounts to settle), then re-arranges DOM based on variant. Every tile's own logic stays untouched — variants only hide / move / wrap. **4 variants**: (1) 📺 **standard** — no-op, current v2 behavior; (2) 🎠 **carousel** — adds a horizontally-scrolling "🔥 חם עכשיו" row at the top with 3-6 cards derived from active tiles (Battle Pass claim ready / league reward / pet crying / daily deal / etc.), each card clicks through to the underlying tile via a stable selector → `el.click()` map. `.hvar-carousel-card.hot` has a 2s pulse animation for time-critical cards; (3) 🎯 **hero** — replaces the hero with a MASSIVE single-action card (60% viewport) showing the highest-emotion signal RIGHT NOW (priority: league reward → BP claim → sad pet → daily deal → bundle → boards → rival), with a giant black "🎁 לאסוף" CTA that re-fires the underlying tile's click. All other secondary tiles collapse into a `📂 עוד N פיצ׳רים` expander above the bottom links. Four hero theme classes: `hero-reward` (gold), `hero-urgent` (red, pulses), `hero-hot` (pink), `hero-neutral` (default orange); (4) 🎓 **jit** — Just-In-Time progressive disclosure. New players see only base CTA + pet. Tiles unlock in 5 waves based on `loadGamesPlayed()` against admin-configurable thresholds (`home_jit_unlock_games`, default `3,7,13,26`). When a tile is shown for the FIRST time, it gets a `🎉 חדש!` floating badge + `hvarJitUnlock` 1.4s scale-pop animation + `soundMilestone(4)` + buzz + scrollIntoView (staggered 1.4s apart). Per-tile first-show dedup via `localStorage[bloom_jit_seen_v1]`. Bottom-of-home teaser banner "עוד **N משחקים** לפתיחת..." with next-wave-content preview labels (e.g. wave 4 = "⚔️ ליגה / יריבות / הישגים") — the prospective-FOMO punch. **Server** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 2 new config keys (`home_variant` default `'standard'`, `home_jit_unlock_games` default `'3,7,13,26'`). No new endpoints — uses existing `/api/config` public endpoint (returns flat dict `{key: value}` so client reads `gameConfig.home_variant` directly). Admin PATCH `/api/config/home_variant` busts `_configCache` so changes propagate within seconds. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): new "🏠 גירסת מסך הבית" section at TOP of 🎮 משחק tab (above existing config) with a 2x2 grid of variant buttons (active variant gets mint-green gradient + "✓ פעיל" badge), plus a JIT-thresholds input with format validation (4 comma-separated numbers). Rich Hebrew tooltips on every variant explaining trade-offs + addiction rationale. **CSS** ([public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)) appended ~150 lines covering all 3 non-standard variants with full dark-theme overrides. Body marker `data-home-variant="X"` lets CSS toggle base presentation per variant. Cache buster `v20260523z`, SW `bloom-v11.0`.
- ✅ **Weekly Leagues — stage 34 — 5-tier weekly ladder (May 2026)** — Brawl Stars pattern. Adds week-over-week competitive structure absent from all the other stages. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_weekly_xp` table (device_id + week_start PK, xp_at_week_start snapshot, best_league_seen, reward_claimed). 10 config keys: enabled + 4 tier thresholds (500/2K/10K/50K) + 5 reward gems (50/150/400/1000/3000). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_currentWeekStartISO()` returns Sunday in Asia/Jerusalem. `_leagueForGain(gain, cfg)` maps weekly XP gain → tier object {id, emoji, label, color}. `_nextLeagueThreshold` returns gap to next tier. `GET /api/league/state`: lazy-inserts snapshot if first call this week (xp_at_week_start = current XP, so this week's gain starts at 0), computes weekly_gain + league + progress + unclaimedReward from LAST week's row. Updates `best_league_seen` if upgraded mid-week. `POST /api/league/claim`: atomic — checks last week's reward_claimed, marks claimed, credits gems based on best_league_seen tier. **Client** ([src/30-leagues.js](src/30-leagues.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in deep purple-indigo (boxing/championship vibe), color-themed badge per league, gold reward pill when unclaimed. Modal: huge gradient league card (color matches tier) + emoji + label + weekly XP, next-tier progress card, unclaimed-reward card with claim button, full 5-tier ladder showing all rewards + thresholds + "אתה כאן" highlight. **Promotion celebration**: full-screen radial overlay with tier emoji + "קודמת לליגה!" + 7-pulse buzz. Fires automatically on `/state` fetch when `leveledUp=true`. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): ⚔️ Weekly Leagues section with 10 config keys + tooltips explaining tier economics ($-equivalents of weekly Master rewards). - ✅ **Rivalry System — stage 33 — auto-paired 24h personal competition (May 2026)** — the Clash Royale pattern. Personal beats abstract: when a player sees a specific named opponent with a specific delta and a 24h deadline, engagement spikes far above what a generic leaderboard does. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_rivalries` BIGSERIAL table (device_id + rival_device_id + xp snapshots at decl + expires_at + resolved + outcome). 3 config keys: enabled / threshold_pct=10 / duration_hours=24 + reward=150💎. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_runRivalryMatchmaker()` runs every 4 hours — pulls 200 recently-active candidates sorted by best score, pairs adjacent ones if delta < threshold%, creates reciprocal rivalries (both sides see each other). Cap 50 pairs per scan. `GET /api/rival/state` returns my active rivalry + fresh lifetime XP for both (re-uses stage 30's `_computeLifetimeXp`) + countdown. `POST /api/rival/resolve` checks expired or proactively-overtaken rivalries — atomic transaction grants 150💎 to winner, marks resolved. Admin: `/api/rivalries/stats` (active/wins/losses/ties breakdown) + manual `match-now` trigger. **Client** ([src/29-rivals.js](src/29-rivals.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): boot calls `/resolve` first (catches any expired/won rivalries → fires win celebration with +150💎 banner), then `/state` for the active one. Home tile in red (boxing-glove theme) with pulsing red border when behind, gold theme when ahead, "חדש!" badge on first view. Live 60s countdown ticker. Modal: big VS card (me vs them with XP numbers + gain-since-decl), big status banner ("👑 אתה לפני!" / "🔥 320 מאחור — אפשר לעקוף!"), countdown row, reward card, tips list ("איך מצברים XP חיים מהר?"). **Win celebration**: full-screen radial-burst overlay with 🏆 spinning icon + "+150💎" + 5-pulse buzz. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated 🥊 section with 4 config keys + 5-stat overview + 30 recent rivalries + "🔄 צור זיווגים עכשיו" manual trigger. 4 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries explaining the matchmaking + reward economy. Cache buster `v20260523x`, SW `bloom-v10.8`.
- ✅ **Guilds / Clans — stage 27 — peer-pressure retention (May 2026)** — the biggest retention mechanic in modern mobile games. Industry data: +35% D30 retention, 3.4× sessions/day vs solo players. **v1 scope** intentionally tight: create/join/leave + daily collective goal + per-member reward claim + leaderboard. **Skipped to v2**: real-time chat, clan-vs-clan wars, league tiers. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 4 tables — `guilds` (id, code 6-char UNIQUE, name, emoji, creator, member_count, total_score_alltime, max_members), `guild_members` (PK on guild+device, role, joined_at, score+crowns contrib counters), `guild_daily_progress` (PK on guild+date, goal_target/progress, is_complete flag), `guild_member_claims` (PK on guild+device+date for atomic dedup). 5 config keys: enabled / create_cost=500💎 / max_members=30 / daily_goal=30 crowns / reward_per_member=200💎. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 7 endpoints. `POST /guilds/create`: atomic gem-deduct + insert guild + insert creator as leader. `POST /guilds/join`: anti-cheat checks (already in guild, guild full) + atomic insert + member_count bump. `POST /guilds/leave`: deletes member; if last out → deletes guild; if leader left → promotes oldest member. `GET /guilds/mine`: returns guild + members (sorted by contribution) + today's progress + my claim status. `POST /guilds/contribute`: atomic — bumps member counters + daily progress + checks if goal just completed (returns `justCompleted=true`). `POST /guilds/claim-daily`: server-side eligibility re-check + atomic UNIQUE-guarded claim + balance credit. `GET /guilds/leaderboard`: top-N by all-time total score. Admin: list + force-delete. **Client** ([src/28-guilds.js](src/28-guilds.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **royal blue + gold** (distinct from all other tiles). When not in a guild: "🛡 הצטרף לקלאן · מטרה משותפת + פרסים יומיים" CTA. When in a guild: emoji + name + member count + progress bar + claim badge. Pulses gold when canClaim. **Join/Create modal**: two sections — top input for join-by-code (auto-uppercases + monospace), bottom for create with name/emoji/description fields. **Guild modal** (when in guild): dark royal-blue header with emoji + name + share code + stats, goal card with progress bar + claim button, member list sorted by contribution with 🥇🥈🥉 medals + role badges (👑 leader / ⭐ officer) + "(אתה)" highlight + contribution numbers, footer with 📤 share code + 🚪 leave. **Game-over hook** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): after pet XP grant, scans the final grid for tier-8 (crown) cells and calls `contributeToGuild(score, crowns)` — server validates membership. **Toasts**: contribution shows "🛡 +N לקלאן · 18/30", goal-complete shows huge celebratory gold "🎉 הקלאן השלים את היעד היומי!". **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): `🛡 קלאנים / Guilds` section with 5 config keys + top-50 guilds list with medals + member counts + completion days + 🗑 force-delete. 5 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with peer-pressure psychology rationale. Cache buster `v20260523w`, SW `bloom-v10.7`.

Pre-filled text uses `{score}`/`{tier}`/`{url}` placeholders with "נסה לשבור אותי" challenge psychology. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `replay_shares` (BIGSERIAL log table) + 5 config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/replay/config` (lightweight, public — returns threshold + share text template), `POST /api/replay/track-share` (rate-limited 30/hr, validates `shared_via` against allowlist). Admin: `GET /admin/api/replay/stats` returns overall counts + breakdown by channel + top-20 sharers (30d). **Client** ([src/27-replay.js](src/27-replay.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): `shouldOfferReplayShare(score)` gate, `renderShareCard(opts)` builds the 720×1280 canvas. - ✅ **Smart Notifications — stage 31 — auto-personalized push scheduler (May 2026)** — server-side scheduler that scans subscribed devices every 30 min, picks the highest-emotional signal per device, sends ONE personalized push. Differs from Stage 10 (admin broadcast): this is fully automatic + per-device. Both still work. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_push_state` (device_id PK, last_sent_at, last_send_reason, total_sent, last_scan_at). 6 config keys for cooldown/scan-interval/allowed-hours/batch-size. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_pickSmartPushFor(deviceId, cfg)` runs 8 parallel queries (each wrapped in catch to tolerate missing tables) and computes the highest-priority signal: **(1) Pet crying 😢** (>48h since visit — guilt mechanic, highest emotion); **(2) Tournament ending 🏆** (within 3h); **(3) Friend played today, you didn't 👥** (FOMO + social); **(4) Streak danger 🔥** (last play was yesterday); **(5) BP unclaimed 🎖** (≥5 rewards waiting); **(6) Comeback 👋** (3-30 days away); **(7) Daily Special 🌟** (after 14:00 if not played today). All messages personalized with player name + specifics. `_runSmartPushScan()` is the scheduler loop — runs every `smart_push_scan_minutes` (30 default) ONLY during 9:00-22:00 Asia/Jerusalem hours. Per-device cooldown 12h. Marks `last_scan_at` even when no push sent so we spread load. `_startSmartPushScheduler()` fires after 60s boot delay. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): new `🤖 התראות חכמות אוטומטיות` section with 6 config keys + live stats (subscribers, sent in 24h/7d, total ever, reason breakdown by category) + "🔄 סרוק עכשיו" manual trigger + recent-30-sends table with emoji-coded reasons. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Public `GET /api/smart-push/preview` shows what would be sent for any device (debug). Cache buster `v20260523u`, SW `bloom-v10.5`.
- ✅ **Lifetime Progression — stage 30 — Call of Duty Prestige (May 2026)** — the longest meta-arc in the game. NEVER resets between seasons. Up to 10 ⭐ stars on profile = permanent prestige badge. **Architecture insight**: XP is **computed server-side** from aggregate of existing player activity — no new XP grants, no schema migrations of existing tables. Existing players are rewarded retroactively for accumulated history. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_lifetime_state` (device_id PK, cached_xp, prestige_count 0-10, last_prestige_at, cosmetic_unlocks JSONB, current_title). 4 config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_computeLifetimeXp(deviceId)` aggregates from 8 sources via parallel queries (each wrapped in catch so missing tables don't break the calc): daily/difficulty/dynamic-board scores ×10, achievements ×75, total_earned÷2, album cells ×25, gacha pulls ×5, pet level ×50, season XP-derived tier ×100, friendships ×200. `GET /api/lifetime/state` returns `{level, prestigeCount, xpThisRun, xpToNext, title, canPrestige, prestigeReward}`. `_lifetimeTitleForLevel(level, prestige)` maps to Hebrew titles ("🌱 מתחיל" → "🌟 אגדה אינסופית"). `POST /api/lifetime/prestige` is the atomic claim: re-verifies eligibility (level≥100), bumps prestige_count, credits 5000💎 reward. **Client** ([src/26-lifetime.js](src/26-lifetime.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **dark purple-gold** to stand apart from other tiles (royal/premium vibe). Shows ⭐⭐⭐ stars + level + title + progress bar. When can-prestige: tile pulses gold with shadow. Modal: 3-column header (stars / huge level number / title), big progress bar, **XP sources breakdown** ("how do I earn XP?") explaining all 8 sources, prestige card. Prestige action: confirm() → atomic POST → **full-screen celebration** with stars + sparkle (yellow-red gradient card, 7-pulse buzz). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `⭐ פרוגרס חיים / Prestige` section + 4 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries explaining the aggregate formula. Cache buster `v20260523t`, SW `bloom-v10.4`.
- ✅ **Tile Collection Album — stage 29 — Genshin-style completionism (May 2026)** — visual album with 8 tiers × N dynamic boards. Returns `unclaimedBoardCount + unclaimedTierCount` for the home badge. `POST /api/album/claim` is the atomic transaction with server-side eligibility re-verification + balance credit + UNIQUE-guarded claim insert. **Client** ([src/25-album.js](src/25-album.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): hooked into the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) — fires `recordAlbumProgress(boardId, highestTier)` after every game. Album modal: header with 3 stats (collected/% complete/🎁 to claim), tier-complete rows at top with mini progress bars + claim buttons, then per-board list with name + claim button + 8-cell grid (indigo when collected, greyed when locked). All claim actions atomic with sound + buzz + balance update + cache invalidation. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `📔 אלבום אריחים` section with 4 config keys (enabled, show_on_home, reward_per_board, reward_per_tier) + 4 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. - ✅ **Achievement-driven Cross-Leaderboard — stage 16 — new competitive axis (May 2026)** — global ranking by NUMBER of achievements unlocked (not score). Rewards completionists / breadth-players over single-board grinders. Until this stage, achievements lived only in `localStorage[bloom_dyn_achievements]` — Stage 16 mirrors them server-side. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_achievements` table with `BIGSERIAL id`, `(device_id, achievement_key)` UNIQUE INDEX (handles dedup), recent-unlock and per-device indexes. Achievement keys are opaque strings — client uses `cross:pioneer5`, `board:42:crown`, etc. 2 config keys: `ach_leaderboard_enabled` + `ach_leaderboard_show_on_home`. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `POST /api/achievements/unlock` (idempotent via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING, validates key against `/^[a-z0-9_:-]+$/`). `POST /api/achievements/sync` for bulk-backfill from localStorage (capped at 500 keys per call, 10/hr rate limit). `GET /api/achievements/leaderboard?limit=50` returns top-N players with LEFT JOINs to `player_profiles` for name/country/player_code (fallback to most-recent `daily_scores` name). Includes "me" row + my-rank computation via `COUNT(*) WHERE count > my_count + 1`. `GET /api/achievements/me` for lightweight count + rank lookup. **Client** ([src/24-ach-leaderboard.js](src/24-ach-leaderboard.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): on boot, reads localStorage state and POSTs bulk sync (one-time per session). `grantPerBoard` + `grantCross` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) now also fire `serverUnlockAchievement` (fire-and-forget) so new unlocks are mirrored immediately. **Home tile**: gold-yellow `.ach-lb-home-tile` mounts only for players with 3+ achievements — shows "🏅 לוח מובילים — הישגים #14 / פתחת 17 הישגים". **Modal**: gold-themed with 🏅 icon, my-rank pill at top (when I'm outside top 50), full ranked list with podium colors (🥇/🥈/🥉), country flags, "you" highlight. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🏅 לוח מובילים — הישגים` section with toggles + top-20 player list (read-only) + refresh button. 2 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523r`, SW `bloom-v10.2`.
- ✅ **Limited-time Bundles — stage 25 — themed event packs (May 2026)** — themed multi-day premium bundles for holidays/events (Hanukkah, Valentine, Black Friday). Stronger FOMO than Daily Deals because the window is multi-day (3-30 days) and the design is theme-specific. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `limited_bundles` table (slug UNIQUE, name, description, emoji, theme_color, decoration_emoji, price_gems, original_value for strikethrough, contents JSONB, starts_at, ends_at, max_purchases_per_device, sort_order). `limited_bundle_purchases` (BIGSERIAL — supports max>1 with counted dedup). 2 config keys + 3 seeded bundles (Hanukkah 8-day, Valentine 14-day, Black Friday 3-day starting in 60 days). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/bundles/active` returns enabled bundles in their start-end window + per-device purchase counts so client knows `canBuy`. `POST /api/bundles/buy` is the atomic transaction: re-verifies window (anti-cheat — not trusting client's claim it's active), checks max_purchases_per_device limit, deducts price + grants gems/skin/BP-tiers atomically (reuses gacha/starter pack patterns). Admin: 4 CRUD endpoints INSIDE adminRouter block. **Client** ([src/23-bundles.js](src/23-bundles.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home banners (max 2 shown) themed per `--theme-color` CSS variable — Hanukkah=deep blue, Valentine=pink, Black Friday=charcoal. Banner shows emoji + name + discount badge + price + strikethrough + live countdown ticker (60s refresh). **Modal**: per-bundle gradient with **floating decoration emojis** (8 scattered 🕎/🌹/💸 with stagger animation) — the "this is a special event" vibe. Live countdown (1s tick), explicit scarcity ribbon, content rows, big "🛒 קנה עכשיו · 600💎" button. **Welcome overlay** on purchase: gold celebration card with contents recap. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🎁 חבילות חג` section + bundles list with status badges (🟢 active / ⏳ upcoming / ⌛ ended / ⏸ disabled) + theme-color left border per row + total purchases/revenue stats. **3 one-click presets**: 🕎 חנוכה / 💕 ולנטיין / 🔥 Black Friday — each pre-fills the editor with appropriate emoji/color/decoration/price/contents/dates. Full editor with datetime-local pickers for start/end. 2 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523q`, SW `bloom-v10.1`.
- ✅ **Pet / Mascot — stage 28 — Tamagotchi emotional anchor (May 2026)** — virtual flower pet that grows with the player. The pattern that built a $10B Tamagotchi industry by itself. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_pet` table (device_id PK, pet_name, level, xp, last_visited_at, last_fed_at, last_petted_at + dedup dates, feeds_today counter, total_pet_count, total_fed_count). 8 config keys: `pet_enabled` (default true), `pet_xp_per_game` (15), `pet_xp_per_level` (100), `pet_max_level` (20), `pet_feed_price_gems` (10), `pet_feed_xp_reward` (50), `pet_feeds_per_day_max` (3), `pet_daily_pet_reward_gems` (20). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_petComputeMood` returns one of happy/neutral/sad/crying by hours since last_visited_at (<24/<48/<72/>72). `_petComputeStage` returns one of 4 evolution stages (🌱 sprout 1-5 / 🌿 sapling 6-10 / 🌸 bloom 11-15 / 🌺 king 16-20). 5 endpoints: `GET /pet/state` (lazy-creates row, returns full state including computed mood + stage + xpToNext + daily action eligibility), `POST /pet/name` (one-time name set, 5/hr rate limit), `POST /pet/pet` (atomic daily pet — dedups on `last_petted_date=today`, grants gems), `POST /pet/feed` (atomic feed — checks daily limit + deducts gems + adds XP + updates level), `POST /pet/grant-xp` (called from game-over flow with gameId dedup via game_config key). All transactions atomic. **Client** ([src/22-pet.js](src/22-pet.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home widget shows pet emoji + name + mood + level + action dots (💗/🍽 if available). **Pulses RED with shake animation when pet is sad/crying** — the guilt-trip emotional pressure. Tap → naming overlay (if no name yet) OR full modal. **Naming overlay**: gradient green card with bobbing 🌱, input field, "💗 הצב שם" CTA. **Pet modal**: huge 100px bobbing pet emoji + name + stage + xp progress bar (gradient green→gold) + mood-themed message ("הפרח שלך בוכה ממך!" for crying) + 2 action buttons (💗 daily pet pink-themed / 🍽 feed gold-themed) + stats footer. Pet/feed actions trigger animated heart/sparkle burst from the emoji (6-8 particles flying in circle pattern with stagger). Level-up triggers a slide-down toast at top "🎉 הפרח שלך עלה דרגה!". **XP grant** wired into [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) universal post-game block (NOT mode-specific — every game contributes, so the pet grows from daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges/dynamic equally). Server dedups by gameId so the same game can't grant twice. Pet name skip allowed — naming is a soft prompt, not blocking. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🌱 Pet / Mascot` section under 💰 כלכלה with master toggle + level/XP config + daily actions config. 8 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with addiction-psychology rationale ("guilt mechanic returns players day after day"). Returns events grouped by date. `GET /api/checklist/today` returns 5 to-do items: free gacha pull (if claimed today), play daily special (client overrides via localStorage), daily deal (if bought today), daily quest (via `_earn:` dedup keys), maintain streak (via daily_scores + difficulty_scores + dynamic_board_scores). 4 admin CRUD endpoints inside the adminRouter block. **Client** ([src/21-calendar.js](src/21-calendar.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): **Daily Checklist tile** mounts at top of home (after lives widget) — cyan-teal theme, "📋 משימות היום · 2/5" header, gradient progress bar, 5 clickable items (cyan with circle icon when pending; mint with ✓ when done). - ✅ **Lives / Energy — stage 19 — scarcity-driven engagement (May 2026)** — Candy Crush pattern, **DEFAULT-OFF** (admin opt-in via `lives_enabled='true'`). Limited lives that regen over time + refill via ad/💎/wait. **Scope**: applies ONLY to dynamic boards. Daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges remain unlimited — intentional to protect existing UX. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_lives_state` (current_lives, max_lives, last_regen_at + 3 stat counters). 6 config keys: `lives_enabled` (default 'false'), `lives_max` (5), `lives_regen_minutes` (30), `lives_refill_price_gems` (50), `lives_ad_refill_count` (1), `lives_per_game_dynamic` (1). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_computeLivesNow(deviceId, cfg)` is the lazy-regen calculator — reads current state, applies floor((now - last_regen) / regen_minutes) regen ticks, advances last_regen_at by the consumed ticks, returns clean state with `msUntilNextRegen`. 4 public endpoints: `GET /lives/state`, `POST /lives/consume` (atomic decrement with current_lives >= n guard), `POST /lives/refill-gems` (atomic deduct + reset to max + last_regen_at=NOW), `POST /lives/refill-ad` (per-gameId dedup via game_config key, +N lives). All with rate-limiting. When `lives_enabled='false'`, all endpoints return `{enabled:false, currentLives:999}` so client gates are no-ops. **Client** ([src/20-lives.js](src/20-lives.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): `maybeShowLivesWidget()` mounts a pink-themed hearts widget at the top of home (red breathing if 0 lives). Widget shows: ❤️❤️🤍🤍🤍 hearts, count "2 / 5 חיים", regen countdown ticker "⏰ 14ד 22ש לחיים הבאים". Click → out-of-lives modal with **3 refill paths**: 📺 ad (mint), 💎 gems (gold), ⏰ wait (close). All disabled when full. `ensureLifeForDynamicGame()` is the gate — called from `startDynamicBoard`. Resolves true if life consumed or system disabled, false if no lives → shows modal. Live ticker decrements client-side every 1s for smooth countdown, re-fetches authoritative state when timer hits 0. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `❤️ חיים / Energy` section with **prominent ⚠ RISKY warning banner** at the top + red ribbon next to the section title. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with explicit "A/B test if you enable" warnings. Cache buster `v20260523n`, SW `bloom-v9.8`.
- ✅ **Skin Gacha — stage 18 — variable-reward Skinner box (May 2026)** — the Genshin/Apex pattern that drives $4B/year in F2P cosmetics. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 3 tables — `gacha_pool` (admin-editable pool of rewards: rarity, reward_type, amount, skin_id, weight, is_featured, is_enabled), `player_gacha_state` (per-device pity counter + total pulls + free pull tracking), `gacha_pulls_history` (full audit log). 15 config keys: master toggle, name, prices (single/ten), pity threshold (50), 5 rarity weights summing to 100, free-pull toggle, featured ID + boost %, dup-to-gems %. Seeded with **17 pool entries** covering all rarities and all reward types (gems/skin/bp_tier/chest/freeze). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_gachaResolveOnePull` rolls rarity weighted by config → then picks reward weighted within rarity (with featured-item boost applied). Pity logic forces legendary+ when counter hits threshold. `_gachaGrantReward` handles all 5 reward types: gems credit, skin insert (with **duplicate detection → auto-convert to gems at 50% of skin price**), BP tier XP boost (advances N tiers in Season Pass), chest/freeze converted to gem-equivalent for v1. `_doGachaPull(deviceId, multiplier, isFree)` is the atomic transaction: deduct price → check free-pull dedup → resolve N pulls → grant N rewards → log history → update state. All in one BEGIN/COMMIT. 3 public endpoints (state, pull, history) + 4 admin CRUD endpoints (placed correctly inside the `if (ADMIN_PATH && ADMIN_PASSWORD)` block — fixed the bug from stage 21). **Client** ([src/19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js) — NEW FILE in own IIFE): home banner purple-cosmic gradient distinct from gold (BP/Starter) and red (Daily Deals). Modal shows: spinning 🎰 icon, pity card with progress bar + "🔥 עוד 7 לאגדי מובטח!" hint, 5-rarity rate breakdown grid color-coded per rarity, featured-banner if any, 3 pull buttons (free/single/10x with "חסכת 10%" badge), history link. **Animated reveal sequence**: click → dark cosmic overlay with spinning glowing orb (1.4s build-up with rolling text) → card pop-in animation per result (scale 0.3 → 1.08 → 1 with rotation easeOutBack), rarity-themed border + glow + emoji + name + pity/featured/dup badges, sound + buzz scaled to rarity (mythic = 7-pulse buzz). 10-pull = 10 cards revealed in sequence with counter + skip-to-summary button. Summary aggregates: per-rarity counts + total gems/skins/BP-tiers won + "שוב!" button that reopens the modal for chain pulling. History modal shows last 50 pulls with rarity-coded left-border + emoji + name + badges + timestamp. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🎰 Skin Gacha` section under 💰 כלכלה with 4 logical groups (master toggles, prices, rarity weights, featured), full pool list with status pills + content summary + total-pulled-count, edit-modal with rarity/reward_type dropdowns + emoji/name/weight/enabled fields, ✏️ ערוך + 🗑 delete buttons. 15 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with rich economic-math + addiction-psychology explanations. Cache buster `v20260523m`, SW `bloom-v9.7`.
- ✅ **Daily Deals — stage 21 — rotating daily offer (May 2026)** — one deal rotates daily (Asia/Jerusalem) from an admin-managed pool. Anchoring psychology ("חסכת 60%!") + 24h countdown + one-purchase-per-day-per-deal. **Daily-return hook** — players open the app each morning to see "what's on sale today". **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_deals` table (id, slug, name, description, emoji, price_gems, original_value for strikethrough, contents JSONB, category, is_enabled, sort_order) seeded with **7 starter deals** — `gem_starter` (50💎→200💎), `gem_bundle` (500💎→1200💎), `skin_deal` (200💎→fire skin), `bp_boost` (300💎→1 BP tier), `chest_x3` (150💎→3 chests), `freeze_x3` (300💎→3 streak freezes), `mega_bundle` (800💎→1000💎+space skin+1 BP tier). `daily_deal_purchases` table with PK `(device_id, deal_id, purchase_date)` for per-day-per-deal dedup. 4 master config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_dailyDealHash` FNV-1a hash of today's date → index into enabled deals. `_pickTodaysDeal()` returns the chosen deal + date, honoring `daily_deals_override_id` admin override. `_msUntilNextIsraelMidnight()` for accurate countdown. `GET /api/daily-deals/today?deviceId` returns `{ ok, enabled, date, expiresAt, msLeft, deal: {...with discountPct calculated}, purchased }`. `POST /api/daily-deals/buy` is the atomic transaction: re-verifies dealId IS today's deal (anti-cheat — can't buy yesterday's/tomorrow's), checks not-already-purchased, deducts price with balance guard, grants gems/skin/BP-tiers/etc atomically, inserts purchase record. Returns `{ok, granted: {...}, newBalance}`. 4 admin CRUD endpoints for managing the pool. **Client** ([src/18-daily-deals.js](src/18-daily-deals.js) — NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeShowDailyDealBanner()` fetched on home mount, mounts a red-orange `.daily-deal-home-banner` AFTER the starter-pack banner (so starter takes priority). Banner shows emoji + name + discount-% badge + price + original-price strikethrough + LIVE countdown ticker (updates every 1s). Click → `showDailyDealModal` opens big card with: red `-N%` ribbon, animated icon, content rows per item type (gems/skin/bp/chest/freezes), price-row (big red current + grey strikethrough), buy button. Live countdown in modal too — auto-disables buy button when expired. On buy success: local balance + skin cache + BP status update, `soundMilestone(5)` + buzz, full-screen welcome celebration overlay. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🔥 Daily Deals` section under 💰 כלכלה with master toggles + deals list (status pill + name + emoji + price + content summary + today/total purchase count + ✏️ ערוך + 🗑 delete buttons). Click ✏️ opens a full modal editor with all fields: slug (locked on edit), emoji, name, description, prices, contents grid (5 input fields for gems/skin_id/bp_tiers/chest_count/streak_freezes), category, sort_order, is_enabled toggle. Cache buster `v20260523l`, SW `bloom-v9.6`.
- ✅ **Starter Pack — stage 20 — first-purchase funnel (May 2026)** — the single highest-conversion offer in F2P puzzle games (50-90% buy-through in industry data). Fires ONCE after a player crosses a score threshold (default 5K). 7-day countdown + one-time-only = strong loss-aversion. Pays out 500💎 → 1500💎 + a skin + 3 Battle Pass tier boost (~5× ROI). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): new `starter_pack_state` table — PK on `device_id`, tracks `eligible_at` + `expires_at` + `purchased_at` + `dismissed_count` + `pack_contents` snapshot at purchase. 9 admin config keys (`enabled`, `name`, `price_gems`, `price_usd`, `trigger_score`, `expires_hours`, `reward_gems`, `reward_skin_id`, `reward_bp_tiers`). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/player/starter-pack/status?deviceId&score` — first checks if the row exists (creates on first call), if `eligible_at` is null AND `score >= trigger_score` stamps `eligible_at = NOW()` + `expires_at = NOW() + N hours`. Returns `{available, expiresAt, priceGems, rewardGems, rewardBpTiers, rewardSkinId, name, dismissedCount}`. Short-circuits `{purchased: true}` if already bought. `POST /api/player/starter-pack/buy` is the atomic transaction — server re-verifies eligibility (not trusting client), deducts price from balance with balance-guarded UPDATE, credits reward_gems, INSERTs the skin (idempotent), computes XP boost to push the player up `reward_bp_tiers` tiers in Battle Pass (reads tier thresholds, calculates the gap to `current_tier + N`, upserts the boost), stamps `purchased_at` + snapshots `pack_contents`. All in one transaction — any failure rolls back. Returns `{ok, newBalance, ...rewards}`. `POST /dismiss` increments a counter for telemetry (player keeps closing the banner — admin can see dismiss rate). Rate-limited: status no limit, buy 5/hr, dismiss 30/hr. **Client** ([src/17-starter-pack.js](src/17-starter-pack.js) — NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeOfferStarterPack(scoreOverride)` is the public entry — throttled 1/min internally, fetches status with the player's best score, and if `available=true` mounts a `.starter-pack-home-banner` at the TOP of `#home-screen-v2`. Banner: 🎁 swinging icon + name + perks line (`1500💎 + סקין + 3 דרגות BP`) + live countdown pill (`⏰ 6י 22ש`) + gold "פתח →" CTA + × close. Click banner OR CTA → `showStarterPackModal(data)` — full-screen overlay with: red "חד-פעמית · ⏰ 6י 22ש" ribbon (loss-aversion stamp), giant 🎁 icon, contents list (3 items: gems / skin / BP tiers), value calculation card showing `~2400💎` total vs `500💎` price = `חסכת 79%` (anchoring psychology), giant gold "✨ קנה עכשיו · 500💎" button. Disabled state when balance insufficient: shows `💎 חסר N💎` instead. Buy → `confirm` → POST → on success: local balance + skin cache update, `soundMilestone(6)` + buzz, full-screen `showStarterPackWelcomeOverlay` (spinning 🎁, "תודה!", contents recap). **Trigger** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): game-over branch fires `maybeOfferStarterPack(score)` BEFORE the over-screen renders so the server can stamp eligibility with this game's score. Skipped for bot/skin-trial games. **Home mount** ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)): also fires `maybeOfferStarterPack()` 800ms after mount — so a returning player who closed the banner sees it again next session (within the 7-day window). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `🎁 Starter Pack` section under 💰 כלכלה tab with 4 logical groups (master + naming, pricing, trigger conditions, pack contents) + 9 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with detailed economic-math examples. Cache buster `v20260523k`, SW `bloom-v9.5`.
- ✅ **Premium Battle Pass — stage 17 — the #1 monetization driver (May 2026)** — dual-track Battle Pass with paid premium tier — the highest-revenue feature in modern F2P (Fortnite, Apex, Genshin all use this exact pattern). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) migrations array): 3 new columns on `player_season_progress` (`is_premium BOOLEAN` / `premium_purchased_at TIMESTAMPTZ` / `claimed_premium_tiers JSONB`); 3 master config keys (`season_pass_premium_enabled` default `'true'` / `_price_gems` default `'1500'` / `_price_usd` default `'4.99'`); 20 premium reward keys `season_tier_<N>_premium_reward` seeded at exactly ×2 the free reward (sum ~32,000💎/season premium vs ~16,000💎 free). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `buildSeasonTiers` now emits `premiumReward` per tier (falls back to `reward × 2` when key missing). `/api/player/season/status` returns `isPremium` + `claimedPremiumTiers` + `premiumEnabled` + `premiumPriceGems` + `premiumPriceUsd`; `unclaimedCount` double-counts when premium owned (so a player who crossed tier 5 with premium and claimed nothing sees `10 🎁`). `/api/player/season/claim-tier` accepts new `track` field (`'free'` | `'premium'`) — gates premium claims on `is_premium=true`, dedups per-track via `claimed_premium_tiers`, returns both arrays so the client can update state. **New endpoint** `POST /api/player/season/buy-premium`: atomic balance deduct + flip `is_premium` in a single transaction (no orphan debits possible). Returns `{ok, price, newBalance}` on success or `{ok:false, reason:'insufficient_funds', price, balance}` for UI hint. Rate-limited 10/hr. Already-premium returns idempotent `{ok:false, reason:'already_premium'}`. **Client** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): rewrote `renderSeasonModalBody` to dual-track layout — each tier now shows TWO buttons side-by-side (mint free + gold premium). When premium NOT owned: premium buttons render as a `.dyn-season-track-tease` (dashed gold border, "🔒 +N💎") for tiers the player has already earned — **pure loss-aversion punch**. New big `.dyn-season-buy-banner` at TOP of modal with: ✨ pulsing star, title "שדרג ל-Premium Battle Pass", subtitle showing total premium gems available, **"🎁 N💎 ב-M דרגות שכבר חצית — מחכים לך!" hint** showing exactly how much value the player is leaving on the table, and a big gold "🔓 שדרג עכשיו · 1500💎" CTA button. New `claimSeasonTier(tierN, track, btnEl)` signature passes track to server. New `confirmAndBuyPremium(btnEl)` → JS confirm() showing price + balance + total expected gems → POST → on success: `showPremiumWelcomeOverlay()` (full-screen golden celebration card with ✨ spinning star, "Premium פעיל!", auto-dismiss 8s). **Surfaces**: (1) Modal "✨ Premium" pill in header sub when owned. (2) Modal big buy banner when not owned. (3) Each tier card shows both rewards (gold one greyed/teased without premium). (4) Home tile: `<span class="home-v2-sp-prem">✨ Premium</span>` badge next to "דרגה N" when owned. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): premium master controls section above XP rates (3 keys: enabled / price_gems / price_usd) with detailed Hebrew tooltip explaining monetization rationale + ROI math; 20-tier table got a 4th column "✨ 💎 Premium" with gold-tinted input cells, auto-saves on blur/Enter; 3 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples ("default 1500💎 → returns 32,000💎 = 20× ROI"). The premium track is fully toggleable — admin can disable via `season_pass_premium_enabled='false'` and the entire premium UI disappears (existing premium-owners keep their claimed rewards intact). Cache buster `v20260523j`, SW `bloom-v9.4`. **Stripe IAP wiring is stage 17b** — currently the USD price is display-only.
