- ✅ **Daily Special Board — stage 15 — daily mini-event boards (May 2026)** — the #1 daily-return hook in F2P puzzle games, ported to BLOOM. Every day at Asia/Jerusalem midnight ONE dynamic board is anointed as "🌟 הלוח של היום" with **×3 Season XP + ×2 quest rewards**. Deterministic pick — all players see the SAME board today, but it rotates. Players who play it daily get massive Season Pass acceleration; players who skip a day feel the loss. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 4 new `game_config` keys — `daily_special_enabled` (master, default `'true'`) + `daily_special_xp_mult` (default `'3'`) + `daily_special_reward_mult` (default `'2'`) + `daily_special_override_id` (default `''`, lets admin force a specific board for today, e.g. Valentine on 14/2). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_dailySpecialHash(dateStr)` FNV-1a hash → deterministic index into the active dynamic-boards list. `pickDailySpecial(boardRows)` is the picker, `getDailySpecialForToday()` re-queries for the XP/reward branches. `GET /api/boards/available` now returns `{ ok, boards, dailySpecial: {enabled, id, xpMult, rewardMult, date, isOverride} }` at the top level — single-fetch, no extra round trip. `POST /api/player/season/grant-xp` reads `meta.boardId` and when it matches today's special multiplies `xpGain` by `xpMult` (capped at `season_xp_max_per_game × Math.ceil(xpMult)` so the daily can earn ~300 XP/game on default). `POST /api/player/earn` `dyn_quest` branch reads `meta.boardId` and multiplies the quest reward by `rewardMult` when the boardId matches today's special. Both are server-authoritative — client never names the multipliers. **Client** ([src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) + [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): `window._dailySpecial` populated from the same `/api/boards/available` response that already runs every 90s. New `hasPlayedDailySpecialToday(date, boardId)` + `markDailySpecialPlayed(date, boardId)` localStorage helpers keyed on the date so it auto-resets at midnight. **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker header banner** — at the ABSOLUTE TOP of the picker (above tournaments + season pass + quests): gold-pink pulsing gradient `.dyn-daily-special-banner` with 🌟 icon (rotating + scaling), board name in strong, 3 inline pills (`3× XP` mint, `2× פרסים` mint, `שחק עכשיו ←` gold CTA). Tap = closes picker + immediately starts the special board. (2) **Picker card glow** — the special board's card gets a `.daily-special` class with breathing gold border + box-shadow (`dailySpecialCardGlow` 2.6s keyframes), plus a unique gold-pink chip at the top of its chip row: `🌟 הלוח של היום · 3× XP · 2× פרסים`. (3) **Home button label** — new `.fomo-daily-special` class with gold-pink gradient. Inserted into the existing priority ladder: `questClaimable > streakDanger > dailySpecial-unplayed > FOMO-countdown > streak-calm > default`. When the player hasn't played today's special yet: `🌟 הלוח של היום: ולנטיין · 3× XP מחכים!`. Auto-disappears after `markDailySpecialPlayed` fires on game-over. (4) **Game-over banner** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js)) — gold-pink `.over-daily-special-banner` immediately after the rank pill (above streak/ach/quest banners) with the celebration message "🌟 שיחקת את הלוח של היום! · קיבלת **3× XP** + **2× פרסים** על המשחק הזה". CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) with full dark-theme overrides. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 4 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples + 2 new `PRESETS_PER_KEY` chip lists (`daily_special_xp_mult: [1.5, 2, 3, 4, 5]` / `daily_special_reward_mult: [1.5, 2, 2.5, 3]`). The `daily_special_override_id` field stays free-text since it's a numeric board id. Cache buster `v20260523g`, SW `bloom-v9.1`.
- ✅ **Daily Login Multiplier Stack — stage 14 — prospective FOMO via breakdown rows (May 2026)** — the existing daily-login bonus already had streak tiers (15→200💎 for 1→30 day streaks), but it was a black box: the player saw `+50💎` and didn't understand why. Now the overlay shows a **breakdown table** with one row per multiplier source, **active rows in mint** (✓ unlocked) and **locked rows in dashed grey** (🔒 with a "do X to unlock" hint). 4 new admin config keys: `daily_login_mult_dyn_streak_pct` (default +25%) + `_min` (default 3 dyn-streak days) + `_friend_shared_pct` (default +20%) + `_max_pct` (default 300% cap). **Server** in [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn` `daily_login` branch now reads `meta.dynStreak` + `meta.friendSharedYesterday` and stacks the multipliers on top of the tier base, capped at `_max_pct`. Returns a `breakdown: { base, baseTier, totalPct, cappedAtPct, breakdown: [{label, factor, contribution}], finalReward }` object so the client can paint the math transparently. **Client** in [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js): `earnCredits('daily_login', ...)` now passes `dynStreak` (from `getDynamicStreak()`) + `friendSharedYesterday` (true if any cached friend has `playedToday`). New `renderDailyLoginBreakdown(overlay, displayStreak)` helper injects a `.dr-breakdown` block above the claim button with 3 rows: **Row 1** (🔥 רצף יומי) is always-active showing tier multiplier (×1/×2/×3/×4); **Row 2** (🎯 רצף לוחות דינמיים) — active mint pill if ≥ `dynMin` else locked grey "עוד N ימים" hint; **Row 3** (👥 חבר שיחק היום) — active mint if friend `playedToday`, locked grey hint if has friends but none played, or pink CTA "הזמן חבר" if no friends. The pink CTA row is the prospective-FOMO punch — a player with NO friends sees what they're leaving on the table. CSS in [public/css/viral.css](public/css/viral.css): `.dr-breakdown`, `.dr-mult-row-active/-locked/-cta` with full dark-theme overrides. Admin tooltips for the 4 new keys with economic math examples ("streak×4 + dyn 25% + friend 20% = 145% → capped at 300% = 4× base"). Cache buster `v20260523e`, SW `bloom-v8.9`.
- ✅ **Friends Invite + Shared Streak — stage 13 — the viral loop (May 2026)** — every player has a `BLOOM-XXXX` code already (from `player_profiles.player_code`); now sharing it is the K-factor lever. **Schema**: `friendships` table with symmetric storage (PK `(device_a, device_b)` where `device_a < device_b` lex, plus `initiator` + `bonus_paid` flag) — eliminates the "duplicate-friendship" footgun. `friendship_shared_days` for per-day shared-play bonus dedup (PK `(a, b, date)`). `player_daily_dyn_activity` tracker for "did this device play a dynamic game today?". 4 admin config keys (`friends_enabled`, `friends_signup_bonus` default 200, `friends_shared_day_bonus` default 100, `friends_max_per_device` default 50). **Server** in [server.js](server.js): `POST /api/friends/invite` resolves `friendCode` → `device_id` via `player_profiles`, validates anti-self + max-cap, atomic insert + dual-credit transaction + push notification to the invitee ("👥 דניאל הוסיף אותך — שניכם קיבלתם 200💎"); `GET /api/friends/list?deviceId=` returns each friend's name + code + `playedToday` flag + my own `iPlayedToday`. **Recurring shared bonus**: hooked into the existing `POST /api/boards/:id/score` flow — `recordDynActivityAndPayShared(deviceId)` runs after every dynamic-board score is recorded. It upserts `player_daily_dyn_activity` for today + scans the player's friends for any who also have an activity row today AND no `friendship_shared_days` row yet → atomic transaction credits both + marks the day claimed. Fire-and-forget (doesn't block score submission). **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchFriends(force)` with 60s cache, `sendFriendInvite(code)`, `buildInviteUrl()` produces `<origin>/?ref=BLOOM-XXXX`, `shareInviteViaWhatsApp()` opens `wa.me/?text=...`, `shareInviteViaNative()` uses `navigator.share` with clipboard fallback. **URL `?ref=` autohandler** runs 1.5s after boot: parses ref, dedups via `localStorage[bloom_ref_seen:<code>]`, skips self-invites (compares to own code), then pops the gold-pink gradient overlay "👥 חבר הזמין אותך! · קוד החבר: BLOOM-XYZW · +200💎 · לשניכם · יחד מקבלים +100💎 בכל יום ששניכם תשחקו". Tap-to-accept → `sendFriendInvite` → milestone sound + buzz + close. **Friends Modal** accessible from new pink-gradient headline pill in picker header ("👥 הזמן חבר → +200💎 לשניכם" if empty; "👥 2 מ-5 חברים שיחקו היום" otherwise). Modal has 3 sections: (1) **My code** with 3 share buttons (💬 WhatsApp green / 📤 Native share / 📋 Copy link); (2) **Add by code** input with `BLOOM-XXXX` placeholder + monospace 14-char input + error states (`friend_not_found` / `cant_self_friend` / `max_friends_reached`); (3) **Friends list** with avatar circles + name + code + per-row "✓ שיחק היום" mint pill OR "⏰ עדיין לא היום" grey pill — the social FOMO surface ("דניאל שיחק היום, אני לא — הוא מקבל את ה-100💎 בלעדיי"). Cache buster `v20260523d`, SW `bloom-v8.8`.
- ✅ **Live Tournaments — stage 12 — scheduled prime-time community moments (May 2026)** — admin schedules a tournament with `[starts_at, ends_at)` window + a top-N prize pool. Any dynamic-board game played within the window auto-submits the player's BEST score (best-score-wins upsert mirroring daily_scores). After ends_at, the **next** fetch of `/api/tournaments` lazy-finalizes: top-N players have their prize credited to balance in a single transaction + receive a push notification ("🏆 זכית בטורניר! מקום 1 · 5,000💎 נכנסו"). No cron needed — pull-based finalize keeps infra simple. **Schema**: new `tournaments` table (id, name, description, starts_at, ends_at, `prize_pool JSONB` = array of `{rank, reward}`, status, finalized_at) + `tournament_scores` table (PK `(tournament_id, device_id)`, best-score-wins upsert + per-player games_played counter + `prize_claimed` int). `idx_tournament_scores_lb` for fast top-N queries. **Server** (4 public + 5 admin endpoints): `GET /api/tournaments` lists live/upcoming/recent-ended in one call with lazy-finalize trigger; `GET /api/tournaments/:id/leaderboard` returns top 50 + my rank + prize pool; `POST /api/tournaments/:id/score` enforces the window + drops anti-cheat + best-score upsert; admin CRUD: list/create/patch/delete + manual finalize. `maybeFinalizeTournament(id)` is the shared helper — atomic transaction: claim_prize + balance credit + status flip + push notification per winner. **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchTournaments(force)` with 60s cache, `getLiveTournament()` / `getUpcomingTournament()` selectors, `submitTournamentScoreFromGame(score, tier, drops)` wired into the dynamic-mode game-over branch (auto-submits silently — best score wins). `renderTournamentBannerHtml()` renders a red-pink-gold pulsing banner at the TOP of the picker header when a tournament is live (or a blue "⏰ בקרוב" banner when one starts within 24h). `showTournamentModal(id)` opens a full leaderboard with 🥇🥈🥉 podium, country flags, you-row highlight, prize-pool display, and "🏆 שחק בטורניר" CTA that opens the picker. **Admin UI** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html) → 🏆 תחרויות tab) new "טורנירים חיים" section with table of all tournaments + status badges (🔴 LIVE / ⏳ עתידי / ⏰ ממתין לסיום / ✓ הסתיים) + "+ טורניר חדש" composer modal with: name + description + starts_at/ends_at datetime pickers + prize_pool freeform input (format `#1:5000, #2:2000`) + **3 quick-presets** (⭐ Prime Time = today 20:00-21:00, 🎉 Weekend = next Friday 14:00-16:00, ⚡ Quick = +5 min for 1h) + manual "💰 סיום" button for early finalize + cascade delete. Cache buster `v20260523c`, SW `bloom-v8.7`.
- ✅ **Season Pass — stage 11 — the #1 F2P retention engine (May 2026)** — 20-tier reward track that turns every action into progress toward a visible goal. Inspired by Fortnite/Genshin/Apex Battle Pass — the single most addictive feature in modern F2P. **Schema**: new `player_season_progress` table with `(device_id, season_id)` PK + `xp INT` + `claimed_tiers JSONB[]` + `recent_game_ids JSONB[]` (per-game dedup buffer, trimmed to last 50). 4 master config keys (`season_pass_enabled` / `season_id` / `name` / `ends_at`) + 6 XP-source rates + 40 tier keys (`season_tier_<N>_xp` + `season_tier_<N>_reward` for N=1..20). Tier curve: 40 XP → 5,950 XP across 20 tiers, rewards 25💎 → 3,000💎 (sum ~16,000💎 per season). Easy early game ("first 5 tiers in day 1") + harder late game ("tier 20 needs 3-4 weeks consistent play"). **Server** (3 endpoints in [server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/player/season/status` returns `{xp, currentTier, claimedTiers, unclaimedCount, tiers, seasonName, endsAt}`; `POST /api/player/season/grant-xp` validates `source` against allowlist (`dyn_game_finish` / `quest_done` / `achievement`), recomputes XP server-side from meta (anti-cheat — client can't claim arbitrary XP), dedups per `gameId` via the in-row buffer, caps at `season_xp_max_per_game`; `POST /api/player/season/claim-tier` atomic credit+claim in a transaction (claimed_tiers append + balance increment) so a player can never get one without the other. **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchSeasonStatus(force)` with 60s cache, `grantSeasonXpForGame(gameId, score, tier)` called from the dynamic-mode game-over branch, `showSeasonPassModal()` renders the full 20-tier roadmap with claim buttons, `showSeasonLevelUpToast(tier)` fires 4.5s after game-over (after chest reveal lands) when player crosses a tier — `soundMilestone(5)` + buzz `[60,50,90]`. **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker header headline** — gold gradient pill at the TOP of the picker (highest priority) with current tier number + thin progress bar + "🎁 N לקבל" unclaimed badge that pulses when present. Tap → opens Season Pass modal. (2) **Modal**: gold gradient header with season name, top progress bar (XP toward next tier), scrollable 20-tier list. Each tier card: numbered circle (gold for unlocked, mint for claimed, grey for locked) + XP threshold + reward amount + status pill (locked / claim button / "✓ נאסף"). (3) **Game-over level-up toast** lands AFTER the chest reveal — choreography: rank pill (200ms) → personal best banner → chest animation (4.5s) → season level-up toast (4.5s) → fade. No surface overlap. Cache buster `v20260523b`, SW `bloom-v8.6`.
- 🐛 **Critical bug-fix: missing `updated_at` column + reward-clamp bypass + shop expansion (May 2026)** — user-reported triple bug: (1) quest/achievement rewards announced N💎 but balance only went up by ≤10💎, (2) `/api/player/streak-freeze/buy` and similar endpoints returning 500, (3) skin/powerup purchases failing intermittently. **Root cause A**: the chest, comeback-claim, and streak-freeze/buy endpoints I added in stages 8-9 all do `UPDATE player_profiles SET balance = balance ± $1, updated_at = NOW()` — but `player_profiles` schema has no `updated_at` column (only `created_at`). Postgres throws "column does not exist" → 500. Fix: added `ALTER TABLE player_profiles ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()` to both [schema.sql](schema.sql) and [db.js](db.js) `initDb()` migrations array for belt-and-suspenders. **Root cause B**: quest/achievement/streak-milestone rewards all went through `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount})`, and the server's event_gift handler CLAMPS to `[event_gift_credits_min, event_gift_credits_max]` (production values: 2-10💎). So a quest promising +100💎 paid 10💎. An achievement promising +300💎 paid 10💎. A 60-day streak milestone promising +1000💎 paid 10💎. This was the "credits don't appear" bug — they did appear, just clamped. Fix: 3 new server actions in [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn`: `dyn_quest` / `dyn_ach` / `dyn_streak_milestone` — each reads the actual reward amount from the existing `dyn_*_reward_*` config keys, with per-action allowlists for the `meta.quest_id` / `meta.ach_id` / `meta.milestone` (anti-cheat — cheater can't invent unknown ids to mint payouts). Extended `META_DEDUP_ACTIONS` to include the three so dedup works correctly per-quest/ach/milestone. Client updated in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) (`claimQuestReward` + `checkAndGrantAchievements`) and [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) (streak milestone fire path). **Shop expansion**: added "לוחות דינמיים" section to the in-game shop ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)) with two new items — 🛡 **Streak Freeze** (price from `dyn_streak_freeze_price`, default 200💎, integrates with existing freeze count display) and 🎁 **Bonus Mystery Chest** (100💎 to open an extra chest bypassing the daily cap — pure Skinner-box gambling, sold transparently). Both gated by their respective master toggles so an admin who disabled the system never sees the items. Bonus chest path: `/api/player/spend` for the 100💎 deduction → instant `openMysteryChest()` call which rolls server-side and animates the reveal. Cache buster `v20260523a`, SW `bloom-v8.5`.
- ✅ **Push Notifications — admin broadcast + smart prompts — stage 10 (May 2026)** — closes the retention loop with the channel that reaches players when the app is closed. **Most of the infrastructure was already in place** from an earlier round: server-side `web-push` integration ([server.js](server.js) lines 7-68 with VAPID setup + `sendPushToDevice` helper used by duels, gifts, challenges), `push_subscriptions` table in [schema.sql](schema.sql) line 410, `/api/push/vapid-public` + `/api/push/subscribe` + `/api/push/unsubscribe` endpoints, full client-side flow in [src/16-push.js](src/16-push.js) (`subscribeToPush`, soft pre-prompt overlay, `maybeAskForPushPermission` exposed as `window.__bloomMaybeAskPush`), and SW handlers in [public/sw.js](public/sw.js) for `push` / `notificationclick` / `pushsubscriptionchange`. **What this commit adds**: (1) Three admin endpoints in [server.js](server.js): `GET /<ADMIN>/api/push/status` (returns `configured` / `enabled` / `subscriberCount` / `vapidPublic`), `POST /<ADMIN>/api/push/test` (send to one device for QA), `POST /<ADMIN>/api/push/broadcast` (send to ALL subscribers in batches of 200 with parallel pushes per batch, soft-fails on individual stale endpoints via the existing 410-Gone cleanup, writes audit log to `admin_actions`). Master toggle `push_enabled` in `game_config` defaults `'true'`. (2) Admin push composer UI in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under 🔧 ניטור tab — status badge with subscriber count, title + body + URL + tag + requireInteraction inputs, 4 quick templates (lוח חג / רצף בסכנה / פרס ממתין / אירוע פרסים), test + broadcast buttons, result panel showing succeeded/failed counts. (3) **Smart prompt triggers** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) — `__bloomMaybeAskPush(reason)` now fires at 3 high-intent dopamine moments: **first 3-day streak milestone** ("נשמור על הרצף שלך"), **first achievement unlock** (≤2 earned total, "הישג ראשון!"), and **comeback claim** ("ברוך שובך! לא תפספס שוב"). The existing 3-day pre-prompt cooldown in [src/16-push.js](src/16-push.js) prevents over-asking. (4) Added `web-push@3.6.7` to `package.json` (first new dep approved by user). Pre-launch checklist for production: set `VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY` + `VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY` + `VAPID_SUBJECT` env vars on Railway (`npx web-push generate-vapid-keys`). Cache buster `v20260522zh`, SW `bloom-v8.4`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Streak Freeze + Comeback Bonus — stage 9 (May 2026)** — two retention safety nets layered on top of the existing streak system. **Streak Freeze** (Duolingo's `🛡` mechanic): player buys "freezes" with 💎 (default 200/each via `dyn_streak_freeze_price`). When `recordDynamicStreakDay()` detects exactly a 1-day miss (`gap === 2`) AND `getStreakFreezes() > 0`, it consumes one freeze and treats the streak as continuous. Server enforces the purchase via the existing balance-guarded `UPDATE` pattern in `POST /api/player/streak-freeze/buy` (10/hr rate-limit). Freeze count is client-side `localStorage[bloom_dyn_freezes]` — a determined cheater could fake the count but freezes have no trade value (protect only their own streak). New freeze pill in the picker header (blue gradient `.dyn-freeze-row`) with current count + buy button. On a successful purchase the picker re-renders to show the new count. When a freeze auto-applies on game-over, a separate `.over-streak-banner-freeze` (blue gradient + `dynFreezePulse` 3-cycle animation) tells the player "🛡 הקפאת רצף הצילה אותך! איבדת יום אבל הרצף ממשיך" so they FEEL the value of their 200💎 investment. **Comeback Bonus** (re-engagement for lapsed players): when `recordDynamicStreakDay()` resets a streak ≥3, it saves `lostStreak` + `lostStreakDate` into the streak object. `getComebackContext()` checks if the player is now eligible — streak was ≥`dyn_comeback_min_streak` (3) AND `daysAway ≥ dyn_comeback_min_days` (3). On picker open, fires `showComebackOverlay()` 350ms after the shell renders — a full-screen rainbow-gradient celebration card with 👋 waving icon, "ברוך שובך!" title, the lost-streak count, the reward amount (+150💎 default), and a freeze-gift bonus (+1 free freeze via `dyn_comeback_freeze_gift`). Tap "🎁 קבל את הבונוס" → `POST /api/player/comeback-claim` (server-side dedup: one claim per device per rolling 7-day window via `_comeback:<deviceId>:<week>` game_config key). Server-side validation: server re-checks `dyn_comeback_min_days/min_streak` against the client-claimed values, refuses if too low. Marks `st.comebackClaimedFor = lostStreakDate` so the overlay never re-fires for the same lost streak. **8 new admin config keys** with tooltips + presets: `dyn_streak_freeze_enabled/price/max_per_streak`, `dyn_comeback_enabled/min_days/min_streak/reward/freeze_gift`. The freeze pill, comeback overlay, and freeze-used banner all respect their master toggles. Cache buster `v20260522zg`, SW `bloom-v8.3`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Mystery Chest (Skinner box) — stage 8 (May 2026)** — the variable-ratio reinforcement layer that makes slot machines addictive, applied to every dynamic-board game-over. **5 rarity tiers** with admin-tuneable weights + amounts (`common/uncommon/rare/legendary/mythic` — defaults `60/25/12/2/1` percent, payouts `3-10 / 15-30 / 50-100 / 200-400 / 800-1500` 💎). **Server-rolled** via `POST /api/boards/chest/open` in [server.js](server.js) ([requireDeviceAuth], 30/hr rate limit) — client never picks the tier (anti-cheat). Atomic credit + per-day counter via a single `game_config` dedup key `_chest:<deviceId>:<date>`. **"Boosted pity"** — first N chests/day (default 3) skip the common tier entirely so a new player's first 3 chests never feel cheap. **Daily cap** (default 20) prevents farming. **Client reveal animation** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) `openMysteryChest()` → 5-stage choreography over ~4.5s: (1) chest 📦 appears + shakes 900ms with knock tone, (2) lid pops + light burst (radial gradient `dynChestBurst` keyframe), (3) **slot-machine reel** spins through tier emojis (📦→🎁→💠→🌟→🔮) with ease-out deceleration + click tone per tick, (4) lands on the real tier — pitch-graded landing sound (320/440/560/700/880 Hz for the 5 tiers), buzz `[60,40,80]`, card adds `.dyn-chest-card-landed` for breathing-glow + rim-pulse infinite, (5) gem amount counts up from 0 over 700ms. **Confetti** spawns for rare+ tiers (18-particle radial burst with per-tier color palettes). **Tier-specific corner sparkles ✨** decorate legendary + mythic via `::before/::after` pseudo-elements. **17 new `game_config` keys** in [schema.sql](schema.sql): `dyn_chest_enabled` (master), 5 `_weight_*`, 10 `_*_min/max`, `_daily_cap`, `_boosted_count`. **Admin tooltips + preset chip lists** for all 17 in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) — explains economic math (e.g. "1 mythic per 100 chests = שחקן יזכור לימים"). **Wired into** the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) — fires 900ms after `render({over:true})` so the player reads the headline before the chest takes over. Also polished 4 weak user-facing strings (picker subtitle, pioneer chip, empty-state copy, streak pioneer banner) for stronger psychological pull. Cache buster `v20260522zf`, SW `bloom-v8.2`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Full admin control over retention systems (May 2026)** — user feedback: "did you make sure the admin controls everything?" → no, the FOMO/PB/global-LB/streak/achievements/quests rewards were all hardcoded. Closing the gap with **34 new `game_config` keys** that let the admin tune the entire retention stack without a redeploy. **6 master toggles** (`dyn_quests_enabled` / `dyn_achievements_enabled` / `dyn_streak_enabled` / `dyn_personal_best_enabled` / `dyn_global_lb_enabled` / `dyn_fomo_enabled` — all default `'true'`, admin opts OUT not in). Setting any to `'false'` hides every chip/banner/modal/in-game-pill associated with that system — the localStorage is preserved so re-enabling restores everything intact. **28 per-reward keys**: 11 quest rewards (`dyn_quest_reward_play2/play3/score10k/score30k/score75k/tier7/tier8/theme/shape/beatself/beatleader`), 5 per-board ach rewards (`played/crown/score10/score50/score100`), 6 cross-board ach rewards (`pioneer5/pioneer10/crown5/all_themes/all_shapes/leaderboard1`), 6 streak milestone rewards (`dyn_streak_reward_3/7/14/30/60/100`). Defaults seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql) match the original hardcoded values. **Client wiring** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): new `dynConfig(key, default)` / `dynConfigInt` / `dynConfigBool` readers from the `gameConfig` module-scope variable (loaded by `/api/config` at boot) + `dynFeatureEnabled(name)` for the 6 master toggles. Reward helpers `dynStreakReward(milestone)` / `dynAchReward(id)` / `dynQuestReward(id)` resolve at runtime. `window.DYN_STREAK_REWARDS` is now a `Proxy` that auto-resolves to `dynStreakReward(N)` so any code reading `DYN_STREAK_REWARDS[7]` picks up the admin's override. Quest rewards are also re-resolved on every `getDailyQuests()` read so an admin's mid-day reward bump applies to already-completed-but-not-claimed quests. **Admin tooltips** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 34 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with rich Hebrew copy explaining each key — recommended value ranges, retention rationale, dependency notes (e.g. "dyn_ach_reward_leaderboard1: requires the /leaderboard fetch to confirm rank=1"). 28 new `PRESETS_PER_KEY` chip lists for one-click typical values (e.g. crown reward presets `[75, 150, 250, 300]`). All keys appear in the existing "כל ההגדרות" config table with auto-detected toggle/preset/free-input UI — `*_enabled` keys get the green ✓ פעיל / red ✗ כבוי toggle buttons, numeric reward keys get input + preset chips. Cache buster `v20260522ze`, SW `bloom-v8.1`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Daily Quests (May 2026)** — the F2P checklist mechanic. 3 fresh quests every Asia/Jerusalem day, deterministic per date via `mulberry32(hashSeed(date + ':dyn-quests-v1'))` so all players see the same pool draw (community talking point) but the menu varies day-to-day. Pool of 11 quests in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) `DYN_QUEST_POOL`: 2/3 different boards (50/100💎), score≥10K/30K/75K (50/100/250💎), tier≥7/8 (75/200💎), play themed/shape (60/60💎), beat your own best (120💎), beat the global leader (300💎). Storage `localStorage[bloom_dyn_quests_<YYYY-MM-DD>]` keeps yesterday's row cleaned up via deferred `setTimeout(0)` removal. **Manual claim pattern** (Clash Royale / Duolingo, NOT auto-claim): completed quest shows a gold-pink pulsing `🎁 קבל +N💎` button. Tap = call `claimQuestReward(id)` → `earnCredits` fires + button replaces itself with `✓ נאסף` + `soundMilestone(3)` + `buzz([30,30,60])`. The "I have rewards waiting" hook drives return visits even when the player doesn't want to play. **Quest pipeline** in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) dynamic-mode game-over branch: synchronous `applyQuestProgressOnGameOver()` returns just-completed quests + asynchronous re-check after the /leaderboard fetch resolves (for the beat_leader quest that needs the global rank). Fires `renderQuestCompletedToast(q)` for late completions. **Surfaces**: (1) **Home button label** — `🎁 N פרסים של משימה ממתינים לך — לחץ!` (mint-green breathing background `.fomo-quest-claim`) takes PRIORITY over streak-danger and FOMO — a sitting unclaimed gem reward is louder than any other signal. (2) **Picker header pill** — `🎯 משימות יומיות: 1/3 · 1 🎁 לקבל` (green gradient, gold-pink pulsing king variant when claimable). (3) **Game-over banner** — green-emerald pulsing card per quest completed this game (`over-quest-banner`). (4) **Quests modal** — full catalog with per-quest progress bar (locked: dimmed `+50💎` pill; completed: gold-pink claim button; claimed: muted `✓ נאסף`). Each row's bar fills 0→100% as progress updates; completed rows recolor to gold-pink gradient. Cache buster `v20260522zd`, SW `bloom-v8.0`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Achievements / Badges (May 2026)** — the completionist engine. 5 per-board + 6 cross-board achievements, each unlock fires `earnCredits` for 25-1000💎. Storage in `localStorage[bloom_dyn_achievements]` (renamed from `ACH_KEY` to `DYN_ACH_KEY` to avoid collision with the existing achievements system in [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)). Shape: `{ perBoard: { <boardId>: { played: ts, crown: ts, score10: ts, ... } }, cross: { pioneer5: ts, all_themes: ts, ... } }`. **Per-board achievements** (5×N boards): 🌱 played (25💎), 👑 reached crown (150💎), 💎 score≥10K (50💎), 🏆 score≥50K (150💎), 💯 score≥100K (300💎). **Cross-board achievements** (6 total): 🗺️ 5 different boards (200💎), 🧭 10 different boards (500💎), 👑 5 crowns (500💎), 🎄 all 4 themes (800💎), 🟦 all 4 shapes (800💎), 🥇 #1 on any board (1000💎). **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker card chip** — `🏅 🌱 👑 💎` icon stack of earned per-board achievements next to the existing chips, gives instant "I have 3 / 5 here, can I get the rest?" psychology. (2) **Picker header button** — `🏅 הישגים: 7 / 34` gold pill, opens the full modal. (3) **Game-over banner** — `over-ach-banner` (gold-pink pulsing) for each achievement unlocked this game, stacks vertically when multiple fire on one big game-over. (4) **Floating top-of-viewport toast** for late unlocks (the leaderboard rank-1 achievement only confirms after the /leaderboard fetch — fires `renderAchievementUnlockToast(u)` 200-400ms after the over screen renders). (5) **Achievements modal** — full catalog with earned items glowing gold + locked items dimmed with reward visible, grouped into "🏆 כלליים" (cross with `x / y` progress lines) + "🎯 פר לוח" (per-board accordion with 5-icon badge grid per board). Rank-1 detection uses a two-phase grant: initial pass grants everything score/tier-based, post-fetch pass grants the `leaderboard1` cross achievement once the /api/boards/:id/leaderboard response confirms `rank === 1`. Cache buster `v20260522zc`, SW `bloom-v7.9`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Cross-board streak (May 2026)** — the multi-day retention layer. Duolingo-style "play any dynamic board for N consecutive days" — losing the streak is on the player (no auto-freeze in v1), regaining it is satisfying. **Storage**: `localStorage[bloom_dyn_streak]` = `{count, last (YYYY-MM-DD Asia/Jerusalem), milestonesClaimed: []}`. The variable was originally named `STREAK_KEY` but conflicted with the existing daily-streak system in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) — renamed to `DYN_STREAK_KEY` etc. so the two streaks coexist. **Logic**: `recordDynamicStreakDay()` (called from the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) compares today's date with `last`: if same day → no-op; if exactly 1 day later → increment; otherwise → reset to 1 + clear `milestonesClaimed`. Milestones: 3/7/14/30/60/100 days; rewards: 50/150/300/600/1000/2000 💎, granted via `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount, streak_milestone: N})`. **Three visible surfaces**: **(1) Home button subtitle** — `isStreakInDanger()` (streak ≥3 AND not played today) takes priority: "🔥 הרצף שלך בסכנה! N ימים — שחק היום" + `.fomo-streak-danger` class adds a red-pink breathing background. Otherwise FOMO countdown / streak headline (`🔥 רצף N ימים · M לוחות זמינים`) per priority. **(2) Picker modal header banner** — three states: `dyn-streak-banner-pioneer` (🌱 onboarding copy with full milestone schedule, no streak yet), `dyn-streak-banner-safe` (calm warm gradient + "שמרת אותו היום ✓"), `dyn-streak-banner-danger` (red breathing gradient + "שחק כל לוח דינמי עד חצות"). All three show the next-milestone progress line ("עוד N ימים לבאדג׳ M (+R💎)"). **(3) Game-over banner** in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) — `over-streak-banner-milestone` (gold-pink pulsing celebration on milestone hits with the reward amount) OR `over-streak-banner` (warm calm version with progress to next milestone) — passed via new `opts.streakResult` from the dynamic game-over branch. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css). Cache buster `v20260522zb`, SW `bloom-v7.8`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Per-board top-50 leaderboard modal (May 2026)** — completes the addiction loop. Each picker card now sports a gold trophy button next to it (`.dyn-boards-trophy-btn`) that opens a per-board top-50 leaderboard modal — totally separate from the play action, so the player can browse standings without committing to a game. The modal in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): gold gradient header with board name + theme/shape meta; live `fetch('/api/boards/:id/leaderboard?limit=50&deviceId=…')` with 30s setInterval refresh; rows show `🥇🥈🥉` for top 3 / `#N` rank for the rest, country flag (regional-indicator codepoint math, no asset work), name, score. "You" row is highlighted with a gold-pink gradient border + box-shadow; off-list players (>50) get a separate sticky "אתה #87" pill at the bottom. **The most addictive piece** is the persistent `🎯 next-target` banner above the list: when the player has a score, it computes `aboveScore - myScore` and renders "⚔️ עוד 1,234 נקודות כדי לעקוף את דניאל" in a pulsing gold-orange pill — same psychological lever as the contest "overtake watch". When the player IS the leader: "👑 אתה המוביל! · המקום השני: 89K" in the full pulsing pink-gold king variant. Modal lifecycle: `_boardLbRefreshHandle` cleared on close + ESC + backdrop click; `_boardLbCurrentBoard` guards paint() against stale fetches if the player switches boards rapidly. Footer has "← חזור" (back to picker) + "▶ שחק עכשיו" primary CTA (closes modal + immediately starts the board) — so the leaderboard is a no-friction stepping stone, not a dead-end. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): full light/dark theme palette, `.dyn-boards-trophy-btn` (46px gold pill on each card), `.board-lb-overlay/.modal/.head/.body/.foot`, `.board-lb-row` with top-1/2/3/you variants, `.board-lb-next-target` + `-king` with `nextTargetPulse` + `nextTargetPulseKing` keyframes. Cache buster `v20260522za`, SW `bloom-v7.7`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Per-board GLOBAL leaderboards (May 2026)** — the social half of the addiction loop, stacked on top of the personal-best layer from the previous commit. Turns "🏆 שיא 47K" (me vs me) into "🏆 47K · #14 מתוך 87 · 👑 דניאל: 89K" (me vs everyone). **Schema**: new `dynamic_board_scores` table in [schema.sql](schema.sql) — PK `(board_id, device_id)`, FK to `board_configurations(id)` with ON DELETE CASCADE so deleting an admin board cleans up its scores. Best-score-wins upsert mirroring `daily_scores`. `idx_dynamic_board_scores_board_score` for fast top-N queries. **Server**: 3 new endpoints in [server.js](server.js): `POST /api/boards/:id/score` (requireDeviceAuth, 60/hr rate limit, drops-required + challengeDropsImplausible anti-cheat, returns `{rank, total, score}` for the over-screen rank pill); `GET /api/boards/:id/leaderboard` (top 50 + my rank); `/api/boards/available` enriched with one JOIN to return `leader_name`, `leader_score`, `leader_tier`, `players` per board. **Client picker chips** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `👑 דניאל: 89K` (pink-gradient leader chip) OR `👑 אתה מוביל!` (gold-pink pulsing king chip when the player's local best ≥ leader_score) PLUS `👥 47 שיחקו` social-proof chip. **In-game leader chip** in the mode-bar subtitle ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) renders side-by-side with the personal-best chip. `bumpScore()` swaps the leader chip to a pulsing gold-pink `👑 חצית את המוביל! +2,408` when score crosses the global leader's number — fires `soundMilestone(6)` + `buzz([60,60,60,60,100])` ONCE (dedup'd via `dataset.celebrated`). **Game-over rank pill** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css)): renders an instant `⏳ מחשב דירוג בלוח…` placeholder, then the POST response patches the `#over-board-rank-host` with the real label: `👑 מקום ראשון בלוח X!` (king variant: pulsing gradient) / `🏆 #2 מתוך 87 · עברת 99% מהשחקנים` / `⭐ #5 מתוך 87 · עברת 95%` / `🎯 #18 מתוך 87` (tiered emoji by rank). Submit is fire-and-forget — the personal-best feedback paints instantly, the global-rank pill slots in 200-400ms later with no UI jank. Cache buster `v20260522z`, SW `bloom-v7.6`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Per-board personal best loop (May 2026)** — the strongest single addiction engine in the dynamic-boards system. Each board now has its own localStorage best record so the player chases their own score per-board, not just the global daily best. Three visible surfaces: **(1) Picker card chip** — `🏆 שיא 47K` (gold gradient) when the player has a record, `🌱 חדש לך` (mint gradient) when this board is unplayed. Drives "be the first / beat your last" psychology side-by-side. **(2) In-game target chip** in the mode-bar subtitle — `🏆 לעבור: 47,392` in soft gold. The chip is live: when `score > target` mid-game, `bumpScore()` swaps it to a pink-orange pulsing `👑 עברת את עצמך! +2,408` + plays `soundMilestone(4)` + `buzz([40,40,80])` for immediate gameplay-time feedback (not just on game-over). The +N overage updates live as score grows. **(3) Game-over banner** — three variants in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `render({over:true})`: gold-pink pulsing "🏆 שיא חדש ב[שם] +N מעל [prev]" when beating own record, red-pink "😱 כמעט עברת את עצמך! חסר N" when within 85% of best, soft gold "🎯 השיא שלך ב[שם]: N · נסה שוב!" otherwise. Storage: `localStorage[bloom_board_best_<boardId>]` = `{score, tier, ts}` keyed by stable server-issued board id. `setBoardBest()` is monotonic — never overwrites with a lower score. Wired into the dynamic-mode branch of game-over in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js): captures `prevBoardBest` BEFORE writing the new value, passes both to `render()` so the over screen can show the delta. New helpers in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `getBoardBest(id)` / `setBoardBest(id, score, tier)` / `formatBoardScore(n)` (compact "K"/"M" notation for chip space). CSS: `.dyn-boards-chip-best/-pioneer` + `.dyn-target-chip-passed` keyframes + `.over-board-best-up/-near/-target` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css). Cache buster `v20260522y`, SW `bloom-v7.5`.
- ✅ **Dynamic Boards — Phase 6 LiveOps FOMO layer (May 2026)** — closes the 6-phase roadmap. Boards already had `starts_at` / `ends_at` columns + a server-side schedule filter, but neither the home button nor the picker surfaced the urgency, so a player browsing the home screen had no signal that today's special board was hours from disappearing. Three-part fix: (1) [server.js](server.js) `/api/boards/available` now SELECTs `starts_at, ends_at` alongside the existing fields (60s cache is invalidated on any admin write so newly-scheduled boards appear quickly). (2) [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) introduces `boardUrgency(board)` returning `'critical'` (<4h to ends_at) / `'new'` (<24h since starts_at) / `'soon'` (<24h to ends_at) / `'normal'` / `'expired'`; `pickFocusBoard(boards)` ranks critical > new > soon. `updateDynamicBoardsButton()` rewrites the home button label every time it runs: `🔥 ולנטיין מסתיים בעוד 4ש 12ד` (critical), `🆕 חנוכה — חדש היום` (new), `⏰ פסח — נשאר 6ש 22ד` (soon), else the vanilla count. A 60s `setInterval` (`startFomoTick` / `stopFomoTick`) re-runs the update + re-renders any open picker — torn down in `hideHomeV2()` via `window.stopDynamicBoardsTick` so detached DOM doesn't keep ticking. (3) Picker cards: each card gets a per-board FOMO badge via `renderFomoBadge(board)` — `🔥 מסתיים בעוד 3ש 22ד` (pulsing red gradient w/ box-shadow), `🆕 חדש היום · עד 25/5` (mint pulse), `⏰ נשאר 18ש 04ד` (warm orange static), `📅 עד 25/5` (subtle calendar pill for non-urgent boards with an end date). `refreshPickerTimers()` updates only the badge hosts on each tick — keeps scroll/focus intact. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.dyn-fomo-pill-{critical,new,soon,cal}` + `@keyframes dynFomoPulseCritical/New` + `.dyn-boards-card.fomo-critical` with `dynBoardCardCritical` border breathing + `.home-v2-boards.fomo-{critical,new,soon}` gradient backgrounds matching urgency. Cache buster `v20260522x`, SW `bloom-v7.4`. Dynamic Boards roadmap is now complete on all 6 phases.
- ✅ **Themed-board UX fix — preview + auto-default + empty-board guard (May 2026)** — user-reported: clicked a board name in the home picker, saw no visual change. Diagnosis via `curl /api/boards/available`: board #3 named "בונוס" had `{type:"themed", definition:{cells:[]}}` — a fully empty themed board with no theme_id, no shape_id, no cells. The admin had selected type='themed' but didn't pick a theme from the dropdown, so saving produced a no-op definition that `applyBoardToSession` correctly applied nothing for. Four-part fix: (1) [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) `onBoardTypeChange()` now auto-sets `board-theme-id` to `'valentine'` when type changes to 'themed' and the picker is empty — instant visible feedback, no silent empty saves. (2) New `refreshThemedPreview()` + `<div id="board-themed-preview">` host renders a live 4×6 mini-grid in the admin editor with the actual theme palette + shape voids + cell emoji as the admin edits — admin sees EXACTLY what the player will see before clicking save. Wired into `onchange` of theme/shape selects, `oninput` of board-name, click of cells-grid, plus on editor open. (3) `saveBoard()` validation: refuses to save when `type === 'themed'` AND `!theme_id` AND `!shape_id` AND `!cells.length` with an explicit Hebrew error "⚠ לוח חג ריק — בחר לפחות ערכה / צורה / תאים מיוחדים" — root-causes the original bug. (4) [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) picker overhaul: per-card theme tint background (matches `body.theme-X-active` hue from boards.css), plus a chip row showing `💕 ולנטיין` / `❤️ לב` / `✨×2` etc. so the player can tell themed boards apart before clicking. New CSS `.dyn-boards-chip` + variants `-theme/-shape/-cell` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). Cache buster `v20260522w`, SW `bloom-v7.3`.
- ✅ **Contest leave actually leaves (May 2026)** — user-reported: "נתק ממכשיר זה" (the leave button on a contest's leaderboard) only cleared `localStorage` and called `clearContestGameState` / `clearContestDisplayName` / `invalidateMyContestsCache`. The `contest_scores` DB row was untouched, so the next page refresh hit `/api/contests/mine`, the row came back, and the contest reappeared in the "my contests" list — making the leave button look broken. Fixes: (a) [schema.sql](schema.sql) adds `ALTER TABLE contest_scores ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS left_at TIMESTAMPTZ` (idempotent); (b) new `POST /api/contests/:code/leave` endpoint in [server.js](server.js) sets `left_at = NOW()` for the device's row (soft-leave preserves the score on the contest's own leaderboard — matching the existing confirm copy "הציון נשמר בלוח") + cleans up `contest_live_state` and `contest_watchers` rows so the player doesn't linger as a live spectator-target after leaving, with a 30/hour rate-limit; (c) `/api/contests/mine` now filters `WHERE cs.left_at IS NULL`; (d) `/api/contests/:code/join` clears `left_at` in its UPSERT's DO UPDATE clause so re-joining via the code resumes the existing row with the score intact; (e) [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `clb-leave` handler awaits `apiPost('/api/contests/<code>/leave', {})` BEFORE the local cleanup so the row is flagged before the next `/mine` fetch. Cache buster `v20260521l`, SW `bloom-v5.1`.
- ✅ **Bonus-tile leak + reward number trust fix (May 2026)** — two user-reported bugs in one batch. **(1) Event overlay leaking onto home.** The "force first event" `setTimeout(spawnRandomEvent, 3000)` in `startEventSystem` was untracked and survived `stopEventSystem`. When a player entered the game and bounced back to home within 3s, the timeout fired, `spawnRandomEvent` found `grid` still populated, and `renderEventOnCell` built a `position:fixed` overlay at the cell's viewport coords — which on a desktop browser sits OUTSIDE the centered 380px `.app` column and visibly floated next to the home card with its `2.0s` countdown. Fixes in [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js): (a) `eventInitTimer` is now tracked + cleared by `stopEventSystem`; (b) a new `eventSystemRunning` flag gates every async callback (interval + init timeout) so a tick that fires between stop and clear early-returns; (c) new `isGameSurfaceVisible()` (false when `#home-screen` / `#contest-screen` / `#challenge-screen` / `#spectator-screen` is mounted) guards `trySpawnEvent`, `spawnRandomEvent`, AND `renderEventOnCell`; (d) `renderEventOnCell` additionally refuses to mount if the cell center sits OUTSIDE the `.app` bounding rect — belt-and-suspenders for any future menu that forgets to call stop; (e) new `purgeEventOverlays()` nukes `#event-drop-overlay` + `.fx-overlay` elements, invoked from both `showHome` and `showHomeV2` after `stopEventSystem`; (f) window resize / orientationchange now repositions the overlay (or purges if no surface). **(2) Daily login reward mismatch.** The reward overlay teased a streak-tiered amount (25 → 50 → 100 → 200 by streak day) via `getDailyRewardAmount`, but `earnCredits('daily_login')` paid a flat `daily_login_reward` config — currently `15` in prod after the 2026-05-17 economy migration (schema.sql line 609). So a returning player saw "+25 💎" in the overlay and a "+15 💎" toast pop up. Fixes: (a) [schema.sql](schema.sql) adds tiered keys `daily_login_reward_streak_3` (50), `_streak_7` (100), `_streak_30` (200) — all `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`; (b) [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn` now picks the tier when `action === 'daily_login'`, reading `meta.streak` (clamped 1..400) — dedup is still one claim/device/day so the worst-case forged-streak payout is bounded by the 200💎 ceiling; (c) [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js) `showDailyLoginReward` resolves the tier from boot-cached `gameConfig`, picks `Math.max(displayReward, srvVal)` as `resolvedReward`, runs the slot reel on that value, and passes `meta: { streak: displayStreak }` to `earnCredits` so the wallet matches; (d) [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) `showCreditToast` gains `daily_login: '🎁 בונוס יומי'` + `comeback: '👋 ברוך שובך!'` labels. **(3) Score-milestone tier credibility (audit catch).** Same family of bug: milestone banners showed 2/3/5/10/20/50 but the call routed through `event_gift` which is server-clamped to `[event_gift_credits_min, event_gift_credits_max]` AND rate-limited to 30s — so back-to-back milestones during a chain reaction silently dropped, and the displayed number lied. Fixes: (a) client switched from `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount, milestone})` → `earnCredits('score_milestone', {milestone})` — uses per-milestone dedup, no rate-limit; (b) 200K renamed to 250K to match the server's `ALLOWED_MILESTONES` allowlist and a new 1M tier added; (c) server [server.js](server.js) reads `score_milestone_reward_<at>` per-tier with the flat `score_milestone_reward` as fallback; (d) [schema.sql](schema.sql) seeds the 7 tier keys mirroring `SCORE_MILESTONES` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) — 2/3/5/10/25/50/100. Cache buster `v20260521k`, SW `bloom-v5.0`.
- ✅ **Contest scoring overhaul + clarity pass (May 2026)** — multi-part work driven by user feedback that the contest UX was confusing and not addictive enough.
  1. **HUD redesign — absolute scores everywhere.** The previous HUD displayed deltas in the target/chaser score positions ("הדס 4,194" = my lead over her). As I scored, that number grew, which read as "Hadas is gaining points!" instead of "my lead is growing". Bad. New layout in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `paintContestHud`: every side shows the **player's actual total** in the big number; a small delta line below with `↑ N לעקוף` (target) or `↓ N לפניך` (chaser) provides the contextual gap with explicit labels. Three rows in each side: name → absolute score → delta. Zero ambiguity.
  2. **Score mode toggle — cumulative vs best-of.** New `score_mode` column on `contests` ('cumulative' default, 'best' alternative). [Server.js](server.js) `POST /api/contests` accepts `scoreMode` body param; `POST /api/contests/:code/score` branches the upsert reducer between `contest_scores.score + EXCLUDED.score` (cumulative) and `GREATEST(contest_scores.score, EXCLUDED.score)` (best). `GET /api/contests/:code` returns `score_mode` with a 'cumulative' fallback for any pre-migration row. Client: new pill picker in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `showCreateContestForm` (🧮 מצטבר / 🏆 הכי גבוה) with a hint line that updates per choice. HUD's projection logic respects mode — best-of uses `Math.max(p.score, myLiveScore)` instead of summing — so the displayed rank reflects "if I lock in this game" under either rule. Leaderboard scoring-note badge swaps between the two modes ("🏆 הכי גבוה — רק המשחק הטוב ביותר נספר" vs "🧮 ניקוד מצטבר — כל משחק מצטרף לסך הכל"). HUD's mode-label line under my score becomes "אתה · 🏆 הכי גבוה" when active so the rule is always glanceable.
  3. **Home resume-game card.** Mid-game contest state was already saved on `beforeunload`/`visibilitychange`/per-drop, but after a refresh the user landed on home with no surfaced indication that a paused game existed — they had to navigate back to the contest manually to find the "שחק עכשיו" button (which silently restored the game). [src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) `renderHeroBannerV2` now checks `findPausedContestGame()` FIRST (highest-priority hero) and renders a clickable card: "⏸ המשך משחק בתחרות [name] · ניקוד: N · נשמר לפני 4 דק׳". Tap → `setActiveContest` + `init('contest')` restores grid/score/nextPiece. Stale runs (>12h old) get a softer "⏱ יש משחק ישן מושהה" treatment but still resume on tap. New helper `findPausedContestGame()` in [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js) iterates every `bloom_contest_state_*` key, returns the freshest valid one, and opportunistically GCs entries past the TTL.
  Cache buster `v20260521j`, SW `bloom-v4.9`.
- ✅ **Spectator render fix + HUD teardown (May 2026)** — user-reported: clicking a live row to spectate showed the spectator header + control buttons but a blank space where the live board should be. Root cause in [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css): `.spectator-grid > .grid` inherited the game's `.grid { display:grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(4, 1fr); grid-template-rows: repeat(6, 1fr) }` rules, which the in-game grid sizes at runtime via `fitGrid()` — the spectator grid never gets that treatment, so `1fr` resolved to 0 and the 24 cells collapsed to 0×0 (invisible). Fix: explicit `width: min(280px, 80vw); aspect-ratio: 4/6; margin: 0 auto` on the spectator grid + smaller SVG (`60%`) inside the cells to match the reduced cell size. Same issue had been silently broken for any contest entered via the contest-screen entry point (not just the new HUD's expand button). Also in [src/10-spectator.js](src/10-spectator.js) `startSpectator()`: tear down the in-game contest HUD on spectate (it shows MY rank + targets, which is irrelevant + visually distracting while I'm watching someone else); `stopSpectator()`'s mid-game-resume branch already calls `init('contest')` which remounts the HUD cleanly. Cache buster `v20260521i`, SW `bloom-v4.8`.
- ✅ **Contest HUD bugfix pass (May 2026)** — two user-reported issues with the brand-new in-game contest HUD:
  1. **"המספרים לא אמיתיים"** — the displayed score, rank, and target/chaser gaps came from two different totals. The 400ms tick wrote just the current game's `score` into the score element, while the 5s paint computed rank + gaps against `accumulated + score`. So the HUD's "10,546" was visually inconsistent with the "−90,412 to overtake X" derived from a totally different number. Fix in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js): the tick now caches the most recent `players` list in `_contestHudCachedPlayers` and re-runs the full `paintContestHud` on every 400ms beat — one render path, one source of truth for all three numbers. The displayed score is now the **projected total** (accumulated + current game), matching what the rank and gap calculations use. Also removed the confusing `−` prefix on the gap (the absolute number reads as "this many points to close"; the prefix made the intent ambiguous).
  2. **"שלוחצים שוב זה לא מחזיר למשחק"** — tapping ⤢ on the HUD opened the leaderboard but the back arrow routed to home or contest-menu, leaving the in-progress game inaccessible without re-entering the contest from the home screen. Fix: new cross-call flag `_contestHudJustOpenedLb` set by the HUD's ⤢ handler and consumed by the next `showContestLeaderboard` mount. When set: (a) shell subtitle becomes "⏸ המשחק שלך מושהה" (so the player knows the game is paused not abandoned), (b) the back arrow calls `init('contest')` which restores from the state saved by the HUD's `saveContestGameState()` call, (c) a prominent green "↩ חזור למשחק שלך" primary CTA renders at the top of the form area, (d) the existing "שחק עכשיו" button gets relabeled "התחל משחק חדש" and styled as secondary, and crucially calls `init('contest', { fresh: true })` so it wipes the saved state instead of resuming it. Cache buster `v20260521h`, SW `bloom-v4.7`.
- ✅ **Contest live HUD — in-game opponent widget (May 2026)** — until now contest gameplay had no ambient signal showing where you stood: scores updated silently on a separate leaderboard screen, and the only mid-game feedback was the transient `showContestAlert` toast (fires only on threshold events). Mirroring the duel-HUD pattern, new `startContestHud(code)` / `stopContestHud()` / `paintContestHud(players)` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) mount a `.contest-hud` pill at the top of the viewport whenever `init('contest')` runs. Three-column layout: **לעקוף ⚔️** (player above me, with `−1,234` gap in pink) · **אתה** (large gold score + `#3 / 47` rank pulse) · **רודף 👀** (player below me, with `+800` lead in mint). Tap `⤢` → saves contest state via `saveContestGameState()` + `stopLivePush()` then opens the full leaderboard via `showContestLeaderboard` (same pause/resume pattern as the existing exit-game flow). Data refresh: 5s `fetchContest` poll + 400ms local `score` tick — opponent scores reflect their actual heartbeat between my drops, my own number updates instantly between merges. **Live-rank projection**: paint logic recomputes ranking locally by substituting my live `score` for what the server has on `cs.score+ls.live_score` (server hasn't seen my in-flight game yet). So the rank shown isn't "where I am now" — it's "where I'd be if I locked in this score this second", which is the projection that turns "where do I stand?" into "if I keep this up I overtake דניאל". Rank-up = gold pulse + scale-up keyframe, rank-down = pink pulse + scale-down. Lifecycle: mounts via `init('contest')` block (alongside `startOvertakeWatch`), tears down on game-over (both branches in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)), on mode switch (init's else branch), and on `hideContestScreens()` (so navigating to leaderboard via the HUD itself doesn't leave a stale floating widget). Cache buster `v20260521g`, SW `bloom-v4.6`.
- ✅ **Smart contest leaderboard (May 2026)** — the contest board ([src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js)) used to render every participant in a flat scroll-wall; with 50+ players that meant "where do I stand?" was lost in noise and the most-addictive comparisons (just above/below me) were invisible without scrolling. New layout, gated by player count:
  - **≤ 12 players** — flat list, unchanged (no value from sectioning small contests).
  - **> 12 players (compact view, default)** — `🏆 המובילים` section with top 5, then if I'm rank ≥6 a `📍 המיקום שלך · #N מתוך M` section with me + 2 neighbors above and 2 below, separated by a `· · ·` divider. Bottom CTA: `הצג את כל N השחקנים` (gold-on-black gradient pill).
  - **Expanded view** — every row shown flat. If `> 20` players a search input also appears (`חיפוש לפי שם…`, 140ms debounced; focus + caret preserved across the 20s silent refresh so typing isn't eaten). Top-of-list `⌃ חזרה לתצוגה קומפקטית` to fold back. Expand scrolls MY row to viewport center.
  - **Top-3 podium** — `🥇 🥈 🥉` medal glyphs in the rank circle (instead of digits), plus subtle silver/bronze background tints on rows 2/3 to match the existing gold on row 1.
  - **Persistent "next target" pill** — under MY row, a pulsing gold pill: `⚔️ עוד 1,234 כדי לעקוף את [name]`. The most-addictive moment in any leaderboard is "I can take them in one game" — this is now ambient rather than waiting for the periodic `refreshOvertake` poll to fire a transient banner.
  - **Search smart-ranking** — filtered rows keep their real contest rank (mapped via `players.indexOf`) so a search for "דני" doesn't collapse the matches to "1, 2, 3" and lose context.
  Architecture: `renderContestSmartBoard(players)` is the single entry point now used by both `showContestLeaderboard` (mount) and `refreshContestBoardSilently` (every 20s tick). Row-level `renderContestBoardRows(players, allPlayers, startIdx)` got a new signature: `allPlayers` keeps leader-relative deltas correct on slices, and `startIdx` keeps rank numbers truthful. Module-level state (`contestBoardExpanded`, `contestBoardSearchTerm`) resets on each mount so a stale search from a previous contest visit can't filter the new list to "no results". New CSS in [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) + dark-mode overrides in [public/css/dark.css](public/css/dark.css). Cache buster `v20260521f`, SW `bloom-v4.5`.
- ✅ **One-tap duel rematch (May 2026)** — every terminal-state row in the "הדו-קרבות שלי" list inside the duel modal now carries a gold `⚔️ שוב` button that re-opens the duel modal pre-filled with the opponent's 4-char BLOOM suffix. Closes the loop: a finished duel → 1 tap → ready to send a fresh challenge with the difficulty/wager re-chosen. Implemented in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `loadMyDuels` (gates on `status ∈ {settled, tie, declined, expired}` so in-progress rows still show their existing accept/play/decline buttons) + new `window.rematchDuel(suffix)` global that closes the current duel modal and calls `showDuelModal({prefillSuffix})`. The flex row layout was tightened (`display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap`) so the rematch pill doesn't push other actions off the right edge on narrow phones. Retention rationale: the duels list is effectively your personal opponent leaderboard — surfacing a one-tap rematch turns it into the closest thing BLOOM has to a "play again with the same person" loop, which is the most addictive social pattern in multiplayer casual games. Cache buster `v20260521e`, SW `bloom-v4.4`.
- ✅ **Duel score visibility fix (May 2026)** — user-reported bug: when finishing a duel as the SECOND player (so the duel settled immediately on the server), the result overlay rendered "vs ..." instead of the opponent's actual score. Root cause: `POST /api/duels/:id/score` settle path returned only `{ok, result, winner, prize}` — `opponentScore` was missing, so the client's `(d && d.opponentScore) ? ... : '...'` fell through. The polling path (`pollDuelUntilSettled` — only used when *I* finished first) already passed `opponentScore`, which is why this only repro'd as a second-player. Fix in [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/duels/:id/score`: settled + tie responses now also include `yourScore: s, opponentScore: isChallenger ? u.opponent_score : u.challenger_score`. Same-batch hardening in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js): (a) overlay's `oppScore` guard switched from truthy `?:` to `!= null` so a legitimate opponent score of 0 still renders; (b) the duel notification banner (cross-session "you won/lost" surfacing in `showDuelNotificationBanner`) now appends `· 77,445 vs 60,000` to the sub-line; (c) "my duels" list rows (`loadMyDuels`) now render the full score-vs-score on every settled/tie row, not just "ניצחת!/הפסדת". Cache buster `v20260521d`, SW `bloom-v4.3`.
- ✅ **Duel/event UX fixes (May 2026)** — four user-reported bugs addressed in one batch:
  1. **Explosion FX invisible/delayed**: `triggerBomb` / `triggerFreeze` used to set `cell.style.background` for a 400ms flash, but `render()` ran immediately after with `gridEl.innerHTML = ''` — wiping the inline style before paint. New approach: `fxAtCell()` spawns a `position:fixed` overlay in `<body>` (`.fx-overlay.fx-explode`, `.fx-overlay.fx-freeze`) that lives independently of the grid DOM. Bomb explosions stagger outward from the center (distance × 55ms delay) to read as a real blast. **Plus**: `triggerEvent()` now fires BEFORE `processChains()` in `drop()` — previously a long chain pushed the explosion 1-2s late.
  2. **No notifications for incoming duels**: New `checkIncomingDuels()` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) polls `/api/duels/mine` on boot + every 60s + on `visibilitychange`. Shows a top-of-screen banner (`showDuelNotificationBanner`) for: (a) pending duels where I'm the opponent, (b) settled duels with results I haven't seen. De-duped per session via `sessionStorage[bloom_seen_duel_notifications]`. Tap → opens duel modal.
  3. **Challenger had to refresh to play**: `POST /api/duels` now returns the full duel row, and the client auto-calls `startDuelGame()` 600ms after creation (no more waiting for the opponent). Server-side, `POST /api/duels/:id/score` now accepts submissions while status is `'pending'` OR `'accepted'` — settlement triggers as soon as both scores exist regardless of accept order.
  4. **Opponent score never shown on game-over**: `submitDuelScore` checks for `result === 'waiting'` and starts `pollDuelUntilSettled()` (5s interval, 5 min cap). On settle/tie, `replaceDuelResultOverlay()` swaps the in-flight overlay (tagged `data-duel-result-overlay`) for the final result with the opponent's real score. New `GET /api/duels/:id` endpoint backs this polling.
- ✅ **Player-chosen difficulty per game mode** — five presets (`default`/`easy`/`medium`/`hard`/`insane`) selectable by:
  - **Friends contest**: host picks at creation. Stored on `contests` row (`difficulty_label` / `difficulty_weights` / `difficulty_speed_pct`), inherited by everyone who joins. Form pill in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js).
  - **1v1 duel**: challenger picks. Stored on `duels` row (same 3 columns). Both players get the same setting. Pill picker in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js).
  - **Practice**: player picks for themselves. Stored in `localStorage[bloom_practice_difficulty]`. Inline chip in the mode-bar subtitle (`practice-diff-chip`) opens a modal.
  - **Daily**: NOT player-selectable — admin-only (fairness). Practice scores ALSO STOP submitting to the daily leaderboard when difficulty != default (or when running a duel). Check: `practiceFairForLeaderboard = (mode === 'practice') && !sessionDifficulty && !window._duelMode` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js).
  - Server-side single source of truth: `DIFFICULTY_PRESETS` + `resolveDifficulty(label)` in [server.js](server.js). Frontend mirror in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) (for label/emoji/name display only). The presets are snapshotted onto each contest/duel row at creation, so changing the preset table later never re-balances live contests.
  - Engine integration: `sessionDifficulty` is reset on every `init()` and populated based on mode (practice from localStorage, contest from `activeContestData.*`, duel from the duel row passed into `startDuelGame`). `getDropWeights()` and `gameSpeedScale()` check `sessionDifficulty` BEFORE the admin global `gameConfig`. Daily stays uniform because its `init()` branch never touches `sessionDifficulty`.
- ✅ **Admin difficulty / speed / slot machine controls** — three new tunables in `game_config`. **Drop pool**: `drop_weights` is a comma-separated list of 8 weights (tiers 1..8). The frontend `WEIGHTS` constant is fallback-only; `getDropWeights()` reads from `gameConfig.drop_weights`. All-zero falls back to default. Admin section ships with 5 presets (default 55/28/12/5/0/0/0/0, easy, medium, hard, insane) + 8 sliders with live `%` calculation. **Game speed**: `game_speed_pct` (50-200) multiplies every gameplay sleep via `gsleep(ms)` wrapping `sleep()` in `src/11-game.js`. **Slot machine**: `slot_enabled` / `slot_duration_ms` (200-2000) / `slot_intensity` (1-8) replace the old 4-tier sweep in `revealNextTier`. Default: 3 passes through tiers 1..8 over 650ms with ease-in-quad deceleration + 380ms bounce-up landing animation (`.tier-cell.slot-landed` keyframes in [public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css)). Cost-aware via `revealToken` bail-out for fast tappers.
- ✅ **Layout regression fix + engine self-test (May 2026)** — practice-mode subtitle ("ברירת מחדל ⌄ · תתחרה על לוח המובילים 🏆") was wrapping to two lines on narrow phones, inflating the mode-bar height by ~14px. `fitGrid()` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js#L1059) is height-bound on tall-narrow viewports, so every lost pixel translates to ~1px off each cell × all 6 rows — users saw smaller board cells AND smaller tier-bar tiles (the tier-bar shares fitGrid's width budget). Two fixes: (1) compacted the subtitle to a single line by replacing the long "תתחרה על לוח המובילים 🏆" sentence with a small 🏆 (or ⊘ when difficulty != default) icon next to the chip — tooltip on hover keeps the full meaning accessible; (2) added `white-space: nowrap; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis;` to `.mode-title` and `.mode-sub` in [public/css/home.css](public/css/home.css) so future copy can't silently re-trigger the bug. Added engine diagnostics: `?debug=1` URL param turns on `[drop]`/`[merge]`/`[gravity]` console logs with compact `serializeGrid()` snapshots; `__bloomDumpGrid()` and `__bloomLayoutLog` are exposed for one-off devtools queries; `[fitGrid]` is logged on every render (cell px, width/height-bound, mode-bar height, viewport). Built [scripts/test_engine.mjs](scripts/test_engine.mjs) — runs 500 games × 100 drops asserting the gravity invariant after every step. Found a backwards invariant in v1; corrected v2 passes 41,242 drops / 26,557 merges / 16 crown tiles / 0 floating-tile bugs. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517q`.
- ✅ **Bot mode expansion + admin leaderboard surgery (May 2026)** — three coordinated changes:
  1. **Bots now play every mode**: [bot-engine.js](bot-engine.js) accepts `mode: 'duel'` and `mode: 'challenge'` in addition to the existing practice/daily/contest. Duel mode pairs finishing bots into real rows in the `duels` table (challenger/opponent both bots, status 'settled' or 'tie', synthetic `opponent_code` like `BOT-XXXX`). Challenge mode resolves the admin-provided slug → `challenges.id`, then INSERTs a `completed` row into `challenge_entries` with a score-derived `drops_count` so the cheat heuristic doesn't auto-flag. The pre-existing `daily_scores` INSERT was broken (used non-existent `display_name`/`highest_tier`/`games_played`/`drops_count` columns) — fixed to use the real schema `(date, device_id, name, score, tier)`. Every bot already heartbeats every 5s with `grid_json` so they're spectatable via `/?watch=DEVICE_ID` and visible in admin live view.
  2. **Per-row leaderboard deletion**: new admin endpoints `DELETE /api/score/:date/:deviceId` (daily_scores → cascades through day/week/month leaderboard windows) and `DELETE /api/contest-score/:code/:deviceId` (contest_scores + contest_live_state). Wired with 🗑 buttons in the "ניקודים מובילים" table and a new "👁 הצג חברים" expander on every contest row that shows full member list with per-entry deletes. Helper endpoint `GET /api/contest/:code/scores` returns up to 200 contest members. Every delete writes to `admin_actions` audit log.
  3. **Version visibility + live bot panel**: new admin endpoint `GET /api/version` reads the cache-buster from `public/index.html`, plus `RAILWAY_GIT_COMMIT_SHA`, node version, and uptime. Surfaced in the header as a monospace `build vXXXX · gitsha · ↑uptime` pill. The bot status panel now shows ALL active bots (not just 8) in a scrollable list with name/tier/games/score, auto-refreshing every 3s, with a toggleable auto-refresh checkbox. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517p`.
- ✅ **Duel live spectator (May 2026)** — when a player finishes a duel before their opponent, the "ממתין ליריב" overlay used to show a static spinner with no insight into the opponent. Now `submitDuelScore()` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js), upon a `result: 'waiting'` response, calls `attachDuelLiveSpectator(duelId, myScore, oppName)` which: (1) GETs `/api/duels/:id` to learn the opponent's device ID, (2) injects a mini live-board widget (`[data-duel-spec-widget]`) into the waiting overlay showing the opponent's name, real-time score, and actual grid using `getActiveTiers()` SVGs, (3) polls `/api/live-state/:opponentDeviceId` (universal endpoint backed by 5s `/api/heartbeat` snapshots) every 1.5s. Self-terminates when the widget DOM is removed (player dismissed overlay) or the duel poller resolves to settled/tie. Settle-poll cadence also tightened from 5s→2s (still 5-min total cap) so the final result lands faster. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517o`. Not a mirror — the opponent's *actual* live game state.
- ✅ **Audio recovery fix (May 2026)** — players who had ever tapped the legacy unified mute button (`bloom_muted=1`) on a pre-volume-slider version were stuck silent forever: `readVolumeKey` in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) treated the legacy flag as authoritative and migrated *both* channels to volume=0. New behavior: only the per-channel legacy keys (`bloom_muted_music`/`bloom_muted_sfx`) are honored on migration; the unified `bloom_muted` is intentionally ignored. After read, the resolved volumes are immediately persisted to the new keys and all legacy keys are cleared so migration runs exactly once. Also fixed: `ensureAudio()` now re-arms `currentTrack` inside the `resume().then(...)` callback (Safari leaves pre-gesture BufferSources scheduled but silent), and a one-shot `pointerdown`/`touchstart`/`keydown` capture-phase listener calls `ensureAudio()` unconditionally on the very first user gesture as a belt-and-suspenders unlock. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517n`.
- ✅ **Admin bonus simulator** — new section in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) "🎁 סימולטור בונוסים" that visually previews every in-game event (💣 bomb, ⭐ star, 🎁 gift, 🔥 fever, ❄️ freeze, 🎯 target). Admin clicks a bonus → it animates on a 4×6 mock board with the same `fx-explode`/`fx-freeze` overlays, banners, confetti, fever bar, and target-glow used in the real game. A persistent gold "טיפ לשימוש" card above the list explains the section's purpose, and the tip pane below the board updates per-bonus with the relevant config keys (`event_bomb_radius`, `event_fever_weight`, etc.) so admins know what to tune in "הגדרות משחק". - ✅ **Scope × time leaderboard (v2, May 2026)** — the day/week/month tabs are now the *secondary* axis. Primary axis is scope: **🌍 עולמי / 🇮🇱 מדינתי / 🎚️ קושי**. Admin controls which scopes appear via `game_config.leaderboard_tabs_enabled` (CSV preserving order; default `"world,country,difficulty"`), plus `leaderboard_default_tab` and `leaderboard_default_difficulty`. Players pick a flag once via a 4-column country-picker modal (`promptForCountry` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) that chains after `promptForName` on first home view, with a "החלף דגל" affordance inside the leaderboard modal for returning users. Country list is a hardcoded Hebrew-labeled set in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) `COUNTRY_LIST` (~55 ISO-3166 alpha-2 codes) — `flagEmoji(cc)` derives the flag glyph from regional-indicator codepoints, so adding a country needs no asset work. Stored in `localStorage[bloom_country]` + `player_profiles.country` (new column) + mirrored onto every `daily_scores`/`difficulty_scores` row at submission time. Difficulty board reads from a new `difficulty_scores` table (PK `date+device_id+difficulty_label`, same "best score wins" upsert + day/week/month windowing as `daily_scores`); practice + duel modes write here via [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `submitPracticeOrDuelScore()` — called from both the chain-continuation and the regular game-over branches. Daily mode is **explicitly excluded** from the difficulty board (admin-controlled fairness — daily seed is uniform). New endpoints: `GET /api/leaderboard/v2?scope=world|country|difficulty&period=day|week|month&difficulty=...&endDate=...&deviceId=...&country=...` (returns `{ list, total, rank, from, to, period, scope, country, difficulty, needsCountry }`), `POST /api/profile/country` (idempotent), `POST /api/score/practice` (with anti-cheat drops-implausibility check matching `/api/score`). Old `/api/leaderboard/range/:period` stays in place for back-compat. New CSS section in [public/css/home.css](public/css/home.css) for `.country-grid` + compact `.lb-period-tabs`/`.lb-diff-tabs` pills + `.lb-flag` inline glyph. Admin section "🏆 טבלאות מובילים" in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) — checkbox-per-tab with ↑↓ reorder, default-tab + default-difficulty dropdowns. Cache buster bumped to `v20260518b`.
- ✅ **Identity + invite UX (May 2026)** — addressed two long-standing pain points around player identity:
  1. **Admin dedup fix**: there were **two duplicate `adminRouter.get('/api/players', ...)` definitions** in [server.js](server.js). Express only ever served the first, which `SELECT`ed from `daily_scores` and had no `player_code` column — so admins saw two "דניאל" rows with no way to tell them apart. Deleted the dead second route; rewrote the active one to LEFT JOIN `player_profiles` and return `player_code`, profile `display_name`, and `country`. Admin search `?q=` now matches on `player_code` too. [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) `loadPlayers()` table now leads with a monospace `BLOOM-XXXX` column + country flag next to the name. Local `flagEmoji(cc)` helper added in admin (regional-indicator codepoint math, no asset work).
  2. **Easier 1v1 invite**: duel modal in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) used to require typing the full `BLOOM-XXXX`. Now the input is split — fixed `BLOOM-` prefix pill (dark, gold text, matches difficulty pills) + 4-char suffix input restricted to the same `A-HJ-NP-Z2-9` alphabet as `generatePlayerCode`. Paste is normalized: `BLOOM-WXYZ` / `bloom-wxyz` / `WXYZ` all become `WXYZ` automatically. A new "הקוד שלי: BLOOM-XXXX 📋" pill at the top of the modal lets a player copy their own code and send it to a friend who will challenge them back.
  3. **Challenge from leaderboard**: in the v2 leaderboard modal ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `renderLbModalBody`), every row whose player has a known BLOOM code now renders a small `⚔️` button and becomes clickable. Tapping closes the modal and reopens the duel modal with the suffix pre-filled (`showDuelModal({ prefillSuffix })`). The codes ride along on each row via a new `LEFT JOIN player_profiles pp ON pp.device_id = best.device_id` inside `/api/leaderboard/v2`.
  4. **Name editing from home**: the home pid pill now shows the player's display name next to their BLOOM code with a `✏️` button. Clicking opens `promptForName(cb, { edit: true })` — a new mode that pre-fills the current name, swaps the title/copy to "עריכת שם", and skips the country-picker chain. Save persists to `localStorage[NAME_KEY]` AND fires `POST /api/profile/name` (new endpoint, 10/hr rate-limit) so the change shows up in admin / leaderboards / duels instantly.
  5. **Auto-sync `display_name` on daily submit**: `POST /api/score` now runs `UPDATE player_profiles SET display_name = $1 WHERE device_id = $2 AND (display_name IS NULL OR display_name <> $1)` right after the `daily_scores` upsert. Guarantees the canonical profile name stays aligned with whatever the player picked on the leaderboard, with no extra round-trip from the client. Cache buster bumped to `v20260518e`, SW `CACHE_NAME` to `bloom-v3.6`.
- ✅ **BLOOM Challenges** — public single-shot prize contests. Four types (`race`, `top_n`, `beat`, `first_to_tier`), admin picks at creation. PK on `(challenge_id, device_id)` enforces "single attempt" at the DB layer. Score-only-grows guard on `/score` heartbeat. Winner slots assigned eagerly under `SELECT FOR UPDATE` for race/first-to-tier (race-safe), on `/complete` for `beat`, on admin `/finalize` for `top_n`. Cheat-flag heuristics: z-score > 3σ AND drops-vs-score sanity table. Frontend mode `'challenge'` (4th mode tab "אתגרים"): no save/load, no reset button, `beforeunload` warning, prize chip floats over the grid, custom result screen with in-line winner contact form. Admin section "אתגרים" — full CRUD with lock-down once entries exist + starts_at passed (only safe fields editable). Helpers added: `cleanSlug`, `challengeDropsImplausible`, `challengeZScore`, `maybeGrabWinnerSlot`. New rate-limit buckets: `challenge:enter` (5/hr), `challenge:score` (600/hr), `challenge:claim` (5/hr).
- ✅ **Admin dashboard — tabbed UX + per-field tooltips (May 2026)** — [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) previously ran 20 sections as one ~3,135-line scroll. Refactored into a sticky **6-tab navigation** at the top: `📊 דשבורד` (KPIs + DAU + funnel + retention + heatmap), `🎮 משחק` (config / difficulty / LB tabs / bonus simulator), `💰 כלכלה` (AdSense / Stripe / diamonds / wager / jackpot), `👥 שחקנים` (gift, bots, top scores, players list), `🏆 תחרויות` (contests + challenges), `🔧 ניטור` (admin guide + live + audit + CSV). DOM order is preserved — each `<section>` is wrapped in `<div class="admin-tab-panel" data-tab="X">` and toggled with `display`. `switchAdminTab()` persists the choice in `localStorage[bloom_admin_active_tab]` and closes any open tooltip. **Per-control tooltips**: the existing `showTip()` system was extended with a new `data-tip-text="HTML"` attribute (in addition to the existing `data-tip="KEY"` lookup) — every save button, slider, toggle, and form field gets its own inline `?` with a focused Hebrew explanation (50 occurrences total). The 42-key game-config table gained a tooltip column backed by a new `TIPS_PER_KEY` dictionary covering every event/shake/wager/referral/diamond/pricing key. `wireTips()` is re-invoked after the config table renders so the new buttons get wired. No backend changes — all existing PATCH `/config/:key` and other endpoints work unchanged; `display:none` keeps hidden panels in the DOM so `getElementById` and `refreshAll()` continue to operate on every section regardless of which tab is active.

- ❌ 6-step interactive tutorial (board intro, first drop, first merge, multi-merge demo, chain, full path to Crown)

`ROADMAP_1.md` still describes these as "shipped" — that doc is **stale**. Trust the code, not the roadmap.
