## 7. APIs and integrations

### Backend routes (server.js)

| Method | Path | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `GET /api/health` | — | `{ ok: true }` |
| `GET /api/flags/game_v2` | `?deviceId&force=v2\|classic&force_key` | **GV.1.** Public. Returns `{ enabled, rollout_pct, variant }`. `variant` is sticky: `enabled=false`→`classic` (kill switch); else `bucket(deviceId)%100 < rollout_pct`→`v2`. `force` honored only with a valid `force_key` (= `V2_FORCE_KEY`, HMAC(ADMIN_PASSWORD,…)). 15s cache, fail-safe classic. |
| `POST /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/flags/game_v2` | `{ enabled, rollout_pct }` (Basic Auth) | **GV.1.** Admin-only write to `feature_flags.game_v2`. Busts the flag cache + audit-logs. The matching admin `GET` also returns `force_key` + ready force-URLs for the panel. |
| `POST /api/score` | `{ date, deviceId, token, name, score, tier, drops, country? }` | Upsert with `WHERE daily_scores.score < EXCLUDED.score` — only higher scores win. **drops is required** (400 missing_drops) and stored on the row. **Hard-token auth** (requireDeviceAuth). Returns `{ ok, rank }`. |
| `GET /api/leaderboard/:date` | `?deviceId=...` | Top 50 for one date. Returns `{ list, total, rank }`. |
| `GET /api/leaderboard/range/:period` | `period ∈ {day,week,month}`, `?endDate&deviceId` | Rolling window (1/7/30 days). Best score per device via `DISTINCT ON (device_id)`. Returns `{ list, total, rank, from, to, period }`. **Kept for back-compat only — frontend uses `/v2`.** |
| `GET /api/leaderboard/v2` | `?scope=world\|country\|difficulty&period=day\|week\|month&difficulty=default\|easy\|medium\|hard\|insane&endDate&deviceId&country` | Unified scope × time leaderboard. `world`/`country` query `daily_scores`; `difficulty` queries `difficulty_scores`. Country tab returns `{ needsCountry: true }` if no country resolved. Each row includes `country` (alpha-2 or null) **and `player_code` (BLOOM-XXXX or null)** so the client can offer "challenge to 1v1" affordances. |
| `POST /api/profile/country` | `{ deviceId, country }` | Persists ISO-3166 alpha-2 (or null = skipped) to `player_profiles.country`. Idempotent. Rate-limit 10/hr. |
| `POST /api/profile/name` | `{ deviceId, name }` | Updates `player_profiles.display_name`. Backs the "✏️ edit name" home pill. Rate-limit 10/hr. |
| `POST /api/score/practice` | `{ date, deviceId, name, score, tier, drops, country, difficulty, source, token }` | "Best score wins" upsert into `difficulty_scores` per `(date, device_id, difficulty_label)`. Source = `'practice'` or `'duel'`. Same anti-cheat drops/score sanity table as `/api/score`. Rate-limit 120/hr. |
| `GET /api/contests/mine` | `?deviceId=...` | All contests the device has joined. Returns `{ ok, contests[] }` with rank, score, games, last-played per contest. |
| `POST /api/contests` | `{ name, hostName, deviceId, durationDays, boardType }` | Create a new contest (rate-limit 5/hour/device). Generates a 6-char code, seeds `host` into `contest_scores`. |
| `GET /api/contests/:code` | `?deviceId=...` | Contest details + leaderboard. Each player row now includes `liveScore`, `liveTier`, `liveUpdatedAt`, `watchers[]`, `hasWatchers` (filtered by `LIVE_FRESH_SECONDS = 10`). Sort key is `cs.score + liveScore` so mid-game players appear at their projected rank. |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/join` | `{ deviceId, displayName }` | Strict name-uniqueness check, then upsert into `contest_scores`. |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/score` | `{ deviceId, displayName, score, tier }` | Submit a finished game (rate-limit 60/hour). `score = contest_scores.score + EXCLUDED.score` — accumulates. Updates `games_played`, `last_played_at`. |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/live-score` | `{ deviceId, displayName, liveScore, tier }` | Heartbeat 1Hz from active player. Upserts `contest_live_state`. Returns `{ ok, hasWatchers, watcherCount }` so the client knows whether to also POST `/live-state`. Rate-limit 120/min. |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/live-state` | `{ deviceId, displayName, liveScore, tier, nextTier, gridJson }` | Same as `/live-score` + writes `grid_json`. Frontend only fires this when previous `/live-score` said `hasWatchers: true`. `gridJson` is a 24-cell array of integers 0-8. Rate-limit 120/min. |
| `GET /api/contests/:code/live-state/:targetDeviceId` | — | Spectator polls this at 1Hz. Returns 404 once `updated_at` is older than 10s (= "the game ended"). |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/watch` | `{ watcherDeviceId, watcherName, watcherLastScore, targetDeviceId }` | Upsert into `contest_watchers`. Acts as both "start" and 5s heartbeat. Rate-limit 60/min. |
| `POST /api/contests/:code/unwatch` | `{ watcherDeviceId, targetDeviceId }` | Best-effort immediate delete. TTL would handle it anyway in ≤10s. |
| `POST /api/ping` | `{ deviceId }` | Upserts today's `device_visits` row, increments `visit_count`. Rate-limit 30/hr. Called fire-and-forget on every page boot. |
| `GET /api/active-board` | — | **Legacy / back-compat.** Returns `{ ok, board: {...} \| null }` — single highest-priority active board. Still served but no longer used by clients (replaced after phase-3 per-mode targeting). |
| `GET /api/active-board/:mode` | `mode ∈ {dynamic,practice,daily,duel,contest,challenge}` | Returns `{ ok, mode, board: {...} \| null }` — highest-priority active board whose `applies_to` includes `:mode`. Per-mode 60s in-memory cache, invalidated on any admin write. Used by `init()` for daily / practice; duel snapshots into the duel row at creation. |
| `GET /api/boards/available` | — | Returns `{ ok, boards: [...] }` — only boards whose `applies_to` includes `'dynamic'` (i.e. the home picker list). Empty list = the home "🎯 לוחות דינמיים" button is hidden. 60s in-memory cache. |
| **Admin Dynamic Boards** | | Under `/<ADMIN_PATH>/api/boards/*` |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/boards` | — | List all board configurations (active first). |
| `POST /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/boards` | `{ name, type, definition, is_active?, starts_at?, ends_at?, target_audience?, priority? }` | Create. `type` must be one of `multipliers \| special_cells \| shape \| themed \| mode \| vip`. `definition` validated per-type (multipliers: array of 4 numbers in [0.5, 20]). Writes audit. |
| `PATCH /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/boards/:id` | Partial update | Same validation as POST. |
| `DELETE /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/boards/:id` | — | Hard delete + audit. |
| **Skin Shop catalog** | | Admin-managed cosmetics |
| `GET /api/skins/available` | — | Returns `{ ok, skins: [...] }` — only enabled rows from `skin_configurations` ordered by sort_order. Each row carries `skin_id`, `name`, `price`, `is_sellable`, `definition`, `special_class`. 60s in-memory cache (`_skinsCache`). Client uses on boot to rebuild `SKIN_PACKS`. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/skins` | — | All skins (incl. disabled) + per-skin `owner_count` LEFT JOIN on `player_skins`. |
| `POST /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/skins` | `{ skin_id, name, price, is_enabled?, is_sellable?, definition, special_class?, sort_order? }` | Create. `skin_id` validated as lowercase `[a-z][a-z0-9_]{1,39}`; `definition.tiers` must be 8 entries each with valid hex/gradient `bg`, hex `fg`, SVG key from the allowlist, name, emoji. 409 `skin_id_taken` if duplicate. |
| `PATCH /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/skins/:id` | Partial update | Same validation as POST except `skin_id` is immutable. Patching `is_enabled=false` hides from shop; `is_sellable=false` keeps it visible but un-buyable. |
| `DELETE /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/skins/:id` | `?force=1` to skip the owners check | 409 `has_owners` if `owner_count > 0` and `force` not set. `force=1` cascades the delete to `player_skins` (lost data for existing owners). |
| **Public Challenges** | | Single-shot prize contests |
| `GET /api/challenges` | `?deviceId` | Active challenges + my entry status. 30s frontend cache. |
| `GET /api/challenges/:slug` | `?deviceId` | One challenge + top-20 standings + my entry. |
| `POST /api/challenges/:slug/enter` | `{deviceId, displayName}` | PK violation → 409. Rate-limit 5/hr. |
| `POST /api/challenges/:slug/score` | `{deviceId, token, score, tier, drops}` | Heartbeat per drop. **drops is required** (400 missing_drops). Race/first-to-tier check winner-slot under `SELECT FOR UPDATE`. Rate-limit 600/hr. **Hard-token auth**. |
| `POST /api/challenges/:slug/complete` | `{deviceId, token, score, tier, drops}` | Locks the entry → 'completed'. **drops is required**. Sets cheat_flag if `challengeDropsImplausible` OR z-score>3. Beat-type assigns winner here. **Hard-token auth**. |
| `POST /api/player/gift` | `{deviceId, token}` | Server-decided gift event. Server rolls jackpot dice (chance from `event_gift_jackpot_chance` config, amount from `event_gift_jackpot_amount`) and pays out atomically. Normal payout `[event_gift_credits_min, event_gift_credits_max]`. 30s rate gate + 20/hr cap. Returns `{ok, reward, isJackpot, newBalance}`. |
| `POST /api/player/ad-watch` | `{deviceId, token, gameId}` | Claim a watch-ad reward. Three layers: per-game dedup (`_ad:<deviceId>:<gameId>` → `already_claimed`), per-day cap (`ad_daily_cap` config, default 5 → `daily_cap`), 30s cooldown via `_ad_rate:<deviceId>` (→ `rate_limited` with `cooldownMs`). Pays `ad_watch_reward` (default 30). Returns `{ok, reward, newBalance, dailyRemaining, dailyCap}`. |
| `GET /api/player/skins` | `?deviceId=...` | List of owned skin IDs from `player_skins` table. Used by client at boot to sync `ownedSkins`. |
| `POST /api/player/skins/declare` | `{deviceId, token, skins[]}` | One-time legacy migration. Idempotent (ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING). Only valid SKIN_PRICES keys are accepted. Rate-limit 3/day. After first success, client sets `bloom_skins_grace_done=1` and never calls again. |
| `POST /api/duels/:id/score` | `{deviceId, token, score, drops}` | **Single-submission guard**: WHERE `(challenger|opponent)_score IS NULL` — second submission returns `{ok:false, reason:'already_submitted'}`. **drops required**. |
| `POST /api/challenges/:slug/claim` | `{deviceId, contactName, contactPhone, contactEmail}` | Winner-only contact form. Phone OR email required. |
| **Admin Challenges** | | All under `/<ADMIN_PATH>/api/`, Basic Auth |
| `GET /challenges` | — | All challenges + entries_count + winners_filled + cheat_count. |
| `POST /challenges` | full create body | Auto-generates slug from name if absent. Status 'draft' unless explicit. |
| `PATCH /challenges/:id` | partial | Lock-down: once entries_count>0 AND starts_at passed, only `name/description/prize_text/prize_image_url/rules_text/ends_at(extend only)/status` editable. |
| `DELETE /challenges/:id` | — | Cascade. |
| `GET /challenges/:id/entries` | — | Full leaderboard with contact info + cheat_flag. |
| `POST /challenges/:id/finalize` | — | Marks in_progress→abandoned, runs top_n winner assignment. |
| `PATCH /challenges/:id/entries/:device_id` | `{is_winner?, cheat_flag?, prize_claimed?}` | Manual override. |
| **Admin (gated by `requireAdmin` middleware — Basic Auth)** | | All under `/<ADMIN_PATH>/api/*` |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/dashboard` | — | KPIs (DAU/WAU/MAU/new/games/contests/D1) + 30-day sparkline + anomaly flag (if DAU < 70% of 7-day avg). |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/retention` | — | 8 weekly cohorts × D1/D7/D30. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/funnel` | `?days=7` | visited / played / completed / returned-next-day buckets. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/heatmap` | `?days=30` | 7×24 game-overs grid in Asia/Jerusalem TZ. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/top-scores` | `?date=YYYY-MM-DD` | Top 50 daily scores with z-score + outlier flag (>3σ). |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/contests` | — | All contests + member counts + top score. |
| `PATCH /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/contest/:code` | `{ name?, endsAt?, status? }` | Edit contest fields. Writes `admin_actions` row. |
| `DELETE /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/contest/:code` | — | Cascade-delete contest. Writes `admin_actions` row. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/players` | `?limit&offset&q` | Paginated player list. **LEFT JOINs `player_profiles`** so each row includes `player_code`, `display_name`, `country` — admins can finally tell two "דניאל" rows apart by BLOOM handle. `q` searches `name`, `device_id`, `player_code`, and profile `display_name`. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/player/:id` | — | Drill-down: scores + contests + visits. |
| `DELETE /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/player/:id` | — | Manual cascade across all tables (no FK to devices). Writes audit. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/audit` | `?limit=100` | Recent `admin_actions` rows. |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/live` | — | Active games + spectators (fresh 30s). |
| `GET /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/export/:table.csv` | — | UTF-8 BOM CSV for `daily_scores`, `contests`, `contest_scores`, `device_visits`, `admin_actions`. |
| `POST /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/privacy/purge` | — | Wipe `contact_name/phone/email` on `challenge_entries` whose prize was claimed >90 days ago. Writes `admin_actions` audit. Also runs automatically every 24h. |

Validation rules (`server.js`):
- `date` must match `^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$`
- `deviceId` 8–64 chars
- `score` / `liveScore` / `watcherLastScore` finite, 0–10,000,000
- `tier` integer 1–8 for `/score` (final), 0–8 for `/live-score` / `/live-state` (fresh boards allowed)
- `gridJson` must parse to an array of exactly 24 integers each in `0..8`
- `name` trimmed and sliced to 24 chars (50 for contest display names); empty → `אנונימי`
- JSON body limit: 4 KB

### Postgres

```sql
CREATE TABLE daily_scores (
  date TEXT NOT NULL,
  device_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  score INTEGER NOT NULL,
  tier INTEGER NOT NULL,
  country VARCHAR(2),        -- ISO-3166 alpha-2; NULL = player skipped
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  PRIMARY KEY (date, device_id)
);
CREATE INDEX idx_daily_scores_lookup ON daily_scores (date, score DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_daily_scores_country ON daily_scores (country, date, score DESC) WHERE country IS NOT NULL;

-- Difficulty leaderboard (practice + duel only — daily is excluded for fairness).
CREATE TABLE difficulty_scores (
  date DATE, device_id, difficulty_label,
  name, score, tier, country, source,    -- source: 'practice' | 'duel'
  created_at, updated_at,
  PRIMARY KEY (date, device_id, difficulty_label)
);

-- Friends contests
CREATE TABLE contests (
  code VARCHAR(8) PRIMARY KEY,
  name, host_name, host_device_id, board_seed, board_type,
  duration_days, ends_at, status, created_at
);

CREATE TABLE contest_scores (
  contest_code FK, device_id, display_name,
  score INTEGER,         -- cumulative across games
  highest_tier, games_played, joined_at, last_played_at,
  UNIQUE (contest_code, device_id)
);

-- Ephemeral: stale rows are filtered out at read time (10s window), not by cron.
-- A best-effort DELETE for rows >1h old runs probabilistically inside POST /live-score.
CREATE TABLE contest_live_state (
  contest_code FK, device_id, display_name,
  live_score, highest_tier, next_tier, grid_json, updated_at,
  PRIMARY KEY (contest_code, device_id)
);

CREATE TABLE contest_watchers (
  contest_code FK, watcher_device_id, watcher_name,
  watcher_last_score, target_device_id, updated_at,
  PRIMARY KEY (contest_code, watcher_device_id, target_device_id)
);
```

`db.js` reads `schema.sql` and runs it on every boot — additions to the schema must remain idempotent (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`, `ALTER TABLE ... ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, etc.).

### External integrations

- **Railway** — hosting + Postgres plugin. Deploy via `railway up --service bloom-web --detach --ci`. `DATABASE_URL` is injected from `${{Postgres-z2RQ.DATABASE_URL}}`. The internal hostname only resolves inside Railway; for local DB work use `DATABASE_PUBLIC_URL`. Two extra env vars unlock the admin dashboard: `ADMIN_PATH` (random URL slug) and `ADMIN_PASSWORD` (long random string). If either is unset, the admin surface is disabled.
- **No Firebase** in the current build, despite older memory entries describing the stack as "Vanilla JS + Firebase" (that's from the SST project; BLOOM uses Postgres on Railway).
- **No AdMob / IAP / analytics SDKs** yet.

---

## 8. Coding style

- Vanilla ES2017+ JS in a single IIFE, split across 13 source files in `src/` and concatenated by `build.sh` into `public/app.js`. `var`/`let`/`const` mixed (mostly `const`/`let`). Plain `function` declarations preferred over arrow functions for top-level helpers.
- Server uses ESM (`"type": "module"` in `package.json`).
- No comments except where the *why* is non-obvious.
- No new dependencies without explicit user approval. Frontend stays dep-free; backend's only deps are `express` and `pg`.
- All inline SVG is embedded as JS strings inside `TIERS[]` and the `SVG` icon map.
- RTL Hebrew is canonical for player-facing copy. Code/identifiers stay in English.
- Use `localStorage` for any state that must survive a page reload. Read-once at boot, write-through on change.
- Async UI sequences use `await sleep(ms)` — keep merge/gravity timing snappy (current cell-merge delay is ~220–280 ms).

---

## 9. Important decisions

- **Single-file frontend.** Do not split `public/index.html` into separate JS/CSS files. The user values "open file, see whole project."
- **No build step.** No bundler, no transpiler, no PostCSS, no Tailwind, no CDN libraries. If you need a polyfill, write it inline.
- **No frontend npm deps.** Backend deps are limited to `express` + `pg`.
- **No Firebase.** Despite older notes, the current backend is Postgres on Railway. Don't introduce Firebase unless the user explicitly asks.
- **One row per device per date.** Re-submissions only update if score improves. Don't change the primary key.
- **Best score wins.** The `WHERE daily_scores.score < EXCLUDED.score` guard in the upsert is intentional — don't replace it with a blind overwrite.
- **DeviceId is anonymous and client-generated.** No login flow. Treat any future auth work as a major design change requiring explicit user signoff.
- **Daily seed is Asia/Jerusalem time.** Do not switch to UTC or to user-local time without explicit approval — the leaderboard's fairness depends on every player getting the same daily seed.
- **Schema migrations must be idempotent** — `schema.sql` runs on every boot.
- **Retention beats revenue (for now).** Suggest features that drive return visits over monetization until the user signals otherwise.

---

## 10. What should NOT be changed

Treat the following as load-bearing. If a task seems to require touching any of them, surface the trade-off and ask before proceeding:

1. The IIFE architecture of the frontend JS. Source lives in `src/*.js`, built into `public/app.js` via `build.sh`. Don't edit `public/app.js` or `public/styles.css` directly.
2. The 4×6 grid dimensions and 8-tier ladder.
3. The chain multiplier ladder (×1, ×1.5, ×2, ×2.5, ×3) — touching it would invalidate every recorded leaderboard entry. The tier-weighted score formula `tier × 10 × (1 + (tier-1)*0.3) × group_size × chain` IS tunable (it was rebalanced from the original linear `tier × 10 × group × chain` in the score-economy update — see §11) but the chain ladder is load-bearing.
4. The Asia/Jerusalem daily-seed contract.
5. `daily_scores` primary key (`date, device_id`) and the "score must improve" upsert guard.
6. The anonymous-only identity model.
7. The Hebrew RTL UI direction.
8. The inline SVG icon set and tier color palette (don't swap art casually).
9. The no-build, no-framework, no-CDN rule.
10. `idx_daily_scores_lookup` — leaderboard queries depend on it.

---

## 10b. UX gate — 5 questions every new surface MUST pass (auto-applied)

This is a **standing rule, applied automatically**, even when the user doesn't explicitly ask for a UX review. The prime directive is "המשחק חייב להיות ממכר" — and after 48+ shipped retention stages, the biggest threat to addiction is **UI overload**, not missing features. Every new modal / banner / tile / button / floating widget / overlay must pass all 5 questions before shipping. If any answer is "no" or "not sure" — redesign or hold back.

**The 5 questions** (must answer YES to all):

1. **Does it add to the next session?** — Will the player be more likely to return tomorrow because this surface exists today? If it only serves this one session, it's noise.
2. **Does the player understand it in <3 seconds?** — Without reading docs, without prior context, without thinking. A new player landing on it should know what to do.
3. **Does it not cover something more important?** — Stage 35 home variants + Stage 39 Priority Calmer exist precisely because we hit overload. New surface must not steal attention from a higher-emotion signal (streak-danger > trophy-claim > rivalry-behind > free-spin > daily-deal > passive tiles).
4. **Is there ONE clear way to close it?** — ESC + visible close button (≥40px, with label, not just an icon) + backdrop tap. The global TC.1 ESC handler covers `[class*="modal-overlay"]` + the curated full-screen views (`#contest-screen`, `#challenge-screen`, `#spectator-screen`). NEW full-screen views must be added to the selector in `src/04-ui-utils.js` `__bloomGetCloseableModals()`.
5. **Is it visible ONLY when relevant?** — Empty board → no boosters / no "claim" badges / no "buy" prompts. First-time player (level < 5) → JIT-unlock gates everything advanced. After game-over → strips that need an in-progress game (booster strip, etc.) get torn down. Mode-specific surfaces (e.g. dynamic-board picker) must not appear in daily/contest/duel.

**What this rule replaces**: dozens of after-the-fact UX fixes. Each post-ship "user reported X doesn't make sense" carries a real retention cost — a confused player leaves. The 5 questions are the pre-ship filter that prevents that loss.

**When the user says "find similar problems"**: this is the lens. Walk every visible surface (home, in-game header, mode-bar, picker, all modals, all banners, all floating widgets) and check each against the 5. Surface failures get fixed in the same sprint.

---

## 11. Current progress

- **v1 core gameplay** — shipped.
- **v2 daily challenge + Postgres leaderboard** — shipped (single-day API + day/week/month modal).
- **v3 sound + mute** — shipped (Web Audio synth only; no MP3 music in current build).
- **v3a layout polish** — recent commits (`4236be2`, `1c3565a`) fixed scrollable game-over, modal layering above the viewport, and score-area clipping.
- **Auto-play bot (dev-only)** — `public/bot.js`, loaded inertly from `index.html` and gated by `?bot=1` (auto-start) or `?botui` (panel only). Talks to the game via `window.BloomDebug` (exposed at the tail of the IIFE: `ready/getGrid/getCurrentPiece/getScore/getHighestTier/isGameOver/isBusy/drop/restart`). No effect on normal users; used for testing and recording.
- **Tier-ladder next-piece indicator** — replaced the single-tile `הבא:` preview with a horizontal row of all 8 tier icons (rock → crown) plus per-tile merge-points beneath each. The currently-chosen piece is scaled up with a colored glow ring; its score un-fades to the tile color. After each drop a silent ~500 ms left-to-right cycle across tiers 1-4 settles on the chosen piece (teaching device, no audio). Helpers: `buildTierBar`, `highlightNextTier`, `revealNextTier`, `rollNextPiece`.
- **Admin dashboard + visit tracking + demo seeder** — single-file `admin/index.html` (vanilla, no build), gated by `ADMIN_PATH` (URL slug) + `ADMIN_PASSWORD` (Basic Auth). New routes under `/<ADMIN_PATH>/api/*` for dashboard / retention / funnel / heatmap / top-scores / contests / players / audit / live / CSV export. New tables `device_visits` (fed by `/api/ping`) and `admin_actions` (audit log). `scripts/seed_demo.js` fakes 30 players × 30 days × 5 contests, scoped to `demo-%` device IDs. **Outside-the-box choices**: KPI cards compare against 2026 hybrid-casual benchmarks (D1≥40%, D7≥20%, D30≥7%); top-scores carry a z-score column and an `⚠ OUTLIER` flag for scores >3σ above the daily mean (statistical anti-cheat MVP); time-of-day heatmap in Asia/Jerusalem TZ; CSV exports include UTF-8 BOM for Excel + Hebrew; admin URL is intentionally hidden (no `/admin` route) so password-spray attacks don't even reach the auth check.
- **Score economy rebalance** — `pointsFor()` switched from linear `tier × 10 × group × chain` to **exponential** `tier × 10 × (1 + (tier-1)*0.3) × group × chain`. Per-merge values: tier 1=20, tier 4=152, tier 5=220, tier 8=496 (~3× higher at the top). Added **first-time-tier-up bonuses** keyed by `TIER_UP_BONUS = {5:500, 6:1500, 7:5000, 8:15000}`, tracked per-game via `tierUpHit = {}` (reset in `init()`). New helper `showMilestoneBanner(tier, points)` renders a gold-on-black celebration card (1.5s) with `soundMilestone()` + buzz. The chain ladder (×1, ×1.5, ×2, ×2.5, ×3) is **untouched** — leaderboards stay valid. Server-side `challengeDropsImplausible()` recalibrated to match new scoring (100K/25, 200K/50, 500K/100, 1.5M/200, 3M/350). **Architectural prep for the App launch** added in the same diff: `getActiveTiers()` wraps the `TIERS` constant (17 callsites migrated) so future skin packs swap palettes via this single getter; `getBoardRows()`/`getBoardCols()` wrap board dimensions (originally `const ROWS=6, COLS=4`) so future "Pro mode" 5/6-column boards swap dimensions via these getters. Both abstractions are pure refactors today — no behavior change.
- **Live contest + spectator mode** — added 5 new endpoints + 2 ephemeral tables. Active player heartbeats `/live-score` at 1Hz; server tells them whether anyone is watching, and only when watched do they POST grid frames to `/live-state`. Spectators poll `/live-state/:targetDeviceId` every 1s and heartbeat `/watch` every 5s. Stale rows filtered at read time by a 10s `updated_at` window. The contest leaderboard sort key is `accumulated + live` so a mid-game player visibly climbs the table in real time. Frontend touchpoints: live push (`pushLiveScore`, `pushLiveState`, `scheduleLiveScorePush`), audience badge (`renderAudienceBadge`), spectator (`openSpectatorPicker`, `startSpectator`, `spectatorTick`, `renderSpectatorView`). "צא לצפייה במשחקים חיים" button appears on the game-over modal only in contest mode. Also fixed: "שחק שוב" in contest game-over now correctly restarts in contest (previously it kicked back to practice). New localStorage key: `bloom_contest_last_final_<code>` — used as the score shown to the player you're watching ("your watcher's last score").

Live URL: https://bloom-web-production-f3bd.up.railway.app
GitHub: https://github.com/shlomixxx/bloom-game (private)
Railway project: `bloom-game` / service `bloom-web` / Postgres `Postgres-z2RQ`.

Home screen links to own profile.

Home screen shows premium gold banner with prize, countdown, player count, and join CTA. Admin shows "שבועי" badge on weekly contests. Config: `weekly_enabled`, `weekly_prize` (500💎), `weekly_name`.

- ✅ **Security hardening — phase 1 (May 2026)** — four critical economy fixes in one commit. (1) `POST /api/player/buy-skin` no longer accepts a client-supplied `price` — costs come from a new server-side `SKIN_PRICES` map (`classic:0, ocean:200, candy:200, space:300, fire:300, gold:500`). The historical bug let anyone buy any skin for 0 by sending `price: 0`. Deduction is now an atomic `UPDATE ... WHERE balance >= cost RETURNING balance`. (2) `POST /api/player/buy-powerup` lost its `refund` branch — that branch credited up to 1000 💎 per call with zero proof of a prior purchase. Cancel UX is now local-only on the client (optimistic balance refund until next sync). (3) `POST /api/duels/:id/score` now accepts `drops` + `token`, runs the same `challengeDropsImplausible` check as `/api/score`, and the settlement step is wrapped in a `BEGIN…COMMIT` transaction with a `status IN ('pending','accepted')` guard against double-settle under concurrent requests. (4) `GET /api/duels/:id` now reads `?deviceId=` and nulls out the opponent's score until the viewer has submitted their own — previously a cheater could peek at the target before playing. (5) `POST /api/challenges/:slug/score` and `/complete` accept a soft `token` field. All four flows in the client (`src/01-constants.js` for skin buy, `src/02-shop.js` for duel score + duel polling, `src/09-challenges.js` for challenge submit) updated to send `token: deviceToken` and to query duel state with `?deviceId=`. Cache buster bumped to `v20260519a`, SW `CACHE_NAME` to `bloom-v3.8`.
- ✅ **Security hardening — phase 2 (May 2026)** — `softDeviceAuth` middleware applied to all 27 state-mutating `POST /api/*` endpoints (everything except `/api/register`, which is what issues the token). Two flavors: `requireDeviceAuth` (hard — 400/401/403 if missing or wrong) for future use, and `softDeviceAuth` (rollout — accepts missing tokens, rejects only present-and-invalid ones). Both read `deviceId`/`token` from the JSON body or from `x-device-id`/`x-device-token` headers, and set `req.deviceId` for downstream handlers. The rollout strategy is to let `softDeviceAuth` ride existing clients without breaking them, then swap to `requireDeviceAuth` once telemetry shows ≥99% of requests carry tokens. Client adds an `apiPost(path, body, opts?)` helper in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) that auto-injects `{ deviceId, token }` so new code lands on the wire with the right shape. Existing fetches are unchanged. Cache buster bumped to `v20260519b`.
- ✅ **Security hardening — phase 3 (May 2026)** — every credit-mutating endpoint now uses an atomic `UPDATE player_profiles SET balance = balance - $1 ... WHERE balance >= $1 RETURNING balance` instead of the older `SELECT balance` → check → `UPDATE` pattern. The old pattern had a TOCTOU race: two concurrent requests could both pass the check against the same stale balance and both succeed at deducting, letting a player double-spend (or end up with a negative balance). Touched: `POST /api/score` (daily jackpot auto-contribution), `POST /api/contests` (host wager), `POST /api/contests/:code/join` (opt-in wager), `POST /api/player/spend`, `POST /api/player/buy-powerup`, `POST /api/player/buy-tile`, `POST /api/duels` (challenger deposit), `POST /api/duels/:id/accept` (opponent deposit). `POST /api/player/buy-skin` was already converted in phase 1. Cache buster bumped to `v20260519c`.
- ✅ **Security hardening — phase 4 (May 2026)** — three perimeter tightening fixes. (1) **CORS allowlist** in [server.js](server.js) is now an exact `Set` match (`https://<host>`, `http://<host>`, plus the canonical Railway URL) instead of the previous `origin.includes(host)` substring check — the old form trusted `https://evil.com.attacker.com` against host `attacker.com`. Direct/curl requests with no `Origin` header still pass. (2) **Contest score caps**: `POST /api/contests/:code/score` now rejects any single-game score over `MAX_SCORE_PER_GAME = 1_500_000` (in addition to the broader 10M sanity check), and enforces a per-device 30-second cool-down between game submissions per contest — the cumulative `contest_scores.score` can no longer be inflated by spamming back-to-back submissions. (3) **Referral hardening**: `POST /api/referral` now rate-limits 3/day/device and refuses any device that doesn't appear in `device_visits` (i.e. hasn't actually loaded the site via `/api/ping`). Doesn't 100%-stop a determined cheater (they can hit ping then refer), but ping itself is 30/hr and the referral itself is 3/day, so the abuse cap is bounded. Cache buster bumped to `v20260519d`.
- ✅ **Privacy compliance — phase 5 (May 2026)** — challenge-winner contact details (`contact_name` / `contact_phone` / `contact_email` on `challenge_entries`) are now auto-purged 90 days after `prize_claimed_at`. Two triggers: (a) a 24-hour `setInterval` in [server.js](server.js) that runs the wipe `UPDATE`; (b) a new admin-only `POST /<ADMIN_PATH>/api/privacy/purge` endpoint for on-demand purges (writes `admin_actions` audit row with the row count). New partial index `idx_challenge_entries_purge` on `challenge_entries (prize_claimed_at) WHERE prize_claimed_at IS NOT NULL` keeps the wipe cheap as the table grows. Added [public/privacy.html](public/privacy.html) — Hebrew RTL privacy policy covering what we collect, why, third-party sharing (none), right-to-erasure, cookies (none), security, and contact email. Served at `/privacy` (clean URL) and linked from the `/welcome` footer + the home-screen footer in [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js). New admin section in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under 🔧 ניטור: a "🧹 הרץ ניקוי PII עכשיו" button that hits the new endpoint and shows the row count. `/privacy` added to the sitemap. Israel Privacy Law + GDPR compliance. Cache buster bumped to `v20260519e`.
- ✅ **Security hardening round 2 — phases 1-7 (May 2026)** — seven-commit security overhaul addressing impersonation, credit-inflation, and operational hygiene gaps left after round 1.
  1. **Hard device-token auth on 20 endpoints**: replaced `softDeviceAuth` (accepts missing tokens) with `requireDeviceAuth` (401 missing_token, 403 bad_token) on every credit/state-mutating route — `/api/score`, `/profile/{country,name}`, `/score/practice`, `/contests`, `/contests/:code/{join,score}`, all 4 `/challenges/:slug/*`, all 5 `/player/*` mutators, `/referral`, all 3 `/duels/*`. Frontend updated to send `token: deviceToken` in every POST body (touched: 02-shop, 06-contests, 07-identity, 08-contest-helpers, 09-challenges, 11-game, 12-tour-info, 13-boot). Closes the duel-theft / score-griefing / profile-takeover vectors that round 1 left open. Heartbeat/live/ping/watch stay soft for now (high-frequency, will migrate after telemetry).
  2. **event_gift hardened**: server cap from `event_gift_credits_max` (was hardcoded 500), 30s rate gate (was 10s), new hourly 20/device cap via `checkRateLimit('gift:hourly', ...)`. New `POST /api/player/gift` endpoint where the SERVER rolls the jackpot dice — `triggerGift()` in [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js) now calls this instead of the legacy `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount})` where client supplied the amount. Closes ~180K credits/hour DevTools loop.
  3. **drops mandatory + stored**: `daily_scores` and `difficulty_scores` get `drops INTEGER` columns (idempotent). `/api/score`, `/score/practice`, `/challenges/:slug/score`, `/challenges/:slug/complete`, `/duels/:id/score` now return `400 missing_drops` if drops is omitted. Old pattern `if (dropsN !== null && implausible)` let cheaters skip the check by omitting drops — now `challengeDropsImplausible` always runs.
  4. **earn dedup locked down**: `dedupKey = action + ':' + today + JSON.stringify(meta)` let `meta:{x:Math.random()}` mint unlimited daily rewards. New logic uses `META_DEDUP_ACTIONS = Set(['score_milestone'])` allowlist + `ALLOWED_MILESTONES` integer-tier allowlist; everything else dedups on `action+date` only. **Bug found during testing + fixed**: `game_config.key VARCHAR(60)` was too short for `_earn:<deviceId>:score_milestone:<date>:<meta>` keys (~75 chars), making the dedup INSERT fail silently inside `.catch(() => {})`. Schema migrated to `VARCHAR(255)` + the catch now logs instead of swallowing.
  5. **Duel single-submission**: `UPDATE duels SET challenger_score = $1 WHERE id = $2 AND challenger_score IS NULL AND status IN ('pending','accepted') RETURNING 1` (mirrored for opponent). Second submission returns `{ok:false, reason:'already_submitted'}`. Closes the "submit low, see I'd lose, submit higher" trick.
  6. **Server-authoritative skin ownership**: new `player_skins (device_id, skin_id, purchased_at)` table + index. `POST /api/player/buy-skin` records ownership in the same transaction as the balance deduction (no orphan debits / skips). Already-owned skin returns `{ok:true, cost:0, alreadyOwned:true}`. New `GET /api/player/skins?deviceId=` for boot sync + `POST /api/player/skins/declare` for one-time legacy migration (existing localStorage owners declare once; rate-limited 3/day; client sets `bloom_skins_grace_done=1`). `migrateOwnedSkinsOnce()` in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) runs `setTimeout(800ms)` after boot. Closes the localStorage-edit-equals-free-skins hole + survives browser clears.
  7. **Ops hardening**: `Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains` + tight `Content-Security-Policy` (script-src allows GA, style-src allows inline, frame-ancestors 'none'). `ERROR_WEBHOOK` env var forwards `unhandledRejection`/`uncaughtException` to a webhook (Discord/Slack/etc) when set. Two new periodic-cleanup intervals: hourly `_earn:*` (>30d) and `_gift_rate:*` (>1d) purge; 5-min `contest_live_state` + `contest_watchers` (>1h) purge. Cache buster `v20260519i`, SW `bloom-v3.9`. Each phase shipped as its own commit + Railway deploy + curl smoke test before moving to the next.
- ✅ **Aurora skin pack (May 2026)** — 7th skin pack, layered atop the existing `SKIN_PACKS` infrastructure but with exclusive CSS-effects. **Visual identity**: gradient backgrounds per tier (e.g. tier-3 = `linear-gradient(140deg,#FFD3E2 0%,#E07AA8 100%)`, tier-8 = 6-stop multi-color shimmer); per-tier `box-shadow` for depth. **Animations**: tier-8 crown has continuous `auroraCrownShimmer` (3s linear) + `auroraCrownPulse` (1.6s breath) + `auroraCrownIcon` (5s tilt); tiers 6-7 breathe with `auroraBreath` (2.2s); danger-mode accelerates breathing to 0.7s. **Merge juice**: `auroraMerge` keyframe replaces vanilla merge with hit-stop (scale 0.85 → 1.4 → 1.0) and `--merge-peak` CSS variable randomized to 1.30-1.50 per merge for slot-machine variance; chain-4+ switches to `auroraMergeBig` (bigger scale, hue-rotate, longer duration). **Drop**: `auroraDrop` keyframe with bouncy overshoot. **Text bursts**: "GREAT!" / "AMAZING!" / "INSANE!" / "GODLIKE!" on chains 2/3/4/5+ via `auroraShowTextBurst(chainCount)` — single reused DOM node `#aurora-text-burst` re-animated by toggling `.show`. **Score particles**: `auroraFlyParticlesToScore(cellEl, count)` spawns gold balls that CSS-transition from cell coords to score counter coords over 600ms (Vampire-Survivors style). **Score bump**: `auroraScoreBump()` adds `.bump` class to score elements for a quick scale 1→1.35→1 animation. **Architecture**: Aurora is gated by `body.skin-aurora-active` class — every selector in [public/css/tiles-aurora.css](public/css/tiles-aurora.css) is scoped under it, so other skins are completely unaffected. Class is toggled by `syncBodySkinClass()` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) which is called from every `activeSkinId` mutation site (boot, purchase, equip, trial start, trial revert). JS helpers (`auroraIsActive`, `auroraShowTextBurst`, `auroraScoreBump`, `auroraFlyParticlesToScore`, `auroraSetMergeVariance`) all check `auroraIsActive()` first → safe to call unconditionally from the engine; non-Aurora skins are no-op paths. **Render integration** in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js): `tier-N` (N=1..8), `chain-N` (when merging), and `--merge-peak` CSS var are set during DOM creation. **Engine hooks** in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `processChains` fire after each `render({ merging })`: text burst on chain≥2, score bump, particles from merged cell. **Bonus events** ([src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js)) also fire `auroraScoreBump` on bomb/freeze/gift-jackpot and `auroraSetMergeVariance` on the star-upgraded cell. **Admin gate**: new `game_config.aurora_skin_enabled` (default `'true'`). Client-side gate in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) (after `/api/config` resolves) deletes `SKIN_PACKS.aurora` when disabled and reverts active skin to classic — `player_skins` ownership rows are never deleted so re-enabling restores it. Admin sees the toggle in the rebuilt config UI (✓ פעיל / ✗ כבוי), with a rich tooltip. Three-layer disable: (1) per-player via shop, (2) global via admin toggle (no redeploy), (3) `git revert` of the 5 commits. **Build**: `public/css/tiles-aurora.css` added to `build.sh` before `dark.css` so dark-mode overrides still win. Cache buster `v20260520c`.
- ✅ **Admin config UX — toggles, preset chips, rich tooltips (May 2026)** — the "כל ההגדרות" table in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) was a flat list of `<input type="text">` boxes — admins had to type `true`/`false` manually and look up sensible numeric values elsewhere. Now every row is rendered through `renderConfigValueCell(key, value)`:
  1. **Boolean keys** (`*_enabled`, `crown_merge_enabled`, `wager_enabled`, `jackpot_enabled`, `tile_shop_enabled`, etc — also auto-detected when value is `'true'`/`'false'`) → 2-button toggle (`✓ פעיל` mint / `✗ כבוי` pink). Click = auto-save via `persistConfigValue()`. Active state has a colored ring.
  2. **Numeric / enum keys with sensible defaults** (~95 keys mapped in new `PRESETS_PER_KEY`) → input box + pill chips below it. Click a chip = auto-save + visual "on" state. Custom values still typeable into the input. Examples: `event_bomb_radius` → [1,2,3] chips; `game_speed_pct` → [50,75,100,125,150,200] chips; `merge_mode` → [anchor, classic, smart] chips; `wager_rake` → [0, 3, 5, 10, 15] chips.
  3. **Free-form keys** (`drop_weights`, `weekly_name`, `adsense_client_id`, `stripe_publishable_key`) → plain input + manual שמור button.
  4. **Rich tooltips with examples** — `TIPS_PER_KEY` was a 100-entry one-liner dict; now every entry has a `<div class="tip-example">` block with concrete values, scenarios ("שחקנים חדשים נושרים? תוריד ל-15-20"), economic math ("100 שחקנים × 5💎 = קופה של 500💎"), and warnings ("⚠️ ערך 2+ + weight גבוה = משחקים קצרים מאוד"). Also **fixed wrong key names** that existed in the old dict but didn't match the schema: `event_freeze_bonus_points` → `event_freeze_points`, `event_star_bonus_points` → `event_star_points`. Added tips for previously undocumented keys: `event_star_upgrade`, `event_freeze_clear_rows`, `events_min_empty_cells`, `jackpot_*`, `duel_*`, `tile_shop_enabled`, `tile_price_2/3/4`, `tile_price_multiplier`, `powerup_*`.
  5. **Wider internal-key filter** — the table now skips ALL keys starting with `_` (was only `_earn:`), hiding `_ad:`, `_ad_count:`, `_ad_rate:`, `_gift_rate:` dedup rows.
  New CSS: `.cfg-cell`, `.cfg-toggle-row`, `.cfg-toggle-btn` (with `on-true`/`on-false` states), `.cfg-preset-row`, `.cfg-preset-btn` (with `on` state), including dark-mode overrides. Helper `persistConfigValue(host, key, val)` is the single source of truth for PATCH /config + toast + active-state refresh; toggle, chip, and manual שמור all funnel through it. Cache buster bumped to `v20260520b`.
- ✅ **Smart merge mode (May 2026)** — `game_config.merge_mode` now accepts a third value `'smart'` in addition to `'anchor'` (default — bottommost row, tie → closest to drop column) and `'classic'` (bottommost row, tie → leftmost). `smart` invokes `pickSmartSurvivor(group, anchorCol, newTier)` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) which clones the grid, simulates placing the merged tile at each candidate survivor cell, runs gravity on the clone, locates where the merged tile lands (sentinel approach), then scores: `sameAdj * 1,000,000 + upAdj * 1,000 + landRow * 100 + surviveRow * 10 - |landCol - anchorCol|`. Same-tier neighbor post-gravity = immediate chain (highest priority); next-up-tier neighbor = ladder setup. Falls back to anchor logic if simulation returns no candidate. Admin toggle in 🎮 משחק → "הגדרות משחק" cycles `anchor` (🎯 mint) → `classic` (⬅ pink) → `smart` (🧠 gold). Engine cost: O(group_size × rows × cols) per merge — group is usually 2-4 so negligible. The 'crown explosion' branch is unaffected (handled before survivor pick). Cache buster bumped to `v20260520a`.
- ✅ **Ad-watch per-game dedup (May 2026)** — user-reported exploit: finishing a game and refreshing brought back the "watch ad for 30💎" button on the game-over screen, and the player could harvest credits ~200💎/hour by F5-spamming. Root cause: the watch-ad button paid via `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount: 30})` (which goes through `/api/player/earn`, gets clamped to `event_gift_credits_max` and gated by a 30s `_gift_rate`), but there was **no concept of "this game already claimed its ad"** — every refresh re-rendered the same offer, and the in-memory `lastAdWatchTime` was wiped on each page load. Fix has three layers:
  1. **New endpoint `POST /api/player/ad-watch`** with `requireDeviceAuth`. Body: `{deviceId, token, gameId}`. Server checks (a) per-game dedup: `_ad:<deviceId>:<gameId>` key in `game_config` — second claim returns `{ok:false, reason:'already_claimed'}`; (b) per-day cap: `_ad_count:<deviceId>:<YYYY-MM-DD>` counter vs new `ad_daily_cap` config (default 5) — when reached returns `daily_cap`; (c) 30s cooldown via separate `_ad_rate:<deviceId>` key (independent of event_gift gate so they don't interfere). On success: atomic UPSERT of all three keys + `UPDATE player_profiles SET balance = balance + ad_watch_reward`. Returns `{ok, reward, newBalance, dailyRemaining, dailyCap}`.
  2. **Client gameId helper** in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js): `getCurrentGameId()` reads/creates in `sessionStorage[bloom_active_game_id]` (survives F5 in same tab, regenerated on `init({fresh: true})`), plus `adClaimedForCurrentGame()` / `markAdClaimedForCurrentGame()` via `sessionStorage[bloom_ad_claimed_<gameId>]`.
  3. **Client watch-ad button** in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `render({over: true})`: if `adClaimedForCurrentGame()` returns true the button is replaced with `"✓ קיבלת 30💎 על המשחק הזה"` text. The click handler now posts to `/api/player/ad-watch` with the gameId and handles `already_claimed` / `daily_cap` / `rate_limited` responses with proper button states (disabled with informative text, or temporary disable + re-enable for the cooldown case). The legacy `earnCredits('event_gift', ...)` path is no longer used by the watch-ad button.
  Math: before — F5-spam farmed ~200💎/hour with no real ceiling; after — capped at `ad_daily_cap × ad_watch_reward` = 150💎/day from ads. Real AdSense SDK integration is the long-term answer (then `ad_daily_cap` can rise because each watch is paid for); this is the right gate until impressions are actually tracked. Cache buster `v20260519j`. NOTE: the separate `continue-ad` button (clear top 2 rows for a "second chance") still uses `simulateAdWatch` without server dedup — that's a different surface (gameplay, not credits) and may need a similar `usedContinue` per-gameId fix if abuse surfaces.
- 🔙 **Home v3 rolled back (May 2026)** — built an opt-in v3 home (star mascot, tile-ladder legend, week-over-week stats, "what's new" banner, animated background mesh, pre-game tier-up teaser, full a11y) targeting the 9.4/10 score we left on the table in v2's self-audit. After live testing the user said "לא אהבתי את הגירסה הזאת" so we rolled it back instead of pushing forward. v2 is once again the canonical home for everyone. The v3 source files ([src/05b-home-v3.js](src/05b-home-v3.js) + [public/css/home-v3.css](public/css/home-v3.css)) are kept in the repo as a reference for the audit-prescribed shape; they're concatenated into the bundle (so the IIFE-internal function declarations stay accessible if we ever need them) but no code path reaches `showHomeV3()` anymore. The delegation chain in [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js) `showHome()` dropped the v3 branch entirely; the "✨ נסה את הגירסה החדשה" link at the bottom of v2 was removed; and a one-shot `localStorage.removeItem('bloom_home_v3')` runs on every load so anyone who opted in is migrated back to v2 transparently. Cache buster `v20260520s`.
- ✅ **Home v2 → default (May 2026)** — after a short opt-in period via the "✨ נסה את הגירסה החדשה" toggle, the v2 home (see HOME_AUDIT.md task plan + the v2 commit) is now the canonical home for everyone. The delegation in [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js) `showHome()` flipped: previously `if homeV2Enabled() { return showHomeV2() }` based on opt-in flag `bloom_home_v2`; now `homeV2Enabled()` returns true by default and only returns false if `localStorage[bloom_home_v1_force]` is set (toggled by `?home=v1` or the "↩ הגירסה הישנה" button at the bottom of v2). v1 still ships in the same bundle — anyone who lands there explicitly sees a "↩ חזור לגירסה החדשה (מומלץ)" link instead of the old "✨ נסה" CTA. Existing players who had `bloom_home_v2` set keep v2; existing players without it also get v2 now (the very small "opted-into-v1" cohort is acceptable churn for a feature that was only opt-in for hours). Cache buster `v20260520n`, SW `bloom-v4.1`.
- ✅ **UX audit §1.7 — Slot-machine reel on daily-login reward (May 2026)** — variable-reward juice on top of the existing deterministic payout. `showDailyLoginReward` in [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js) now renders `+??? 💎` initially and runs a 22-tick reel (50→180ms cadence, decelerating past tick #14, sampling from `[reward*0.4, reward*2.2]` so the reel can't visually contradict the outcome). Landing fires `soundMilestone` at a streak-scaled tier + a short `buzz([10,30,10])` + the `drRewardLand` overshoot keyframe (0.92→1.18→0.97→1). CSS in [public/css/viral.css](public/css/viral.css): `.dr-reward` gets stable `min-width:160px` + `tabular-nums` so digits don't jitter; `.dr-reward-spinning` (blur + scale-down + opacity) and `.dr-reward-landed` (bounce + resume existing glow loop with a 550ms delay) wrap the two states. Zero economy change — the math is identical, just the experience. Cache buster `v20260520j`.
- ✅ **UX audit Phase 4 + showToast (May 2026)** — four retention-focused additions shipped together: §1.4 social proof, §1.5 streak FOMO, §1.6 practice funnel, plus the §3.4 toast helper. **§1.4 social proof** (server.js + [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js)): new `GET /api/stats/live` returns `activeNow` (distinct device_id in `contest_live_state` updated within 30s), `playingNow` (distinct device_id in `device_visits` with `last_at` within 3 min), and `gamesToday` (`daily_scores` rows for today in Asia/Jerusalem). Home now sports a `.home-live-pulse` bar with a blinking green dot and "N שחקנים פעילים · M משחקים היום" — hidden until first response so a cold-start ghost doesn't flash; 15s refresh interval torn down by `hideHome()`. **§1.5 streak FOMO** (sharpened) ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css)): the existing single-line streak hint in game-over now branches into four tones by streak length — cold (none) / low (1-2) / mid (≥3, soft border pulse) / hot (≥7, pulsing gradient card with a slight scale-up + glow). **§1.6 practice funnel** — the daily countdown screen used to dead-end when the player had already finished today's run; new `.over-funnel` block (only renders when `mode === 'daily' && opts.alreadyPlayed`) shows three CTAs ("שחק פרקטיס" primary gradient + "תחרות חברים" + "אתגרי BLOOM"), wired into the existing `init('practice')` / `showContestMenu()` / `showChallengesList('game-over-funnel')` entry points. **§3.4 showToast** ([src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)): new thin wrapper over `showTransientBanner` with info / success / error / warning palettes, de-duped via per-type banner tag so rapid successive calls collapse cleanly. Exposed as `window.__bloomToast`. Existing fetch sites are **NOT** mass-retrofitted to use it — the audit explicitly framed this as additive infrastructure; retrofitting confirmations across the whole app would be its own multi-file PR. Cache buster `v20260520i`.
- ✅ **UX audit Phase 3 — First-Time User Experience (May 2026)** — the audit's #1 retention lever: brand-new players who don't grok merge mechanics in their first 30 seconds leave before finishing a board. New [src/15-ftue.js](src/15-ftue.js) (inside the IIFE — auto-picked up by `build.sh`'s `[0-9]*.js` glob between 14-events.js and 99-close.js) opens a fullscreen `.ftue-overlay` (z-index 10000) for any device whose `localStorage[bloom_ftue_done]` is unset AND `loadGamesPlayed() === 0`. Three choreographed steps run in <30s on a 4×6 mock board that uses the real `getActiveTiers()` art so muscle memory transfers cleanly: (1) **Drop** — empty grid, arrow on a hinted column, single tap → tile drops + lands + soundDrop + light buzz; (2) **Merge** — two tier-1s pre-stacked, third tier-1 drops on top, three-stack merges to tier-2 with `soundMerge(2)`, longer buzz, big "WOW!" card; (3) **Chain** — tier-1×2 in column 1 plus a tier-2 in column 2, drop triggers primary merge + adjacent chain to tier-3 with `soundChain(2)`, confetti, "שרשרת ×2" banner. Step dots show progress (active = wide pill, done = soft gold); "דלג על המדריך" is always reachable. The flag is written on either completion or skip so the FTUE never re-fires. Boot wiring in [src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js): the existing first-time branch now calls `startFTUE(function() { showHome(); })` instead of `showHome()` directly when `ftueShouldRun()` is true and there's no game history. URL-param contexts (`?bot=1`, `?botui`, `?watch=…`) are explicitly excluded by `ftueShouldRun()` so QA and spectator-share routes are untouched. **Architectural choice**: this is a *demo* tutorial — every drop/merge/chain is a scripted animation sequence, not engine output. Decoupling from the real BFS+gravity pipeline was deliberate; real-engine seeding would have demanded surgery on `init()` / `grid` / `nextPiece` for a surface that fires once per device. CSS landed in [public/css/viral.css](public/css/viral.css) (built on the §2.2 design tokens — light/dark themes work without extra overrides). Analytics: `tutorial_step` / `tutorial_complete` / `tutorial_skip` events ride the existing trackEvent() pipeline. Cache buster `v20260520h`.
- ✅ **UX audit Phase 2 — Shell + NavStack infrastructure (May 2026)** — addresses the audit's biggest "feels like different apps" complaint: every non-game screen used to redraw its own header. This commit lays the unified-shell foundation and adopts it in one screen as proof of pattern, with the rest of the rollout intentionally deferred. New in [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js): `NavStack` (push/back/replace/current/depth/reset on descriptors of shape `{ id, title, enter, exit }` — empty-stack pop routes home via `showHome`, exposed as `window.__bloomNav` for delegated handlers) and `mountShell({target, title, subtitle, onBack, actions})` (renders a sticky 56px-tall header — back arrow [←], centered title with optional subtitle, up to 3 right-side action buttons; backed by `NavStack.back()` unless explicit onBack is supplied; pass `onBack:null` to render without a back button). New CSS in [public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css): `.shell` + `.shell-back` + `.shell-title` + `.shell-subtitle` + `.shell-actions` — sticky-to-container (not viewport, so each screen keeps its own scroll context), backdrop-filter blur + saturate for the frosted effect, uses the §2.2 design tokens throughout so light/dark themes work without separate overrides. **Proof of pattern**: [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `showContestLeaderboard` drops its old `createBackButton` + `<div class="contest-title">` pair from the innerHTML; `mountShell()` injects both inside the same container right after content lands. Back uses the existing back-target logic (home vs contest-menu depending on member count) so navigation behavior is unchanged — only the visual shell switches over. **Explicit non-scope**: the in-game `.top` header (score/best/streak/balance) is NOT migrating to mountShell — it's not a "back + title" pattern, it's the live game HUD, and changing it would break a lot of layout. Other contest screens (`showContestMenu`/`showCreateContestForm`/`showJoinContestForm`/`showContestPreview`/`showMyContestsList`) + challenge screens (`showChallengesList`/`showChallengeDetail`/`showChallengePreEnter`/`showChallengeClaim`) still use the legacy `createBackButton` and are pending. Cache buster `v20260520g`.
- ✅ **UX audit Phase 1 — Quick Wins (May 2026)** — three retention-focused tweaks driven by a UX audit doc (BLOOM_UX_AUDIT.md, not in the repo, lives in the user's Downloads). Shipped as three independent commits:
  1. **§1.3 — Emotional game-over** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `render({over:true})` + [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/score` + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css)). The pill that used to say bare "#23" now reads "🏆 מקום #23 מתוך 847" — `total` is a new field on the `/api/score` response, mirrored from the count query that `/api/leaderboard/:date` already ran. New `bestDeltaHtml` block: when `isNewBest`, prints "🎉 שיא אישי חדש! +<delta>" (delta calculated from `prevBest` captured at `init()` before `best` gets overwritten by the post-game save); when the score is ≥90% of best but didn't beat it, "😱 קרוב לשיא! החמצת ב-<miss> בלבד". New `rankTierHtml` block: walks `[3,10,20,50,100]`, finds the smallest tier above the player's rank, emits "⬆️ עוד <gap> נקודות והיית ב-TOP N" — reads from the in-memory top-50 leaderboard, no extra round trip. Primary "שחק שוב" CTA visual overhaul: 360px wide, gradient fill, breathing gold ring animation (`ctaGlow` keyframe) so it unambiguously dominates the share / ad / leaderboard secondaries that used to compete for attention.
  2. **§1.2-mod — Drop pre-leaderboard name prompt** ([src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) + [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)). The audit framed §1.2 as "name + country picker before the player sees the board", but the prompts actually fire at the leaderboard-submit moment immediately after first daily/practice — same drop-off in spirit (asking for commitment the moment the player is processing a result). Fix: new `defaultPlayerName(deviceId)` returns "שחקן XXXX" using the last 4 alphanumeric chars of the deviceId — cheap, stable, never persisted to localStorage (so `hasRealPlayerName()` can still distinguish "default placeholder" from "real name"). The four `if (!playerName) promptForName(...)` call sites are now unconditional submits with the default name. `promptForName`'s skip handler no longer falls back to "אנונימי" (default name is always there). New game-over CTA "✏️ קבע שם אמיתי בלוח" renders only when `hasRealPlayerName()` is false AND the player just landed on the leaderboard, then opens promptForName in edit-mode + re-submits + re-renders so the rank updates inline without a page reload.
  3. **§2.2 — Design tokens** ([public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css) + freshly-added [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) rules). New `:root` block defining `--color-accent` / `--color-accent-soft` / `--color-accent-ink` / `--color-accent-glow`, `--color-bg` / `--color-surface` / `--color-surface-2` / `--color-border`, `--color-text` / `--color-text-muted` / `--color-text-faint`, `--color-success` / `--color-danger` / `--color-warning`, `--radius-sm/md/lg`, `--shadow-sm/md/glow`. Dark theme overrides live under `html[data-theme="dark"]`, matching the existing theme switcher. **Important deviation from the audit's text**: the audit suggested a fresh RGB palette (#FF6B9D / #6BCB77 / #FFD93D / dark bg #1e2327) — that's off-brand vs the warm neutrals + gold + mint green that BLOOM actually ships, so the tokens carry the audit's *vocabulary* but the *values* came from the established palette. **Also deviated**: the audit asked for a bulk migration of every hard-coded color across screens/home/viral/dark — 100+ occurrences, real visual-regression risk if batched. Instead this commit migrates only the freshly-added §1.3 / 1.2-mod rules as proof-of-pattern; remaining surfaces will adopt the tokens incrementally as we touch them.
  Cache buster bumps: `v20260520d` → `v20260520e` → `v20260520f`.
- ⚠️ **Postgres incident + backup hardening (2026-05-13 → 2026-05-20)** — on 2026-05-13 around 14:00 UTC the Railway Postgres-z2RQ volume was reset/reinitialized as part of a Railway-side incident. All pre-13/05 data, including every player's original BLOOM-XXXX code, was lost — the oldest surviving row across the schema is `daily_scores` from 2026-05-13 14:33 UTC (33 min after the crash). bloom-web was always correctly pointed at z2RQ (`DATABASE_URL → postgres-z2rq.railway.internal`), so the issue was data loss inside the DB, not a misrouted DATABASE_URL as initially hypothesised. The two stray sibling services in the project — `Postgres` (🔴 crashed, `PG_VERSION=missing`) and `Postgres-mQVd` (🟢 online but with 0 tables) — both turned out to contain no recoverable BLOOM data either. Railway's GraphQL API (`volumeInstanceBackupList`) confirmed there were no Railway-side snapshots to restore from. Closing actions taken on 2026-05-20: (a) two automated backup schedules now exist on the z2RQ volume instance — `DAILY` at 03:35 UTC (retention 6 days) and `WEEKLY` at 04:30 UTC Saturday (retention 27 days) — created via `mutation volumeInstanceBackupScheduleUpdate(kinds: [DAILY, WEEKLY])`; (b) an immediate manual baseline snapshot named `manual-baseline-20260520` was triggered via `volumeInstanceBackupCreate` so the user has at least one Railway-side restore point regardless of when the first scheduled run lands; (c) the local `pg_dump` text + custom-format dumps from the diagnostic session are kept under `railway-backups-YYYYMMDD-HHMM/` and `.gitignore` already excludes that path via `railway-backups-*/`. The two orphan Postgres services were NOT deleted in this session — they remain in the project pending a 24h-stability decision. Future automation idea: a server-side weekly `pg_dump` cron that uploads to S3/Drive, fully decoupled from Railway, so a parallel incident can't take out both the live DB and its backups simultaneously.

## 13. Known issues / debt

- **Fixed bug (state-bleed across contests)**: when switching contests via "↕ החלפת תחרות", `activeContestCode` changed before the in-memory `grid`/`score` were reset. Any `saveContestGameState()` call between that switch and `init('contest')` for the new contest wrote the previous contest's grid into the new contest's `bloom_contest_state_<code>` slot. Fix: track `activeGameContestCode` separately — `saveContestGameState()` writes to the contest the in-memory game *belongs to*, not whichever `activeContestCode` currently is. `activeGameContestCode` is set inside `init('contest')` after load and cleared on game-over and on entering non-contest modes.
- **Fixed bug (silent dedup failure)**: `game_config.key` was `VARCHAR(60)`; `_earn:<deviceId>:score_milestone:<date>:<meta>` dedup keys could exceed 60 chars and the INSERT silently failed under a `.catch(() => {})` swallow. Next call looked like a first call and the reward was paid twice. Fix: column widened to `VARCHAR(255)`; the catch now logs instead of swallowing. Caught during phase 4 of round-2 security hardening curl tests.
- `ROADMAP_1.md` is stale (describes home screen + tutorial + MP3 music as shipped — they were rolled back).
- One-per-day gating is client-only (`localStorage`). A determined player can wipe storage and re-submit; the "score must improve" upsert guard limits abuse but doesn't prevent it.
- ~~`deviceId` is spoofable — no HMAC on score submission yet.~~ **Resolved (May 2026)**: every state-mutating endpoint now requires an HMAC token via `requireDeviceAuth`. Heartbeat/ping/live-score/watch remain `softDeviceAuth` pending client-adoption telemetry.
- Rate limiting exists per-endpoint via `checkRateLimit` but is in-memory (resets on server restart). For a single-replica deploy this is acceptable; horizontal scaling would need Redis.
- `WEIGHTS = [0, 55, 28, 12, 5]` means only tiers 1–4 ever spawn naturally. Higher tiers exist only via merging. This is intentional but worth keeping in mind if rebalancing.
- `pg` `ssl: { rejectUnauthorized: false }` is the default — fine for Railway's managed Postgres, would need rethinking for a different host.
- No tests. There is no test framework configured. If introducing tests, ask first about which framework — the user values "no build step" and tests typically violate that.
- **Backup coverage is Railway-side only (since 2026-05-20)** — DAILY + WEEKLY volume snapshots on z2RQ via Railway's native backup schedules. If Railway suffers another volume-reset incident like the one on 2026-05-13, those snapshots could in theory be reset too. The defence-in-depth move would be an off-Railway `pg_dump` cron uploading to S3/Drive. Not implemented yet.
- **Two orphan Postgres services left in the project**: `Postgres` (crashed, `PG_VERSION=missing` on its volume) and `Postgres-mQVd` (online but empty). Neither is referenced by bloom-web and both are safe to delete, but they're kept for now in case the user wants to inspect them. Each carries a small monthly volume cost (~$5/mo per attached 1GB volume on Railway's pricing).

---

## 14. Local dev

```bash
npm install
export DATABASE_URL="postgres://..."
export PGSSL="false"     # only if your local Postgres has no SSL
npm start                # http://localhost:3000
```

For pure-frontend work, opening `public/index.html` directly in a browser works — only the leaderboard fetches will fail.

For DB inspection from a laptop, use `DATABASE_PUBLIC_URL` from the Railway Postgres variables panel (the internal `DATABASE_URL` only resolves inside Railway).

---

## 15. Deploy

```bash
railway up --service bloom-web --detach --ci
```

`schema.sql` is re-applied on every boot via `initDb()`, so deploys are idempotent. The Railway CLI is logged in as `shlomibusiness@gmail.com`.

Do not deploy without the user's go-ahead — production is live and shared with playtesters.

---

## <a id="living-docs-rule"></a>16. Living-docs rule (very important)

**Whenever the project changes — feature added, file added/renamed/removed, API changed, dep changed, architectural decision made, or roadmap status changed — update BOTH `README.md` and `CLAUDE.md` in the same change.** Don't wait to be asked.

Why: the user wants every future session to start fully primed from these two docs, so we don't burn time/credits/context re-summarizing the project. If either doc drifts from the code, the contract breaks and the next session pays for it.

How to apply:
- Treat doc updates as part of the diff, not a follow-up.
- For small bug fixes that don't shift surface area, a single line in §11 (Current progress) or §13 (Known issues) is enough.
- For feature work or API/schema changes, also reconcile §3, §4, §5, §7, §10, and §12 as needed.
- If `ROADMAP_1.md` ever needs to come back into sync, update it too — but until then, leave the "stale" warning in §6 in place.
